    j       j    w iii   
             
 suttantapiṭake  khuddakanikāye 
 jātakapāḷi  tatiyo bhāgo  
 namo tassa bhagavato arahato sammā sambuddhassa  
 mahānipāto 
    mugapakkhajātakaṃ 
            
       mā paṇḍitiyaṃ  vibhāvaya bālamato bhava sabbapāṇinaṃ  
 sabbo jano  taṃ ocināyatu evaṃ tava attho bhavissati  
  
       karomi te taṃ vacanaṃ yaṃ maṃ bhaṇasi devate  
 atthakāmāsi me amma hitakāmāsi devate  
  
             
       kinnusantaramānova kāsuṃ khaṇasi sārathi  
 puṭṭho me samma akkhāhi kiṃ kāsuyā karissasi  
  
       rañño mugo ca pakkho ca putto jāto acetaso  
 sombhi raññā samajjhiṭṭho  puttaṃ me nikhaṇaṃ  vane  
  
       na khadhiro na mugosmi na pakkho napi paṅgulo   
 adhammaṃ sārathi kayirā mañce tvaṃ nikhaṇaṃ vane  
  
             
       ūrū bāhu ca me passa bhāsitañca suṇohi me  
 adhammaṃ sārathi kayirā mañce tvaṃ nikhaṇaṃ vane  
  
       devatānusi gandhabbo ādu  sakko purindado  
 ko vā tvaṃ kassa vā putto kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ  
  
       nambhi devo na gandhabbo napi  sakko purindado  
 kāsirañño ahaṃ putto yaṃ kāsuyā nighaññasi  
  
    paṇḍiccayaṃ  machasaṃ  syā vi    tañajato  machasaṃ  syā 
    samajjhattho  machasaṃ  syā    nikkhaṇaṃ  machasaṃ  syā 
    vikalo  syā piṅgalo  machasaṃ    adu  machasaṃ    nāpi nambhi  machasaṃ  syā 
  
             
       tassa rañño ahaṃ putto yaṃ tvaṃ samupajivasi    
 adhammaṃ sārathi kayirā maṃ ve tvaṃ nikhaṇaṃ vane  
  
       yassa rukkhassa chāyāya nisideyya sayeyya vā  
 na tassa sākhaṃ bhañejayya mittadubho  hi pāpako  
  
       yathā rukkho rājā yathā sākhā tathā ahaṃ  
 yathā chāyupago poso evaṃ tvamasi sārathi 
 adhammaṃ sārathi kayirā maṃ ve tvaṃ nikhaṇaṃ  vane  
  
             
       pahutabhakkho  bhavanti vippavuttho  sakāgharā    
 bahu naṃ upajivanti yo mittānaṃ na dubhati  
  
       yaṃ yaṃ janapadaṃ yāti nigame rājadhāniyo    
 sabbattha pujito hoti yo mitatānaṃ na dubhati  
  
       nāssa corā pasahanti nātimaññeti  khattiyo  
 sabbe amitte tarati yo mittānaṃ na dubhati  
  
       akkuddho   sagharaṃ eti sabhāya   paṭinandito  
 ñātinaṃ uttamo hoti yo mitatānaṃ na dubhati  
  
       sakkatvā sakkato hoti garu hoti sagāravo     
 vaṇṇakittibhato hoti yo mitatānaṃ na dubhati  
  
       pujako labhate pujaṃ vandako paṭivandataṃ  
 yaso kittiñca pappoti yo mitatānaṃ na dubhati  
  
       aggi yathā pajjalati devatāva virocati  
 siriyā ajahito hoti yo mitatānaṃ na dubhati  
  
    sammupajivasi  machasaṃ    mitatadubbho  machasaṃ  vi    nikkhaṇaṃ  machasaṃ 
    bahutta  machasaṃ    vipapamutto     sakaṅgharā  machasaṃ  sya    na dubbhati  machasaṃ    rājaṭṭhāniyo  machasaṃ    nātimaññati  machasaṃ 
     akuḍo  machasaṃ     sahāyaṃ  machasaṃ     garuko hoti gāravo  machasaṃ 
  
             
       gāvo tassa pajāyanti khette vuttaṃ virūhati  
 vuttānaṃ phalamasanāti  yo mitatānaṃ na dubhati  
  
       darito pabbatāno  vā rukkhāto  patito naro  
 cuto patiṭṭhaṃ labhati yo mitatānaṃ na dubhati  
  
       virūḷhamulasantānaṃ nigrodhamiva māluto  
 amittā nappasahanti yo mitatānaṃ na dubhati  
  
             
       ehi taṃ paṭinessāmi rājaputta sakaṃ gharaṃ  
 rajjaṃ kārehi bhaddante kiṃ araññe karissasi  
  
       alaṃ me tena rajjena ñātakehi  dhanena vā  
 yaṃ me adhammacariyāya rajjaṃ labbhetha  sārathi  
  
       puṇṇapattaṃ palabbhehi  rājaputta ito gato  
 pitā mātā ca me dajjuṃ rājaputta tayī gate  
  
       orodhā ca kumārā ca vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇā  
 tepi attamanā dajjuṃ rājaputta tayī gate 
  
       hatthārūhā  aṇikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārakā  
 tepi dajjuṃ patitā me rājaputta tayī gate 
  
       bahu  jānapadā caññe negamā ca samāgatā  upāyanāni me dajjuṃ rājaputta tayī gate 
  
             
       pitumātu cahaṃ catto raṭṭhassa nigamassa ca  
 atho sakyakumārānaṃ natthi mayhaṃ sakaṃ gharaṃ  
  
       anuññāto ahaṃ matyā sañcatto pitarā ahaṃ  
 eko araññe pabbajito na kāme abhipatthaye  
  
       api ataramānānaṃ phalāsāva samijjhati  
 vipakkabrahmacariyosmi evaṃ jānāhi sārathi  
  
    vutatāna phala  machasaṃ    pabbato  machasaṃ    rukkhato  machasaṃ 
    ñātakena  machasaṃ  syā    labhetha  machasaṃ    maṃ palābhehi  syā  maṃ lābhehi    rohā  machasaṃ  vi    bahuttadhaññā  machasaṃ  syā 
  
             
       api ataramānānaṃ sammadatthā vipaccati  
 vipakkabrahmacariyosmi nikkhanto akutobhayo  
  
       evaṃ vaggukatho  santo vissaṭṭhaccano casi    kasmā pitucca mātucca santike na bhaṇi tadā  
  
       nāhaṃ asanthitā  pakkho na badhiro asotatā  
 nāhaṃ ajivhatā  mugo mā maṃ mugamadhārayi  
  
       purimaṃ sarāmahaṃ jātiṃ yattha rajjamakārayiṃ  
 kārayitvā tahiṃ rajjaṃ pāpatthaṃ nirayaṃ bhusaṃ  
  
       visatiñceva vassāni tahiṃ rajjamakārayiṃ  
 asitivassasahassāni nirayamhi apaccisaṃ  
  
             
       tassa rajjassahaṃ bhīto mā maṃ rajjābhisecayuṃ  
 tasmā pitucca  mātucca santike na bhaṇiṃ tadā  
  
       ucchaṅge maṃ nisīdetvā pitā atthānusāsati  
 ekaṃ hanatha bandhatha ekaṃ khārāpatacchikaṃ  
 ekaṃ sulasmiṃ appetha  iccassamanusāsati  
  
       tassāhaṃ   pharusaṃ sutvā vācāyo samudiritā  
 amugo mugavaṇṇena apakkho   pakkhasammato 
 sake muttakarisasmiṃ acchāhaṃ samparipaluto  
  
       kasirañca parittañca tañca dukkhena saṃyutaṃ  
 ko taṃ jīvitamāgamma veraṃ kayirātha kenaci  
  
       paññāya ca alābhena dhammassa ca adassanā  
 ko taṃ jīvitamāgamma veraṃ kayirātha kenaci  
  
       api ataramānānaṃ phalāsāva samijjhati  
 vipakkabrahmacariyosmi evaṃ jānāhi sārathi  
  
    vaggukato  machasaṃ    vacanova so  machasaṃ syā    tasmā  vi 
    asandhitā  machasaṃ  syā    asandhitā  machasaṃ  syā    apaccasaṃ  syā apaccayiṃ  vi    pituva mātuva  machasaṃ  syā    kharā  machasaṃ  syā 
    uppetha  machasaṃ uppetha  syā     tāsāhaṃ  machasaṃ tyāhaṃ  syā accetha  vi     apakkhe  machasaṃ 
  
              
       api ataramānānaṃ sammadattho vipaccati  
 vipakkabrahmacariyosmi nikkhanto akutobhayo  
  
             
       ahmapi pabbajissāmi rājaputta tavantike  
 avhayassu maṃ bhaddaneta pabbajjā mama ruccati  
  
       rathaṃ niyyādayitvāna anaṇo ehi sārathi  
 anaṇassa hi pabbajjā etaṃ isihi vaṇṇitaṃ 
  
       yadeva tyāhaṃ vacanaṃ akaraṃ bhaddamatthu te  
 tadeva me tvaṃ vacanaṃ yācito kattumarahasi  
  
       idheva tāva acchassu yāva rājānamānaye  
 appeva te pitā disvā pitato sumano siyā  
  
             
       karomi te taṃ vacanaṃ yaṃ maṃ bhaṇasi sārathi  
 ahmapi daṭṭhukāmosmi pitaraṃ me idhāgataṃ  
  
       ehi samma nivattassu kusalaṃ vajjāsi ñātinaṃ  
 mātaraṃ pitaraṃ mayhaṃ vutto vajjāsi vandanaṃ  
  
       tassa pāde gahetvāna katvā ca naṃ padakkhiṇaṃ  
 sārathi rathamāruyha rājadvāraṃ upāgami  
  
       suññaṃ mātā rathaṃ disvā ekaṃ sārathimāgataṃ  
 assupuṇṇehi nettehi rodanti naṃ udikkhati  
  
       aya so sārathi eti nihanatvāna mamatujaṃ  
 nihato nūna me putto pathavyā bhumivaddhano  
  
       amittā nūna nandanti patitā nūna verino  
 āgataṃ sārathiṃ disvā nihanatvāna mamatujaṃ  
       suññaṃ mātā rathaṃ disvā ekaṃ sārathimāgataṃ  
 assupuṇṇehi nettehi rodanti paripucchati   
  
    nihanatvā mama atrajaṃ  machasaṃ    rodanti naṃ paripucchi  machasaṃ 
  
              
       kinnu mugo kinnu pakkho kinnu so vilapi tadā  
 nihaññamāno bhumiyā taṃ me akkhāhi sārathi  
  
       kathaṃ hatthehi pādehi mugo pakkho vivajjayi  
 nihaññamāno bhumiyā taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito  
  
             
       akkhissaṃ te  ahaṃ ayye dajjāsi abhayaṃ mama  
 yaṃ me sutaṃ vā diṭṭhaṃ vā rājaputtassa santike  
  
       abhayaṃ samma te dammi abhito bhaṇa sārathi  
 yaṃ te sutaṃ vā diṭṭhaṃ vā rājaputtassa santike  
  
       na so mugo na so pakko vissaṭṭha vacanova so 
 rajjassa kira so bhito akari  ālaye bahu  
  
       purimaṃ sarati so jātiṃ yattha rajjamakārayi  
 kārayitvā tahiṃ rajjaṃ pāpattha nirayaṃ bhusaṃ  
  
       visatiñce ca vassāni tahiṃ rajjamakārayi  
 asiti vassa sahassāni nirayamhi apacci so  
  
       tassa rājassa so bhīto mā maṃ rajjābhisecayuṃ    
 tasmā pitucca mātucca  santike na bhaṇi  tadā  
  
       aṅgapaccaṅga sampanno ārohapariṇābhavā  
 vissaṭṭhava vano pañño magge saggassa tiṭṭhati  
  
       sace tvaṃ daṭṭhukāmāsi  rājaputti  tavatrajaṃ  
 ehi taṃ pāpayissāmi yattha sammati temiyo 
  
             
       yojayantu rathe asse kacchaṃ nāgāna   bandhatha  
 udirayantu saṅkhapaṇavā vadantu   ekapokkharā  
  
       nadantu bheri sannaddhā vagguṃ vadatu dundubhī  
 negamā ca maṃ anventu gacchaṃ puttanivedako   
  
    akkheyyante  machasaṃ  syā    visaṭṭha  machasaṃ 
    akarā  machasaṃ  syā    apaccisa  machasaṃ 
    rajjebhisecayuṃ  machasaṃ    pituca mātuva 
    nabhaṇe  machasaṃ    kāmosi  machasaṃ 
    rājaputtaṃ  machasaṃ  syā     nāgāni  machasaṃ  syā 
     vagguvādantu  machasaṃ     nivādako  machasaṃ 
  
              
       orodhā ca kumārā ca vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇā  
 khippaṃ yānāni yojentu gacchaṃ puttanivedako  
  
       hatthārohā aṇikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārākā  
 khippaṃ yānāni yojentu gacchaṃ puttanivedako  
  
       samāgatā jānapadā negamā ca samāgatā  
 khippaṃ yānāni yojentu gacchaṃ puttanivedako  
  
             
       asse ca sārathi yutte sindhave sīghavāhane  
 rājadvāraṃ upāgañachuṃ yuttā deva ime bhayā  
  
       thulā javena bhāyanti kisā bhāyanti thāmunā    
 kise thule vivajjetvā saṃsaṭṭhā yojitā bhayā  
  
       tato rājā taramāno yuttamāruyha sandanaṃ  
 itthāgāraṃ ajjhabhāsi  sabbāva anuyātha maṃ  
  
       vāḷavijanimuṇibhisaṃ khaggaṃ chattaṃ ca paṇḍaraṃ  
 upādirathamāruyha suvaṇṇena  alaṅkato  
  
       tato ca rājā pāyāsi purakkhatvāna  sārathi  
 khippameva upāgañachi yattha sammati temiyo  
  
             
       tañca disvāna āyantaṃ jalantamiva tejasā  
 khattasaṅghaparibbuḷhaṃ  temiyo etadabravi  
  
       kaccinnu  tāta kusalaṃ kacci tāta anāmayaṃ  
 kacacinnu rājakaññāyo arogā mayha mātaro  
  
       kusalañceva me putta atho putta anāmayaṃ  
 sabbāva  rājakaññāyo arogā tuyha mātaro  
  
       kaccissa majjapo  tāta kacci te suramappiyaṃ  
 kacci sacce ca dhamme ca dāne te ramati mano  
  
    thāmasā  syā  kāmunā  machasaṃ    abhāsatha  machasaṃ ajjhabhāsittha  vi 
    suvaṇṇehi  machasaṃ    alaṅkatā  machasaṃ  syā 
    purakkhitvāna  machasaṃ  syā    paribuḷhaṃ  machasaṃ 
    kaccinu  machasaṃ    sabbā ca  machasaṃ    kacci amajjapo  machasaṃ syā 
  
              
       amajjapo ahaṃ puttaṃ atho me suramappiyaṃ  
 atho sacce ca dhamme ca dāne me ramati mano  
  
       kacci arogaṃ yoggaṃ te kacci vahati  vāhanaṃ  
 kacci te vyādhayo natthi sarirassupatāpanā  
  
       atho arogaṃ yoggaṃ me ato vahati vāhanaṃ  
 atho me vyādhayo natthi sarirassupatāpanā  
  
       kacci antā ca te phitā majjhe ca bahalā tava  
 koṭṭhāgārañca kosaññaca kacci te paṭisanthataṃ    
  
       atho antā ca te phitā majjhe ca bahalā mama  
 koṭṭhāgārañca kosaññaca sabbaṃ me paṭisanthataṃ  
  
       svāgataṃ te mahārāja atho te adurāgataṃ  
 patiṭāpentu pallaṅkaṃ pattha rājā nisakkati  
  
             
       idheva te nisinnassa niyate paṇṇasanthate    
 etto udakamādāya pāde pakkhālayantu te  
  
       idampi paṇṇakaṃ mayhaṃ randhaṃ rāja aloṇakaṃ  
 maṃ lābhehi    rohā  machasaṃ  vi    bahuttadhaññā  machasaṃ  syā 
  
       na cāhaṃ  paṇṇaṃ bhuñjāmi na hetaṃ mayha bhojanaṃ  
 sālinaṃ odanaṃ bhuñeja suciṃ  maṃsupasevanaṃ  
  
       accherakaṃ maṃ paṭibhāti ekakampi rabhogataṃ  
 edisaṃ bhuñjamānānaṃ kena vaṇṇo pasidati  
  
             
       eko rāja nipajjāmi niyate paṇṇasanthate  
 tāya me ekaseyyāya rāja vaṇṇo pasidati  
  
       na ce  nettiṃsabaddhā me rājarakkhā upaṭṭhitā  
 tāya me sukhāseyyāya rāja vaṇṇo pasidati  
  
    vāhati  machasaṃ  syā vi    tāpiyā  machasaṃ  syā 
    sandhataṃ  machasaṃ    santhare  machasaṃ 
    navāhaṃ  machasaṃ    suci  machasaṃ  syā    nava  machasaṃ 
  
              
  
       atitaṃ nānusocāmi nappajappamanāgataṃ  
 paccuppannena yāpemi tena vaṇṇo pasidati  
  
       anāgatappajappāya atitassasocanā  
 etena bālā sussanti naḷova bharito luto  
  
       hatthāṇikaṃ rathāṇikaṃ asse patti ca vammino  
 nivesanāni rammāni ahaṃ putta dadāmi te  
  
       itthāgārampi te dammi sabbālaṅkarā bhusitaṃ  
 tā putta paṭipajjassu tvaṃ no rājā bhavissasi  
  
       kusalā naccagitassa sikkhitā caturitthiyo  
 kame taṃ ramayissanti kiṃ araññe karissasi  
  
       paṭirājuhi te kaññā ānayissaṃ alaṅkatā  
 tāsu putte janetvāna atha pacchā pabbajissasi  
       yuvā ca daharo cāsi paṭhamuppattite susu  
 rajjaṃ kārehi bhaddante kiṃ araññe karissasi  
  
       yuvā care buhmacariyaṃ brahmacāri yuvā siyā  
 daharassa hi pabbajjā etaṃ isihi vaṇṇitaṃ  
  
             
  
       yuvā care buhmacariyaṃ brahmacāri yuvā siyā  
 brahmacariyaṃ carissāmi nāhaṃ rajjenamatthiko  
  
       passāmi vohaṃ daharaṃ amma tāta vadaṃ naraṃ    
 kicchā laddhaṃ piyaṃ puttaṃ apapatvāna jaraṃ mataṃ  
  
       passāmi vohaṃ dahariṃ kumāriṃ cāru dassanaṃ  
 naḷavaṃsakaḷiraṃva paluggaṃ jīvitakkhaye  
  
    vadantaraṃ  machasaṃ  syā vi  
  
              
       daharāpi hi miyanti narā ca atha nāriyo  
 tattha ko vissase poso daharomhīti jivite  
  
       yasasa ratyā vivasane āyuṃ appataraṃ siyā  
 appodakeva macchānaṃ kinnu komārakaṃ tahiṃ  
  
       niccamabbhāhato loko niccañca parivārito  
 amoghāsu vajantisu kiṃ maṃ rajjena siñcasi  
  
       kenamabbhāhato loko kena ca parivārito  
 kāyo amoghā gacchanti taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito  
  
       maccunābbhāhato loko jarāya parivārito  
 ratyo amoghā gacchanti evaṃ jānāhi khattiya  
  
       yathāpi tante vitate  yaṃ yadevupavīyayati  
 appakaṃ hoti vetabbaṃ evaṃ maccāna jīvitaṃ  
  
       yathā vārivaho puro gacchannupanivatti    
 evamāyu manussānaṃ gacchannupanivattati  
  
       yathā vārivaho puro vahe rukkhupakulaje    
 evaṃ jarāya maraṇena vuyhante vata pāṇino     
  
             
       hatthāṇikaṃ rathāṇikaṃ asse patti ca vammino  
 nivesanāni rammani ahaṃ puttadadāmi te  
  
       itthāgārampi te dammi sabbālaṅkārabhusitaṃ  
 tā putta paṭipajjassu tvaṃ no rājā bhavissasi  
  
       kusalā naccagītassa sikkhitā caturitthiyo  
 kāme taṃ ramayissanti kiṃ araññe karissasi  
  
    vitante  machasaṃ  syā    gacchaṃ nuparivattati  machasaṃ gacchaṃ na parivattati  syā    ruhepakulaje     sabbapāṇino  machasaṃ  syā 
  
              
       paṭipuhi te kaññā ānayissaṃ ajaṅkatā  
 tāsu putte janetvāna atha pacchā pabbajissasi  
  
       yuvā ca daharo cāsi paṭhamuppattito susu  
 rajjaṃ karehi bhaddante kiṃ araññe karissasi  
  
       koṭṭhāgārañca kosañca vāhanāni balāni ca  
 nivesanāni rammāni ahaṃ punta dadāmi te  
  
       gomaṇḍalaparibbuḷho dāsisaṅghapurakkhato  
 rajjaṃ kārehi bhaddanne kiṃ araññe karissasi  
  
       kiṃ dhanena yaṃ jiyetha kiṃ bhariyāyaya marissati  
 kiṃ yobbanena ciṇṇena yaṃ jarā abhihessati    
  
       tattha kā vandi kā khiḍḍā kā ratī kā dhanesanā    
 ki me puttehi dārehi rāja muttosmi bandhanā  
  
       sohaṃ evaṃ pajānāmi maccu me nappamajjati  
 antakenādhipantassa kā rati kā dhanesanā  
  
             
       phalānamiva pakkānaṃ niccaṃ patanato bhayaṃ  
 evaṃ jātānamaccānaṃ niccaṃ maraṇato bhayaṃ  
  
       sāyameke na dissanti  pato diṭṭhā bahujjanā  
 pato eke na dissanti sāyaṃ diṭṭhā bahujjanā  
  
       ajjeva kiccaṃ ātappaṃ  ko jaññā maraṇaṃ suve  
 nahi no saṅgaraṃ tena mahāsenena maccunā  
  
       corā dhanassa patthessa rājā muttosmi bandhanā  
 ehi rāja nivattassu nāhaṃ rajjenamatthikoti  
 mugapakkhajātakaṃ paṭhamaṃ  
  
    yaṃ jarāyābhibhuyyati  machasaṃ  syā    dhanesinā  machasaṃ  syā 
    passanti  vi    ātapa  machasaṃ 
  
              
    mahājanakajātakaṃ 
             
       koyaṃ majjhe samudadasmiṃ apassaṃ tiramāyuhe  
 kaṃ  tvaṃ atthavasaṃ ñatvā evaṃ vāyamase bhusaṃ  
  
       nisamma vattaṃ lokassa vāyāmassa ca devate  
 tasmā majjhe samuddasmiṃ appasaṃ tiramāyuhe  
  
       gambhīre appameyyasmiṃ tīraṃ yassa na dissati  
 mogho te purisa vāyāmo appatvāva marissi  
  
             
       anaṇo ñātinaṃ hoti devānaṃ pituno  ca so  
 karaṃ purisakiccāni na ca pacchānutappati  
  
       apāraneyyaṃ yaṃ kammaṃ aphalaṃ kilamathuddayaṃ  
 tattha ko vāyamenattho maccu yassābhinippataṃ    
  
       apāraneyyaṃ accantaṃ yo viditvāna devate  
 na rakkhe attano pāṇaṃ jaññā so yadi  hāpaye  
  
       adhippāya phalaṃ eke asmiṃ lokasmi devate  
 payojayanti kammāni tāni ijjhanti vā na vā  
  
       sandiṭṭhikaṃ kammaphalaṃ nanu passasi devate  
 sannā aññe tarāmahaṃ tañca passāmi santike  
  
       so ahaṃ vāyamissāmi yathāsattiṃ yathābalaṃ  
 gacchaṃ pāraṃ samuddassa kāsaṃ  purisakāriyaṃ  
  
             
       yo tvaṃ evaṃ gate oghe appameyye mahaṇṇave  
 dhammavāyāmasampanno kammanā  nāvasidasi  
 so tvaṃ tattheva gacchābhi yattha te  nirato mano  
  
    kiṃ  machasaṃ  syā    pitunañca  machasaṃ  syā    nipaphataṃ  syā 
    yati  machasaṃ    kassaṃ  machasaṃ  syā    kammunā  machasaṃ  syā 
    ke  machasaṃ 
  
              
       suriyuggamane nidhi atho oggamane nidhi  
 anno nidhi bahi nidhi na anto na bahi nidhi  
  
             
       ārohane mahānidhi atho orohane nidhi  
 caturo ca mahāsālā samantā yojane nidhi  
  
       dantaggesu mahānidhi vālaggesu ca kekhuke  
 rukkhaggesu mahānidi soḷasete mahānidhi 
 sahassatthāmo pallaṅko sivalārādhanena ca  
  
             
       āsiṃsetheva puriso  na nibbindeyya paṇḍito  
 passāmi vohaṃ attānaṃ yathā icchiṃ tathā ahu  
  
       āsiṃsetheva puriso na nibbindeyya paṇḍito  
 passāmi vohaṃ attānaṃ udakā thalamubbhataṃ  
  
       vāsiṃsetheva puriso na nibbindeyya paṇḍito  
 passāmi vohaṃ attānaṃ yathā icchiṃ tathā ahu  
  
       vāsiṃsetheva puriso na nibbindeyya paṇḍito  
 passāmi vohaṃ attānaṃ udakā thalamubbhataṃ    
  
       dukkhupanītopi naro sapañño 
 āsaṃ na chindeyya sukhāgamāya  
 bahu hi phassā ahitā hitā ca 
 avitakkitā maccumupabbajanti  
  
       acintitampi bhavati cittitampi vinassati  
 na hi cintāmayā bhogā itthiyā purisassa vā  
  
             
       apurāṇaṃ  vata bho rājā sabbabhummo disampati  
 nājja nacce nisāmeti na gīte kurute mano  
  
       na mige napi uyyāne napi haṃse udikkhati  
 mugova tuṇhimāsino na atthamanusāsati  
  
    āsiṃsetho puriso  machasaṃ    maccumubbajanti  machasaṃ 
    aporāṇaṃ  machasaṃ  syā  vi  
  
              
       sukhakāmā rabhosīlā vadhabandhā upāratā    
 kesannu  ajja ārāme daharā vuddhā ca acchare  
  
             
       atikkantavanathā dhīrā namo tesaṃ mahesinaṃ  
 ye ussukambhi lokambhi viharanti anussukā  
  
       te chetvā maccuno jālaṃ taṃ taṃ māyāvino  
 chintālayattā  gacchanti ko tesaṃ gatimāpaye  
  
       kadāhaṃ mithilaṃ phītaṃ visālaṃ sabbatopabhaṃ    
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu  bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ mithilaṃ phītaṃ vibhattaṃ bhāgaso mitaṃ  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ mithilaṃ phītaṃ bahupākāratoraṇaṃ    
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ mithilaṃ phītaṃ daḷhamaṭṭālakoṭṭhakaṃ  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ mithilaṃ phītaṃ suvibhattaṃ mahāpathaṃ  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ mithilaṃ phītaṃ suvibhattantarājaṇaṃ  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ mithilaṃ phītaṃ gavāssarathapīḷitaṃ  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
             
       kadāhaṃ mithilaṃ phītaṃ ārāmavanamāliniṃ  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
    apārutā  machasaṃ  syā upārutā  si  mu     kassanu  machasaṃ  syā 
    sandālayantā  machasaṃ  syā    pabbato pabhaṃ  machasaṃ    kudassu  machasaṃ    bahalapākāratoraṇaṃ  sihaḷa aṭṭhakathā  he vi    piṭa   kāṇḍaya  
  
              
       kadāhaṃ mithilaṃ phītaṃ uyyānavanamāliniṃ  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu  bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ mithilaṃ phītaṃ pāsādavanamāliniṃ  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ mithilaṃ phītaṃ tiparaṃ  rājabandhuniṃ  
 māpitaṃ somanassena vedehena yasassinā 
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ vedehe  phītaṃ nivite dhammarakkhite  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ vedehe phītaṃ ajeye dhammarakkhite  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ antepuraṃ rammaṃ vibhattaṃ bhāgaso mitaṃ  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāhaṃ antepuraṃ rammaṃ sudhāmattikalepanaṃ  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāhaṃ antepuraṃ rammaṃ sucigandhaṃ manoramaṃ  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāhaṃ kūṭāgāre vibhatte bhāgaso mite  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāhaṃ kūṭāgāre ca sudhāmattikalepane  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāhaṃ kūṭāgāre ca sucigandhe manorame  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāhaṃ kūṭāgāre ca litte candanaphosite    
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
    taṃ kudassu  machasaṃ  taṃ kadāsu  syā    taṃ puraṃ  machasaṃ 
    videhe  machasaṃ    bhūsite  machasaṃ 
  
              
       kadāhaṃ suvaṇṇapallaṅke goṇake cittasanthate  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāhaṃ maṇipallaṅke goṇake cittasanthate  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāhaṃ kappāsakoseyyaṃ khomakoṭumbarāni ca  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāhaṃ pokkharaṇiyo rammā cakkavākupakujitā  
 mandālakehi sañachantā padumuppalakehi ca pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssa  bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ hatthigumbe sabbālaṅkārabhusite  
 suvaṇṇakacche mātaṅge hemakappanavāsase  
  
       ārūḷhe gāmaṇiyehi tomaraṅkusapāṇihi  pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāhaṃ assagumbe sabbālaṅkārabhusite  
 ājāniyye ca jātiyā sindhave sīghavāhane  
  
       ārūḷhe gāmaṇiyehi illiyāvāpadhārihi  pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
             
       kadāhaṃ rathaseṇiyo pantaddhe ussitadadhaje  
 dīpe athopi veyyagghe sabbālaṅkārabhusite  
  
       ārūḷhe gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vamamihi  pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ sovaṇṇarathe sannaddhe ussitaddhaje  
 dīpe athopi veyyagghe sabbālaṅkārabhusite  
  
       ārūḷhe gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ sajjhurathe sannaddhe ussitaddhaje  
 dipe athopi veyyagghe sabbālaṅkārabhūsite  
  
       ārūḷhe gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
    cakkavakkapakujitā  machasaṃ    taṃ kudassu  machasaṃ  kadāsu  syā 
    hemakappanivāsaye  machasaṃ 
  
              
       kadāhaṃ assarathe sannaddhe ussitaddhaje  
 dipe athopi veyyagghe sabbālaṅkārabhūsite  
  
       ārūḷhe gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ oṭṭharathe sannaddhe ussitaddhaje  
 dipe athopi veyyagghe sabbālaṅkārabhūsite  
  
       ārūḷhe gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ goṇarathe sannaddhe ussitaddhaje  
 dipe athopi veyyagghe sabbālaṅkārabhūsite  
  
       ārūḷhe gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ ajarathe sannaddhe ussitaddhaje  
 dipe athopi veyyagghe sabbālaṅkārabhūsite  
  
       ārūḷhe gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ meṇḍarathe sannaddhe ussitaddhaje  
 dipe athopi veyyagghe sabbālaṅkārabhūsite  
  
       ārūḷhe gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ migarathe sannaddhe ussitaddhaje  
 dipe athopi veyyagghe sabbālaṅkārabhūsite  
  
       ārūḷhe gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ hatthārūhe  sabbālaṅkārabhusite  
 nīlavammadhare  sure tomaraṅkusa pāṇine pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
    migaratheva  machasaṃ    hatthāroheva  machasaṃ    nīlavammidhareva  machasaṃ 
  
              
       kadāhaṃ assārūhe  sabbālaṅkārabhusite  
 nīlavammadhare sure illiyācāpadhārine pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ rathārūhe  sabbālaṅkārabhusite  
 nīlavammadhare sure cāpahatthe kalāpine   pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
             
  
       kadāhaṃ dhanuggahe sabbālaṅkārabhusite  
 nīlavammadhare sure cāpahatthe  kalāpine pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ rājaputte  sabbālaṅkārabhusite  
 cittavammadhare sure kañcanāveḷadhārine pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāhaṃ ariyagaṇe vatthavante  alaṅkate  
 haricandanalittaṅge kāsikuttamadhārine pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ amaccagaṇe sabbālaṅkārabhusite  
 pitavammadhare sure purato gacchamāline pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadā sattasatā bhariyā sabbalaṅkārabhusitā  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadā sattasatā bhariyā susaññā tanumajjhimā  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadā sattasatā bhariyā assavā piyabhāṇini  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadā sataphalaṃ kaṃsaṃ sovaṇṇaṃ satarājikaṃ  
 pahāya pabbajissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
    assāroheva  machasaṃ  syā    rathāroheva  machasaṃ  syā 
    kalāpino  syā    cāpahattha  machasaṃ    rājaputteva  machasaṃ    vatavante  machasaṃ 
              
       kadāsasu maṃ hatthagumbā sabbalaṅkārabhusitā  
 suvaṇṇakacchā mātaṅgā hemakappanavāsasā  
  
       ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi tomaraṃkusapāṇihi  
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāsasu maṃ assagumbā sabbalaṅkārabhusitā  
 ājāniyā ca jātiyā sindhavā sighavāhanā  
  
       ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi illiyācāpadhārihi  
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāsasu maṃ rathaseṇiyo sannaddhā ussitaddhajā  
 dipā athopi veyyagghā sabbālaṅkārabhusitā  
  
       ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāsasu maṃ soṇṇarathā sannaddhā ussitaddhajā  
 dipā athopi veyyagghā sabbālaṅkārabhusitā 
  
       ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
             
       kadāsasu maṃ sajjhurathā sannaddhā ussitaddhajā  
 dipā athopi veyyagghā sabbālaṅkārabhusitā 
  
       ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāsasu maṃ assarathā sannaddhā ussitaddhajā  
 dipā athopi veyyagghā sabbālaṅkārabhusitā 
  
       ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāsasu maṃ oṭṭharathā sannaddhā ussitaddhajā  
 dipā athopi veyyagghā sabbālaṅkārabhusitā 
  
       ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
              
       kadāsasu maṃ goṇarathā sannaddhā ussitaddhajā  
 dipā athopi veyyagghā sabbālaṅkārabhusitā 
  
       ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāsasu maṃ ajarathā sannaddhā ussitaddhajā  
 dipā athopi veyyagghā sabbālaṅkārabhusitā 
  
       ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāsasu maṃ meṇḍarathā sannaddhā ussitaddhajā  
 dipā athopi veyyagghā sabbālaṅkārabhusitā 
  
       ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāsasu maṃ migarathā sannaddhā ussitaddhajā  
 dipā athopi veyyagghā sabbālaṅkārabhusitā 
  
       ārūḷhā gāmaṇiyehi cāpahatthehi vammihi  
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāsasu maṃ hatthārūhā sabbālaṅkārabhusitā  
 nīlavammadharā surā tomaraṅkusapāṇino 
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
       kadāssu maṃ assārūhā sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā  
 nīlavammadharā surā illiyā  cāpadhārino 
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāssu maṃ rathārūhā sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā  
 nīlavammadharā surā illiyā  cāpadhārino 
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāssu maṃ dhanuggahā sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā  
 nīlavammadharā surā illiyā cāpadhārino 
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
    indiyā  syā 
  
              
       kadāssu maṃ rājaputtā sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā  
 cittavammadharā surā kañcanāveṭṭhārino 
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu  bhavissati  
  
       kadāssu maṃ ariyagaṇā vatthavantā alaṅkatā  
 haricandanalittaṅgā kāsikuttamadhārino 
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāssu maṃ amaccagaṇā sabbalaṅkārabhusitā  
 pitavammadharā surā purato gacchamālinī 
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāssu maṃ sannatā bhariyā sabbalaṅkārabhusitā  
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
             
       kadāssu maṃ sannatā bhariyā susaññā tanumajjhimā  
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāssu maṃ sannatā bhariyā assavā piyabhāṇini  
 yantaṃ maṃ nānuyissanti taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ pattaṃ gahetvā muṇḍo saṅghāṭipāruto  
 piṇḍikāyā carissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ paṃsukūlānaṃ ujjhitānaṃ mahāpathe  
 saṅghāṭiṃ dhārayissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ sattāhaṃ meghe  ocaṭṭo  allacīvaro  
 piṇḍikāyā carissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ sabbahaṃ  ṭhānaṃ rukkhā rukkhā vanā vanaṃ  
 anapekkho viharissāmi  taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ giriduggesu pahinabhatyabheravo  
 adutiyo viharissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
    taṃ kudāssu  machasaṃ  kadusā  syā    sammeghe  vi machasaṃ 
    ovaṭṭho  machasaṃ ovaṭṭhe  syā    sabbaṭṭhāna gantvā  machasaṃ sabbaṇhaṃ  syā    gamissāmi  machasaṃ    gamissāmi  machasaṃ  syā 
  
              
       kadā vīṇaṃva rujako sattatantiṃ manoramaṃ  
 cittaṃ ujuṃ karissāmi taṃ kadāssu bhavissati  
  
       kadāhaṃ rathakārova parikantaṃ upāhanaṃ  
 kāmasaṃyojanena chevachaṃ  ye dibbe ye ca mānuse  
  
             
       tā ca sattasatā bhariyā sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā  
 bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ kasmā no vijahissasi  
       tā ca sattasatā bhariyā susaññā tanumajjhimā  
 bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ kasmā no vijahissasi  
  
       tā ca sattasatā bhariyā assavā piyabhāṇini  
 bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ kasmā no vijahissasi  
  
       tā ca sattasatā bhariyā sabbālaṅkārabhūsitā  
 hitvā sampaddayi  rājā pabbajjāya purakkhato  
       tā ca sattasatā bhariyā susaññā tanumajjhimā  
 hitvā sampaddayi rājā pabbajjāya purakkhato  
       tā ca sattasatā bhariyā assavā piyabhāṇinī  
 hitvā sampaddayi rājā pabbajjāya purakkhato  
  
             
       hitvā sataphalaṃ  kaṃsaṃ sovaṇṇaṃ satarājikaṃ  
 aggahi matatikāpattaṃ  taṃ dutiyābhisecanaṃ  
  
       vesmā aggismā jālā kosā  ḍayhanti bhāgaso  
 rajataṃ jātarūpañca muttā veḷuriyā bahuṃ  
  
       maraṇayo saṅkhamuttā ca vatthikaṃ  haricandanaṃ  
 ajinaṃ dantabhaṇḍañca lohaṃ kāḷāyasaṃ bahu 
 ehi rāja nivattassu mā te taṃ vinasā  dhanaṃ  
  
    chetvā  machasaṃ    sampaddavi  machasaṃ sampadavi  syā 
    satapalaṃ  machasaṃ  syā    mattikaṃ  machasaṃ    koṭṭhā  vi 
    vatthakaṃ  machasaṃ    vinassā  machasaṃ syā 
              
       susukhaṃ vata jivāma yesaṃ no natthi kiñcanaṃ  
 mithilāya  ḍayahmānāya na me kiñci aḍayhatha  
  
             
       aṭaviyo samuppannā raṭṭhaṃ viddhaṃsayanti taṃ  
 ehi rāja nivantassu mā raṭṭhaṃ vinasā idaṃ  
       susukhaṃ vata jivāma yesaṃ no natthi kiñcanaṃ  
 raṭṭhe vilumpamānambhi na me kiñci ajiratha   
  
       susukhaṃ vata jivāma yesaṃ no natthi kiñcanaṃ  
 pitibhakkhā bhavissāma deva ābhassarā yathā  
  
             
       kimbheso mahato ghoso kā nu gāme kililiyā    
 samaṇaññeva  pucchāma kattheso abhisaṭo  jano  
  
       mamaṃ obhāya gacchantaṃ ettheso abhisaṭo jano  
 simātikkamanaṃ yantaṃ munimonassa pattiyā 
 missaṃ nandihi gacchantaṃ kiṃ jānamanupucchasi  
  
             
       māssu tiṇṇo amaññittho  sarīraṃ dhārayaṃ imaṃ  
 atiraṇeyyamidaṃ  kammaṃ bahu hi paripanthayo  
  
       ko nu me paripanthassa mama evaṃ vihārino  
 yo nevadiṭṭhe nādiṭṭhe kāmānamabhipatthaye  
  
       niddā tandī vijambhikā aratī bhattasammado  
 āvasanti sariraṭṭhā bahuhi paripanthayo  
  
             
       kalyāṇaṃ vata maṃ bhavaṃ brāhmaṇamanusāsasi  
 brahmaṇaṃ yeva  pucchāmi konu tvamasi mārisa  
  
    mithilaṃ  machasaṃ    ahāratha  machasaṃ aḍayhatha māme kicī ahāratha  syā 
    gāmeva kiliyā  machasaṃ kiliyā  syā    samaṇaṃ teva  machasaṃ  syā 
    abhisato  machasaṃ    amuññittha  machasaṃ    atiraṇeyya yamidaṃ bahuhi paribandhayo  machasaṃ    paribandhayo  machasaṃ    tveva  vi machasaṃ  
  
              
       nārado iti me nāmaṃ  kassapo iti maṃ vidu  
 bhoto sakāse āgañachiṃ sādhu sabbhi samāgamo  
  
       tassa te sabbo ānando vihāro upavattatu  
 yadunaṃ taṃ paripurehi khantiyā upasamena ca  
  
       pasāraya santatatañca unnattañca pasāraya  
 kammaṃ vijjañca dhammañca sakkatvāna paribbaja  
  
             
       bahuhatthi ca asse ca nagare janapadāni ca  
 hitvā janaka pabbajito kapalle ratimajjhagā  
  
       kaccinnu te jānapadā  mittā maccā ca ñātakamā  
 dubhiṃ akaṃsu  janaka kasmā cetaṃ  aruccatha  
  
       na migājina jātucca  ahaṃ kañci kudācanaṃ  
 adhammena jine ñātiṃ na cāpi ñātayo mamaṃ  
  
       disvāna lokavantantaṃ khajjantaṃ kaddamikataṃ  
 haññare khajjhare vettha yattha satto puthujjano 
 etāhaṃ upamaṃ katvā bhikkhakosmi migājina  
  
             
       konu te bhagavā satthā kassetaṃ vacanaṃ suci 
 nahi kappaṃ vā vijjaṃ vā paccakkhāya rathesabha  
 samaṇaṃ āhu vattantaṃ yathā dukkhassatikkamo  
  
             na migājina jātucca ahaṃ kañci kudācanaṃ  
 samaṇaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vāpi sakakatvāanupāvisaṃ  
  
    nāmena  machasaṃ  syā    janapadā  machasaṃ    dubbimakaṃsu  machasaṃ 
    te taṃ    jātucche  machasaṃ 
  
              
       mahatā cānubhavena gacchanto siriyājalaṃ  
 giyamānesu gitesu vajjamānesu vaggusu turiyatāḷitasaṃsuṭṭhe smatālasamāhite  
  
       samigājina maddakkhiṃ phalaṃ  ambaṃ tirocchadaṃ  
 tujjamānaṃ  manussehi phalakāmehi  jantuhi  
  
       so kho hantaṃ siriṃ hitvā orohitvā vigājina  
 mulaṃ ambassupāgañchiṃ phalino nipphalitassa ca  
  
       phalaṃ abbaṃ bhataṃ disvā viddhasataṃ  vinalikataṃ  
 athetaṃ itaraṃ ambaṃ nīlohāsaṃ manoramaṃ  
  
             
       evameva nunambhepi issare ihukaṇṭake  
 amittā no vadhissanti yathā ambo phali hato  
  
       ajinamhi haññate dīpi nāgo dantehi haññate  
 dhanambhi dhanino hanti aniketamasanthavaṃ 
 phali ambo aphalo ca te satthāro ubho mama  
  
       sabbo jano pavyadhito rājā pabbajito iti  
 hatthārohā aṇikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārikā  
  
       assāsayitvā janataṃ ṭhapayitvā paṭicchadaṃ  
 puttaṃ rajje ṭhapetvā atha pacchā pabbajissasi  
  
             
       vattā mayā jānapadā mitatāmaccā ca ñātakā  
 santi puttā videhānaṃ dighāvu raṭṭhavaḍḍhano 
 te rajjaṃ kārayissanti mithilāyaṃ pajāpati  
  
       ehi taṃ anusikkhāmi yaṃ vākyaṃ mama ruccati  
 rajjaṃ tuvaṃ kārayanti pāpaṃ duccaritaṃ bahuṃ  
 kāyena vācā manasā yena gañachisi duggatiṃ  
  
    balaṃ ambha  machasaṃ    hatamānaṃ  machasaṃ tudamānaṃ  syā 
    balakāmehi  machasaṃ    vidasataṃ  machasaṃ  
  
              
       paradinnakena paraniṭṭhitena  
 piṇḍena yāpehi sadhiradhammo  
  
             
       yopi catutthe bhattakāle na bhuñje 
 ajaddhumāriva  khudāya mīye  
 na tveva piṇḍaṃ lulitaṃ anariyaṃ 
 kulaputtarūpo sappuriso na seve 
 tayidaṃ na sādhu tayidaṃ na suṭṭhu 
 sunakhucchiṭṭhakaṃ bhuñjase tvaṃ  
  
             
       na cā pi me sīvali so abhakkho 
 yaṃ hoti cannaṃ gihino sunakhassa vā  
 ye keci bhogā idha dhammaladdhā 
 sabbo so bhakkho anavajjāti  vutto  
  
       kumārike  upaseniye niccaṃ nigaḷa  maṇḍita  
 kasmā te eko bhujo janati eko te na janati bhujo  
  
       imasmiṃ me samaṇa hatthe paṭimukko ekanīdhuro    
 saṅghātā jāyate saddo dutiyasseva sā gati  
  
       imasmiṃ me samaṇā hatthe paṭimukko ekanīdhuro    
 so aditiyo na chanati munibhutova tiṭṭhati  
  
       vivādappatto dutiyo keneko vivadissati  
 tassa te saggakāmassa ekattamuparovataṃ  
  
             
       suṇasi  sivalī gāthā kumāriyā paveditā  
 pessiyā maṃ garahittho dutiyasseva sā gati  
  
       ayaṃ dvedhā patho bhadde anuciṇṇo pathāvihi  
 tesaṃ tvaṃ ekaṃ gaṇhāhi abhamekaṃ punāparaṃ  
  
       neva maṃ tvaṃ patī meti māhaṃ bhariyāti vā puna  
 imameva kathaṃ kathayantā thuṇaṃ nagarupāgamuṃ  
  
    ajuttamāriva  machasaṃ ajajjhaṭṭhamāriva  syā ajhajuṭṭhumariva  vi 
    anavaye  machasaṃ    kumāriye  machasaṃ  vi    tikala  machasaṃ 
    dunivarā  machasaṃ  syā    ekanivaro  machasaṃ    suṇāsu  machasaṃ 
  
              
             
       koṭṭhake usukārassa bhattakāle upaṭṭhite  
 tatra ca so usukāro  ekaṃ daṇaḍaṃ ujuṃ kataṃ  
 ekañca cakkhuṃ niggayha jimbhamekena pekkhati  
  
       evaṃ no sādhu passasi usukāra suṇohi me  
 yadekaṃ cakkhuṃ niggayha jibhamamekena pekkhasi  
  
       vihi samaṇa cakkhuhi visālaṃ viya khāyati  
 asampatvā paraṃ  liṅgaṃ nujajubhāvāya kappati  
  
       ekañca cakkhuṃ niggayha jimbhamekena pekkhato  
 sampatvā paramaṃ liṅgaṃ ujubhāvāya kappati  
  
       vivādappatto dutiyo keneko vivadissati  
 tassa te saggakāmassa ekattamuparovataṃ  
  
             
       suṇasī sīvali gāthā usukāreṇa paveditā  
 pessiyā  maṃ garahittho dutiyasseva sā gati  
  
       ayaṃ dvedhā patho bhadde anuciṇṇā pathāvihi  
 tesaṃ tvaṃ ekaṃ gaṇhāhi ahametaṃ punāparaṃ  
  
       neva maṃ tvaṃ pati meti māhaṃ bhariyāti vā puna  
 muñajāvisakā  pavāḷhā ekā vihara sīvalī ti  
 mahājanakajātakaṃ dutiyaṃ  
  
    paramaṃ  machasaṃ    pesiyā  machasaṃ    muñachavesikā  machasaṃ 
  
              
             
    sāmajātakaṃ 
       ko nu maṃ usunā vijjhi pattaṃ udahārakaṃ    
 khattiyo brāhmano vesso ko maṃ viddhā niliyasi    
  
       na me maṃsāni khajjāni cammenattho na vijjati  
 atha kena nu vaṇṇena viddheyyaṃ maṃ amaññatha  
  
       ko vā tvaṃ kasasa vā putte kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ  
 puṭṭho me samma akkhāhi kiṃ maṃ viddhā nilīyasi  
  
       rājāhamasmi kāsinaṃ piliyakkhoti maṃ vidu  
 lobhā raṭṭhaṃ pahatvāna  migamesaṃ  carāmahaṃ  
  
       issatthevassami kusalo daḷhadhammoti vissuto  
 nāgopi me na muñceyya āgato usupātanaṃ  
  
             
       tvañca tassa vā puttosi kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ  
 pituno attano cāpi nāmagottaṃ pavedaya  
  
       nesādaputto bhaddante sāmo iti maṃ ñātayo  
 āmantayiṃsu jivantaṃ svājjevāhaṃ  gato saye  
  
       viddhosmi puthusallena savisena yathā migo  
 sakamhi lohite rāja passa semi paripluto  
  
       paṭicamma gato sallaṃ passa vihāmi  lohitaṃ  
 āturo tyānu pucchāmi kiṃ maṃ viddhā nilīyasi  
  
    udahārayaṃ  machasaṃ    niliyyasi  machasaṃ    pahitvāna  machasaṃ  syā 
    migameso  machasaṃ    svajjevavaṃ  machasaṃ    paṭivā  machasa  syā 
    mimbhāmi  machasaṃ thimahāmi  syā  
              
       ajinambhi haññate dīpi nāgo antehi haññate  
 atha kena nu vaṇṇena viddheyyaṃ maṃ amaññatha  
  
       migo upaṭṭhito āsi āgato usupātanaṃ  
 taṃ disvā ubbijji sāma  tena kodho mamāvisi  
  
             
       yatho sarāmi attānaṃ yato pattosmi viññutaṃ  
 na maṃ migā uttasanti  araññe sāpadānipi  
  
       yato nīdhiṃ parihariṃ yato pattosmi yobbanaṃ  
 na maṃ migā uttasanti araññe sāpadānipi  
  
       bhīrū kimpurisā rāja pabbate gandhamādane  
 sammodamānā gacchāma pabbatāni vanāni ca 
 atha kena nu vaṇṇena uttrase so migo mamaṃ  
  
       na taddasā  migo sāma kintāhaṃ alikaṃ  bhaṇe  
 kodhalobhābhibhutohaṃ usuṃ te taṃ avassajiṃ  
  
       kuto nu samma āgamma kassa vā pahito tuvaṃ  
 udahāro nadiṃ gaccha āgato migasammataṃ  
  
             
       andhā mātā pitā mayhaṃ te bharāmi brahāmane  
 tesāhaṃ udahārako  āgato migasammataṃ  
  
       atthi tesaṃ usāmantaṃ atha sāhassa jīvitaṃ  
 udakassa ca alābhena maññe andhā marissare  
  
    ubbijjissāmi  machasaṃ    utrasanti  machasaṃ  syā    na taṃ tasa  machasaṃ  syā    aliko  machasaṃ    udakaṃ hāṇa  chesaṃ  
  
              
       na me idaṃ tathā dukkhaṃ labbhāhi pumunā idaṃ  
 yañca ammaṃ na passāmi taṃ me dukkhataraṃ ito  
       na me idaṃ tathā dukkhaṃ labbhāhi pumunā idaṃ  
 yañca tātaṃ na passāmi taṃ me dukkhataraṃ ito  
  
       sā nūna kapaṇā ammā cirarattāya rucchati    
 aḍḍharatte ca ratte vā nadiva avasucchati  
  
       so nūna kapaṇo tato cirarattāya rucchati  
 aḍḍharatte ca ratte vā nadiva avasucchati  
  
       uṭṭhānapāricariyāya pādaṃ  sambāhanassa ca  
 sāma tātā ti vilapantā hiṇḍissanti  brahāvane  
  
       idampi dutiyaṃ sallaṃ kampeti hadayaṃ mama  
 yañca andhe na passāmi maññe hessāmi  jīvitaṃ  
  
             
       mā bāḷhaṃ paridevesi sāma kalyāṇadassana  
 ahaṃ kammakaro hutvā bharissaṃ te brahavane  
  
       issatthe casmi kusalo daḷhadhammoti vissuto  
 ahaṃ kammakāro hutvā bharissaṃ te brahavane 
  
       migānaṃ vighāsamanvesaṃ vanamula phalāni ca  
 ahaṃ kammakaro hutvā bharissaṃ te brahāvane 
    ruccati  machasaṃ  syā vi    rāja  machasaṃ    hindisasanti  machasaṃ 
    na me bhissāmi  machasaṃ 
  
              
       katamaṃ taṃ vanaṃ sāma yattha mātā pitā tava  
 ahaṃ te tathā bharissaṃ yathā te ahari tuvaṃ  
  
       ayaṃ ekapadi rāja yo yaṃ ussisake mama  
 ito gantvā aḍḍhakosaṃ tattha  tesaṃ agārakaṃ 
 tattha mātā pitā mayhaṃ te bharassu ito gato  
  
             
       namo te kāsirājatthu namo te kāsivaḍḍhana  
 andhā mātā pitā mayhaṃ bharassu brabhāvane  
  
       añjaliṃ te paggaṇhāmi kāsirāja namatthu te  
 mātaraṃ pitaraṃ mayhaṃ mutto vajjāsi vandanaṃ  
  
       idaṃ vanvāna so sāmo yuvā kalyāṇadassano  
 mucchito visavegena visaññi samapajjatha  
  
       sa rājā paridevesi bahuṃ kāruññasaṃhitaṃ  
 ajarāmaro vahaṃ āsaṃ ajjetaṃ  ñāsi no pure 
 sāmaṃ kālakataṃ disvā natthi maccussa nāgamo  
  
       yassu maṃ patimanteti savisena samappito  
             
 svājjevaṃ gate kāle na kiñci mabhihāsati  
  
       nirayaṃ nūna gacchāmi ettha me natthi saṃsayo  
 tadāhi pakataṃ pāpaṃ cirarattāya kibabisaṃ  
  
       bhavanti tassa vattāro gāme kibbisakārako  
 araññe nimmanussambhi ko maṃ vattumarahati  
  
    yattha  machasaṃ    ajjabhaññāmi  machasaṃ  ajjetaṃ ñāmi  syā 
  
              
       sārayanti hi kamamāni game saṃgaccha mānavā  
 araññe nimmanussambha ko nu maṃ sārayissati  
  
             
       sā devatā antarahitā pabbate gandhamādane  
 raññova anukampāya imā gātā abhāsatha  
  
       āguṃ kari mahārāja akarā  kammadukkaṭaṃ  
 adusakā pitā putatā tayo ekusunā hatā  
  
       ehi taṃ anusikkhāmi yathā te sugati siyā  
 dhammenandhe  vane posa maññehaṃ sugatī tayā  
  
       sa rājā paridevitvā bahuṃ kāruññasaṃhitaṃ  
 udakakumbhamādāya pakkāmi dakkhiṇāmukho  
  
             
       kassa na eso padasaddo manussasseva āgato  
 neso  sāmassa nigoso ko nu tvamasi mārisaṃ  
  
       santaṃ hi sāmo vajati santaṃ pādāni ñattiti    
 noso sāmassa niggheso ko nu tvamasi mārisa  
  
       rājāhamassami kāsinaṃ piliyakkhoti maṃ vidu  
 lobhā raṭṭhaṃ pahatvāna  migamesaṃ  varāmahaṃ  
  
       issatthe casmi kusalo daḷhadhammoti vissuto  
 nāgopi me na muñceya āgato usupātanaṃ  
  
       svāgatante mahārāja atho te adurāgataṃ  
 issarosi anuppatto yaṃ idhatthi pavedaya  
  
       tindukāni piyālāni madhuke kāsumāriyo  
 phalāni khuddakappāni bhuñja rāja varaṃ varaṃ  
  
    akari  machasaṃ  syā vi akāraṃ  simu    dhammena te  machasaṃ 
    no  machasaṃ    neyati  machasaṃ    pahitvāna  machasaṃ 
    migameso  machasaṃ 
  
              
       idampi pānīyaṃ sītaṃ ābhataṃ girigabbharā  
 tato piva mahārāja sace tvaṃ abhikaṅkhasi  
  
             
       nālaṃ andhā vane daṭṭhuṃ ko nu me  phalamāharī  
 anandhassevayaṃ samamā nivāpo  mayha khāyati  
  
       daharo yuvā nātibrahā sāmo kalyāṇadassano  
 dighassa kesā asitā atho sunaggavellitā  
  
       so bhave phalamāhatvā ito ādā kamaṇḍaluṃ  
 nadiṃ gato udahāro maññe na duramāgato  
  
       ahaṃ ta ṃavadhiṃ sāmaṃ yo tuyhaṃ paricārako  
 yaṃ kumāraṃ pavedetha sāmaṃ kalyānadassanaṃ  
  
       dīghassa kesā asitā atho sunaggavellitā  
 tesu lohitalittesu seti sāmo mayā hato  
  
             
       kena dukulamantesi hato sāmoti vādinā  
 hato sāmāti sutvāna hadayaṃ me pavedhati  
  
       assatthasseva taruṇaṃ pavālaṃ māluteritaṃ  
 hato sāmoti sutvāna hadayaṃ me pavedhati  
  
       pārike kāsirājāya so sāmaṃ vigasammate  
 kodhasā usunā vijjha tassa mā pāpamicchimbhā  
  
       kicchā laddho piyo putto yo andho abharī vane  
 taṃ ekaputtaṃ ghātimbhi kathaṃ citataṃ na kopaye  
  
       kicchā laddho piyo putto yo andho abharī vane  
 taṃ ekaputtaṃ ghātimbhi akkodhaṃ ahu paṇḍitā  
  
    vo  machasaṃ  syā    nivāto  machasaṃ 
  
              
       mā khāḷhaṃ paridevetha hato sāmāti vādinā  
 ahaṃ kammakaro hutvā bharissāmi brahāmane  
  
       issatthe casami kusalo daḷhadhammoti visasuto  
 ahaṃ kammakāro hutvā bharissāmi brahvane  
  
       migānaṃ  vighāsamanvesaṃ vanamula phalāni ca  
 ahaṃ kammakaro hutvā bharissāmi brahāmane  
  
             
       nesa dhammo mahārāja netaṃ ambhesu kappati  
 rājā tvampi ambhākaṃ pade vandāma te mayaṃ  
  
       dhammaṃ nesāda bhaṇatha katā apaviti tayā  
 pitā tvamasi ambhākaṃ mātā tvamasi pārike  
  
       namo te kāsirājatthu namo te kāsivaḍḍhana  
 añjaliṃ te pagaṇhāma yāva sāmānupāpaya  
  
       tassa pāde pamajjantā  mukhañca bhujadassanaṃ  
 saṃsumbhamānā antānaṃ kālamāgamayāmase  
  
             
       brahā vāḷamigākiṇṇaṃ ākāsantaṃ padissati  
 yattha sāmo hato seti candova patito chamā  
       brahā vāḷamigākiṇṇaṃ ākāsantaṃ padissati  
 yattha sāmo hato seti suriyova patito chamā  
  
       brahā vāḷamigākiṇṇaṃ ākāsantaṃ padissati  
 yattha sāmo hato seti paṃsunā patikuṇṭhito 
  
       brahā vāḷamigākiṇṇaṃ ākāsantaṃ padissati  
 yattha sāmo hato seti idheva vasatha assame  
  
       yadi tattha sahassāni satāni nahutāni ca  
 nevambhakāṃ bhayaṃ koci vane vāḷesu vijjati  
  
    magānaṃ  machasaṃ    pavaṭṭantā  vi samajjantā  machasaṃ  syā  
  
              
       tato andhānamādāya kāsirājā brahāvane  
 hatthe gahetvā pakkāmi yattha sāmo hato ahu  
  
             
       disvāna patitaṃ sāmaṃ puttakaṃ paṃsukuṇṭhitaṃ  
 apaviddhaṃ brahāraññe candaṃva patitaṃ chamā  
  
       disvāna patitaṃ sāmaṃ puttakaṃ paṃsukuṇṭhitaṃ  
 apaviddhaṃ brahāraññe suriyaṃva patitaṃ chamā  
  
       disvāna patitaṃ sāmaṃ puttakaṃ paṃsukuṇṭhitaṃ  
 apaviddhaṃ brahāraññe karuṇaṃ paridevayuṃ  
  
       disvāna patitaṃ sāmaṃ puttakaṃ paṃsukuṇṭhitaṃ  
 bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ adhammo kira bho iti  
  
       khāḷhaṃ khosi tuvaṃ sutto sāmakalyāṇadassana  
 yo ajjevaṃ gate kāle na kiñci mabibhāsasi  
       khāḷhaṃ khosi tuvaṃ matto sāmakalyāṇadassana  
 yo ajjevaṃ gate kāle na kiñci mabibhāsasi  
       khāḷhaṃ khosi tvaṃ pamattosi  sāma kalyāṇadassana  
 yo ajjevaṃ gate kāle na kiñci mabibhāsasi  
       khāḷhaṃ khosi tuvaṃ kuddho  sāmakalyāṇadassana  
 yo ajjevaṃ gate kāle na kiñci mabibhāsasi  
       khāḷhaṃ khosi tuvaṃ ditto sāmakalyāṇadassana  
 yo ajjevaṃ gate kāle na kiñci mabibhāsasi  
       khāḷhaṃ khosi tvaṃsi vimanosi sāmakalyāṇadassana  
 yo ajjevaṃ gate kāle na kiñci mabibhāsasi  
    puttosi  machasaṃ    patuḍosi  machasaṃ    paditto  machasaṃ 
  
              
       jaṭaṃ valitaṃ paṅka gataṃ kodāni saṇṭhapessati  
 sāmo ayaṃ kālakato  andhānaṃ paricārako  
  
       ko ce sammajjanādāya  samamajjissati assamaṃ  
 sāmo ayaṃ kālakato andhānaṃ paricārako  
       kodāni nabhāpayisasti sitenuṇhodakena ca  
 sāmo ayaṃ kālakato andhānaṃ paricārako  
             
       kodāni bhojayissati vanamulaphalāni ca  
 sāmo ayaṃ kālakato andhānaṃ paricārako  
  
       disvāna patitaṃ sāmaṃ puttakaṃ paṃsukuṇaṭhitaṃ  
 aṭṭitā puttasokena mātā saccamabhāsatha  
  
       yena saccenayaṃ sāmo dhammacāri re ahu  
 etena sacacavajjena visaṃ sāmasasa haññatu  
  
       yena saccenayaṃ sāmo brammacāri dura ahu  
 etena sacacavajjena visaṃ sāmasasa haññatu  
  
       yena saccenayaṃ sāmo saccavādi pūre ahu  
 etena sacacavajjena visaṃ sāmasasa haññatu  
  
       yena saccenayaṃ sāmo mātā petti bharo ahu  
 etena sacacavajjena visaṃ sāmasasa haññatu  
  
       yena saccenayaṃ sāmo kule jeṭṭhāpacāyiko  
 etena sacacavajjena visaṃ sāmasasa haññatu  
  
       yena saccenayaṃ sāmo pāṇā piyataro mama  
 etena sacacavajjena visaṃ sāmasasa haññatu  
  
       yaṃ kiñcitthi kataṃ puññaṃ mayhaṃ ceva pitucca te  sacacana tena kusalena visaṃ sāmasasa haññatu  
  
             
       disvāna patitaṃ sāmaṃ puttakaṃ paṃsukuṇaṭhitaṃ  
 aṭṭito puttasokena pitā saccamabāsatha  
  
    paṃsu  machasaṃ    kālaṅkato  machasaṃ    sammajjamādāya  machasaṃ 
    pitati  machasaṃ    sabbena  machasaṃ 
  
              
       yena saccenayaṃ sāmo dhammacāri pure ahu  
 etena sacacavajjena visaṃ sāmasasa haññatu  
  
       yena saccenayaṃ sāmo brammacāri pure ahu  
 etena sacacavajjena visaṃ sāmasasa haññatu  
  
       yena saccenayaṃ sāmo saccavādi pūre ahu  
 etena sacacavajjena visaṃ sāmasasa haññatu  
  
       yena saccenayaṃ sāmo mātāpettibharo ahu  
 etena sacacavajjena visaṃ sāmasasa haññatu  
  
       yena saccenayaṃ sāmo kule jeṭṭhāpacāyiko  
 etena sacacavajjena visaṃ sāmasasa haññatu  
  
       yena saccenayaṃ sāmo pāṇā piyataro mama  
 etena sacacavajjena visaṃ sāmasasa haññatu  
  
       yaṃ kiñcātthi kataṃ puññaṃ mayhaṃ ca mātuyā ca te  
 saccena tena kusalena visaṃ sāmassa haññatu  
       sā devatā antarahitā pabbate gandhamādane  
 sāmassa anukampāya imaṃ saccamābhasatha  
  
       pabbatyāhaṃ gandhamādane cirarattanivāsinī  
 na me piyataro koci añño sāmā  na vijjati  
 etena saccavajjena visaṃ sāmassa haññatu  
  
       sabbe vanā gandhamayā pabbate gandhamādane  
 etena sacacavajjena visaṃ sāmasasa haññatu  
  
             
       sāmo hamasmi bhaddaṃ bahuṃ kāruññasaṃhitaṃ  
 khippaṃ sāmo samuṭṭhāsi yuvā kalyāṇadassano  
  
       samo hamasmi bhaddaṃ vo sotthināmhi samuṭṭhito  
 mā bāḷhaṃ paridevetha mañjunābhivadetha maṃ  
  
       svāgatante mahārāja atho te adurāgataṃ  
 issarosi anupapatto yaṃ idhatthi pavedaya  
  
    samo  machasaṃ  sāmena  syā 
  
              
  
       tindukāni  piyālāni madhuke kāsumāriyo  
 phalāni khuddakappāni bhuñja rāja vara varaṃ  
  
       atthi maṃ pāṇiyaṃ sītaṃ ābhataṃ girigabbharā  
 tato piva mahārāja sace tvaṃ abhikaṅkhasi  
  
       sammuyhāmi pamuyhāmi sabbā muyhanti me disā  
 petaṃ taṃ sāma addakkhiṃ  konu tvaṃ sāma jivasi  
  
       api jīvaṃ mahārāja purisaṃ gāḷhavedanaṃ  
 upanitamanasaṅkappaṃ jivantaṃ maññate mataṃ  
       api jīvaṃ mahārāja purisaṃ gāḷhavedanaṃ  
 taṃ nirodhagataṃ santaṃ jivantaṃ maññate mataṃ  
             
       yo mātaraṃ vā pitaraṃ vā macco dhammena posati  
 devāpi naṃ tikicchanti mātāpetti bharaṃ janaṃ  
  
       yo mātaraṃ vā pitaraṃ vā macco dhammena posati  
 idha ceva naṃ pasaṃsanti pecca sagge ca modati  
  
       esa bhiyyo pamuyhāmi sabbā muyhanti medisā  
 saraṇaṃ taṃ sāma gacchāmi tvañca me saraṇaṃ bhavā 
  
       dhammaṃ cara mahārāja mātāpitusu khattiya  
 idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamisassi  
       dhammaṃ cara mahārāja puttadāresu khattiya  
 idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamisassi  
       dhammaṃ cara mahārāja mittāmaccesu khattiya  
 idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamisassi  
       dhammaṃ cara mahārāja vāhanesu balesu ca  
 idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamisassi  
    tiṇḍunānitipi pātho    mamadakkhi  machasaṃ    naraṃ  machasaṃ  syā 
  
              
       dhammaṃ cara mahārāja gāmesu nigamesu ca  
 idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamisassi  
       dhammaṃ cara mahārāja raṭṭhesu janapadesu ca  
 idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamisassi  
       dhammaṃ cara mahārāja samaṇabrāhmaṇesu ca  
 idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamisassi  
       dhammaṃ cara mahārāja migapakkhisu khattiyā  
 idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamisassi  
       dhammaṃ cara mahārāja dhammo ciṇṇo sukhāvaho  
 idha dhammaṃ caritvāna rāja saggaṃ gamisassi  
       dhammaṃ cara mahārāja dhammo ciṇṇo sukhāvaho  
 idha dhammaṃ caritvāna sa indā devā sabrahmakā 
 suciṇṇena divaṃ sattā mā dhammaṃ rāja pamādoti  
 sāmajātakaṃ tatiyaṃ  
  
    nimijātakaṃ 
             
       accheraṃ vata lokasmiṃ upapajjanti vicakkhaṇā  
 yadā ahu nimirājā paṇḍito kusalatthiko  
  
       rājā sabbavidebhānaṃ adā dānaṃ arindamo  
 tassa taṃ dadato dānaṃ saṅkeppā udapajjatha  
 dānaṃ vā brahmacariyaṃ vā katamaṃsu mahapphalaṃ  
  
             
       tassa saṅkappamaññāya maghavā devakuñajaro  
 sahassanetto pāturahu vaṇṇena nibhataṃ tamaṃ  
  
              
       sa lomahaṭṭho manujindo vāsavaṃ avacā nimi  
 devatānusi gandhabbo ādu sakko purindado  
  
       na ca me tādiso vaṇṇo diṭṭho vā yadi vā suto  
 ācikkha me tvaṃ bhaddante kathaṃ jānemu taṃ mayaṃ  
  
       sa lomahaṭṭhaṃ ñatvāna vāsavo avacā nimiṃ  
 sakkohamasmi devindo āgatosmi tavantiko  
  
       alomahaṭṭho manujinda puccha pañhaṃ yadicchasi  
 so ca tena kātokāso vāsavaṃ avacā nimi  
  
       pucachāmi taṃ mahābāhu sabbabhūtānamissara  
 dānaṃ vā brahmacariyaṃ vākatamaṃsu mahapphalaṃ 
  
       so puṭṭho naradevena vāsavo avacā nimiṃ  
 vipākaṃ brahmacariyassa jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       hītena brahmacariyena khattiye upapajjati  
 majjhimena ca devantaṃ uttamena visujjhati  
  
       nahete pulabhā kāyā yāvayogena kenaci  
 yo kāye upapajjanti anāgārā tapassino  
  
             
       dudipo dāgāro selo mucalindo bhagīraso  
 usinaro  aṭṭhako ca assako ca puthujjano  
  
       ete caññe ca rājāno khattiyā brahmaṇā bahu  
 puthu yaññaṃ yajitvāna petaṃ te nātivattisuṃ  
  
       ye ve adutiyā na ramalanti ekikā 
 vivekajaṃ ye na labhanti pitiṃ  
 kiñcāpi te indasamānabhogā 
 te ve parādhinasukhā varākā  
  
    yamicchasi  machasaṃ    usindaro  machasaṃ usinaro  vi 
  
              
       addhā ime  avattiṃsu anāgarā tapassino  
 sattisayo yāmahanu somayāgo  manojavo  
  
       samuddo māgho bharato ca  isikālikarakkhiyo    
 aṃgiraso kassapo ca kisavaccho akitti ca    
  
              
       uttarena nadi sidā gambhirā duratikkamā  
 naḷaggivaṇṇā jotanti sadā kañcanapabbatā  
  
       parūḷhakacchā tagarā rūḷhakacchā vanā nagā  
 tatrāsuṃ dasasabhassāni porāṇā isayo pure  
  
       ahaṃ seṭṭhosmi dānena saṃyamena damena ca  
 anuttaraṃ vataṃ katvā pakiracāri samahite  
  
       jātimantaṃ ajaccaṃ ca ahamujjugataṃ naraṃ  
 ativelaṃ namassissaṃ kammabandhu hi mātiyā  
  
       sabbe vaṇaṇā adhammaṭṭhā patanati nirayaṃ adho  
 sabbe vaṇaṇā nirujjhanti  caritvā dhammamuttamaṃ  
  
              
       idaṃ vatvāna maghavā devarājā sujampati  
 vedehaṃ anusāsitvā saggakāyaṃ apakkami  
  
       imaṃ honto nisāmetha yāvantettha samāgatā  
 dhammikānaṃ manusasānaṃ vaṇaṇaṃ uccāvacaṃ bahuṃ  
  
       yathā ayaṃ nimirājā paṇḍito kusalatthiko  
 rājā sabbavidehānaṃ adā dānaṃ arindamo  
  
       tassa taṃ dadako dānaṃ saṅkappo udapajjatha  
 dānaṃ vā brahmacariyaṃ vā katamaṃsu mahappalaṃ  
  
    atha ime  machasaṃ    somayāmo  machasaṃ    bharado ca  machasaṃ 
    isikālapurakkhato  machasaṃ    akanati ca  machasaṃ    māṇavā  machasaṃ 
    visujjhanti  vi machasaṃ  
  
              
              
       abbhuto vata lokasmiṃ uppajji lomahaṃsano  
 dibbo ratho pāturahu vedehassa yasassino  
  
              
       devaputto hiddhiko mātalī devasārathi  
 nimantiyitthi rājānaṃ vedehaṃ mithilaggahaṃ  
  
       ehimaṃ rathamāruyha rājaseṭṭha disampati  
 devā dassanakāmā te tāvatiṃsā saindakā 
 saramānā hi te devā sudhammāyaṃ samacchare  
  
       tato ca rājā taramāno vedeho mithilaggaho  
 āsanā vuṭṭhahivona pamukho rathamāruhi  
  
       abhirūḷhaṃ ethaṃ dabbaṃ mātalī etadabravi  
 kena taṃ nemi maggena rājaseṭṭha disampati  
 yena vā pāpakammantā puññakammā ca ye narā  
  
       ubhayeneva maṃ nehi mātalī devasārathi  
 yena vā pāpakammantā puññakammā ca ye narā  
  
       kena taṃ paṭhamaṃ nemi rājaseṭṭha disampati  
 yena vā pāpakammantā puññakammā ca ye narā  
  
              
       niraye  tāva passāmi āvāse  pāpakamminaṃ  
 ṭhānāni luddakammānaṃ dussilānaṃ ca yā gati  
  
       dassesi mātalī rañño duggaṃ vetaraṇiṃ nadiṃ  
 kuthantiṃ  khārasaṃyuttaṃ tattaṃ aggisikhumaṃ  
  
    nirayaṃ  machasaṃ    āvāsaṃ  machasaṃ    kuṭṭhitaṃ  machasaṃ 
  
              
              
       nimi bhave mātalīṃ ajjhabhāsatha 
 disvā janaṃ patamānaṃ vidugge  
 bhayaṃ hi maṃ vindati suta disvā 
 pucchāmi taṃ mātalī devasārathi 
 ime nu maccā kimakaṃsu pāpaṃ 
 yeme janā vetaraṇi  pattati  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ pāpa kammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato  
  
       ye dubbale balavanto jivaloke 
 hiṃsenti rosenti supāpadhammā  
 te luddakammā pasavetvā pāpaṃ 
 te ve janā vetaraṇi patanti  
  
       sāmā ca soṇā sabalā ca gijjhā 
 kākoḷasaṅghā ca adenti bheravā 
 bhayaṃ hi maṃ vindati suta disvā 
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi 
 ime nu maccā kimakaṃsa pāpaṃ 
 yayimaṃ janaṃ  kākoḷā adenti  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ pāpa kammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       ye keci me maccharino kadariyā 
 parihāsakā samaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃ 
 hisenti rosenti supāpadhammo  
 te luddakamamā pasavetvā pāpaṃ 
 tayimaṃ janaṃ kākoḷā adenti  
  
              
       sajotibhūtā paṭhaviṃ kamanti 
 tatetehi khandhehi ca pothayanti pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi 
 ime nu maccā kimakaṃsu pāpaṃ 
 yeme janā khandhahatā sayanti  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ pāpakammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
    vettaraṇiṃ  machasaṃ    akkhāsi  machasaṃ  syā    ye me jane  machasaṃ  syā  
  
              
       ye jivalokasmiṃ supāpadhammino 
 narañca nāriñca apāpadhammaṃ 
 hiṃsenti rosenti supāpadhammā 
 te luddakammā pasavetthā  pāpaṃ 
 teme janā khandhatā sayanti  
  
              
       aṅgakāsuṃ apare thananti 
 narā rudantā paridaḍḍhagantā 
 bhayaṃ hi maṃ vindati suta disvā 
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 ime nu maccā kimakaṃsu pāpaṃ 
 yeme janā aṅgārakāsuṃ thananti  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ pāpakammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       ye keci pugāyatanassa hetu 
 sakkhiṃ karitvā iṇaṃ jāpayanti 
 te jāpayitvā janataṃ janinda 
 te luddakammā pasavetvā pāpaṃ 
 teme janā aṅgārakāsuṃ thananti 
  
       sajotibhūtā jalitā padittā 
 padissati mahati lohakumhī 
 bhayaṃ hi maṃ vindati suta disvā 
 ime nu maccā kimakaṃsu pāpaṃ 
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi 
 yeme janā avaṃsirā lohakumbhiṃ patanti  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ pāpa kammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       ye sīlavaṃ samaṇaṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vā 
 hiṃsenti rosenti  supāpadhammino 
 te luddakammā pasavetvā pāpaṃ 
 tome janā  avaṃsirā  lohakumbhiṃ patanti  
  
    pasavetvāna  machasaṃ    punanti  machasaṃ    hiṃsanti rosanti  machasaṃ 
  
              
              
       luñcenti givaṃ atha veṭhayitvā  
 uṇhodakasmiṃ pakiledayitvā 
 bhayaṃ hi maṃ vindati suta disvā 
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi 
 ime nu maccā kimakaṃsu pāpaṃ 
 yeme janā luttasirā  sayanti  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ pāpa kammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       ye jivalokasmiṃ supāpadhammino 
 pakkhi gahetvāna viheṭhayanti 
 te heṭhayitvā  sakuṇaṃ janinda 
 te luddakammā pasavetvā pāpaṃ 
 teme janā luttasirā sayanti  
  
       pahuta  toyā anikhātakulā  
 nadi ayaṃ sandati supatitthā 
 ghammābhitantā manujā pivanti 
 pivatañca  tesaṃ bhusaṃ hoti pāni  
  
       bhayaṃ hi maṃ vindati suta disvā 
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 ime nu maccā kimakaṃsu pāpaṃ 
 pivatañca  tesaṃ bhusaṃ hoti pāni  
  
              
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ pāpa kammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       ye suddhadhaññaṃ palāpena  missaṃ 
 asuddhakammā kayino dadanti  
 ghammābhitantānaṃ pipāsitānaṃ 
 pivatañca tesaṃ bhusaṃ hoti pāni  
  
    aviheṭṭhayitvā  machasaṃ    luñcasirā  machasaṃ    viheṭhayitvā  machasaṃ    pahutta  machasaṃ    anigādhakulā  machasaṃ    pitañca  machasaṃ    palāsena  machasaṃ  
  
              
       usuhi sattihi ca tomarehi 
 dubhayāni passāni tudanti kandataṃ  
 bhayaṃ hi maṃ vindati suta disvā 
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi 
 ime nu maccā kimakaṃsu pāpaṃ 
 yeme janā sattihatā sayanti  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ pāpa kammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       ye jivalokasmiṃ asādhukammino  
 adinnamādāya karonti jivikaṃ  
 dhaññaṃ dhanaṃ rajataṃ jātarūpaṃ 
 ajeḷakaṃ cāpi pasuṃ mahīsaṃ  
 te luddakammā pasavetvā pāpaṃ 
 teme janā sattihatā sayanti  
  
              
       gīvāya baddhā kissa ime puneke 
 aññe vikattā  bilakatā puneke 
 bhayaṃ hi maṃ vindati suta disvā 
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 ime nu maccā kimakaṃsu pāpaṃ 
 yeme janā bilakatā sayantī  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ pāpa kammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       orabbhikā sukarikā ca macchikā 
 pasuṃ mahisañca ajeḷakañca 
 hanatvāna sunesu pasārayiṃsu 
 te luddakammā pasavetvā 
 teme janā bilakatā sayanti  
  
       rahado ayaṃ muttakarīsapuro 
 duggandharūpo asucī puti vāyati 
 khudā  paretā manujā adenti  
 bhayaṃ hi maṃ vindati suta disvā 
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 ime nu maccā kimakaṃsu pāpaṃ 
 yeme janā muttakarīsabhakkhā  
  
    mahisaṃ  machasaṃ    vikantā  machasaṃ    khuddā  machasaṃ 
    pivanti  aṭṭhakathā  
  
              
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ pāpa kammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
              
       ye keci me kāraṇikā virosakā 
 paresaṃ bhiṃsāya sadā niviṭṭhā 
 te luddakammā pasavetvā pāpaṃ 
 mittadaduno mīḷhamadenti bālā 
 rahado ayaṃ lohitapubbapuro 
 duggandharūpo asucī puti vāyati  
  
       ghammābhintā manujā pivanti 
 bhayaṃ hi maṃ vindati suta disvā  
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 ime nu maccā kimakaṃsu pāpaṃ 
 yeme janā lohitapubbabhakkhā  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ pāpa kammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       ye mātaraṃ vā pitaraṃ vā jivaloke 
 pārājikā arahante hananti  
 te luddakammā pasavetvā pāpaṃ 
 teme janā lohatapubbakkhā  
  
              
       jivhañca passa khalisena viddhaṃ 
 vihataṃ yathā saṅkusatena cammaṃ 
 phandanti macchāva thalamhi khittā 
 muñcanti kheḷaṃ rudamānā kimete  
  
       bhayaṃ hi maṃ vindati suta disvā  
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 ime nu maccā kimakaṃsu pāpaṃ 
 yeme janā vaṅkaghastā sayanti  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ pāpa kammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       ye keci yanthānagatā manussā 
 agghena agghaṃ kayaṃ hāpayanti  
 kūṭena kūṭaṃ dhanalobhahetu  
 channaṃ yathā vāricaraṃ vadhāya  
  
    kalaṃ hāpayanti  machasaṃ 
  
              
       na hi kūṭakārissa bhavanti tāṇā 
 sakehi kammehi purakkhatassa    
 te luddakammā pasavetvā pāpaṃ 
 te me janā vaṅkaghastā sayanti  
  
       nariyo  imā samparibhintagantā 
 paggayha kandanti bhuje dujacca  
 sammakkhitā lohitapubbalintā 
 gāvo yathā āghātane vikattā  
 tā bhumibhāgasmiṃ sadā nikhātā 
 khandhātivattanti sajotibhūtā  
  
              
       bhayaṃ hi maṃ vindati suta disvā  
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 ime nu maccā kimakaṃsu pāpaṃ 
 yā bhūmibhāgasmiṃ sadā nikhātā 
 khandhātivattanti sajotibhūtā  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ pāpa kammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       koliniyāyo  idha jivaloke 
 asuddhakammā asataṃ acāruṃ  
 tā dinnarūpā  pativippahāya  
 aññaṃ acāruṃ ratikhiḍḍahetu 
 tā jivalokasmiṃ ramāpiyitvā 
 khandhātivattanti sajotibhūtā  
  
              
       pāde gahetvā kissa ime puneke 
 avaṃsirā narake pātayanti  bhayaṃ hi maṃ vindati suta disvā  
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 ime nu maccā kimakaṃsu pāpaṃ 
 ye me janā avaṃsirā narake pātayanti  
  
    purakkhitassa  machasaṃ    nārino  machasaṃ    vikantā  machasaṃ 
    kolitthiyāyo  machasaṃ  syā    acaruṃ  machasaṃ    kittharūpā  machasaṃ 
  
              
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ pāpa kammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       ye jivalokasmiṃ asādhukammino 
 parassa dārāni atikkamanti  
 te tādisā uttamabhaṇḍathenā 
 te me janā avaṃsirā narake pātayanti  
  
       te vassapugāni bahuni tattha 
 niraye dukkhaṃ vedanaṃ vedayanti  
 nahi pāpakārissa bhavanti tāṇā 
 sakehi kammehi purakkhatassa 
 te luddakammā pasavetvā pāpaṃ  
 te me janā avaṃsirā narake pātayanti  
  
       uccāvacāme vividhā upakkamā 
 nirayesu dissanti sughorarūpā 
 bhayaṃ hi maṃ vindati suta disvā  
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 ime nu maccā kimakaṃsu pāpaṃ 
 yeme janā adhimattā dukkhā tibbā 
  
 khārā kaṭukā vedanā vedayanti  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ pāpa kammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
              
       ye jivalokasmiṃ supāpadiṭṭhino 
 vissāsakammāni karonti mohā 
 parañca diṭṭhisu samādapenti 
 te pāpādiṭṭhi pasavetvā  pāpaṃ 
 te me janā adhimattā dukkhā tibbā 
 kharā kaṭukā vedanā vedayanti  
  
       viditāni te mahārāja āvāsaṃ pāpakamminaṃ  
 ṭhānāni luddakammānaṃ dussilānañca yā gati 
 uyyāhidāni rājisi devarājassa santike  
 nirayakaṇḍaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ  
  
    pasavetvāna  machasaṃ 
               
              
       pañcathupaṃ dissatidaṃ vimānaṃ 
 mālā piḷandhā sayanassa majjhe  
 tatthacchati nāri mabhānubhāvā 
 uccāvacaṃ iddhiṃ vikubbamānā  
  
       vittī hi maṃ vindati suta disvā 
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 ayaṃ nu nārī kimakāsi sādhuṃ 
 yā modati saggapattā vimāne  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ puññakammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       yadi te sutā khiraṇi jivaloke 
 āmāya dāsī ahu brāhmaṇassa  
 sā pattakālaṃ atithiṃ viditvā 
 mātāva puttaṃ sakimābhinandi  
 saññamā saṃvibhāgā ca 
 sā vimānasmiṃ modati  
  
              
       daddallamānā ābhenti  vimānā satta nimmitā  
 tattha yakkho mahiddhiko sabbābharaṇabhūsito 
 samantā anupariyāti nārigaṇapurakkhato  
  
       vitti hi maṃ vindati suta disvā 
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 ayaṃ nu macco kimakāsi sādhuṃ 
 yo modati saggapatto vimāne  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ puññakammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       soṇaditto gahapati esa dānapati ahu  
 esa pabbajituddissa vihāre satta kārayi  
  
       sakkaccaṃ te upaṭṭhāsi bhikkhavo tattha vāsike  
 acchādanañca bhattañca senāsanapadipiyaṃ 
 adāsi ujubhutesu vippasannena cetasā  
  
       cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiṃ yāva pakkhassa aṭṭhamiṃ  
 pāṭihāriyapakkhañca aṭṭhaṅgasusamāgataṃ  
  
    āhanti  machasaṃ    aṭṭhaṅgaṃ susamāhitaṃ  machasaṃ  syā 
  
               
       uposathaṃ ca upacasi sadā sīlesu saṃvuto  
 saṃyamo saṃvibhāgo ca so vimānasmiṃ modati  
  
              
       pabhāsati idaṃ vyambhaṃ eḷikāsu sunimmitaṃ  
 nārivaragaṇākiṇṇaṃ kuṭāgāravarocitaṃ 
 upetaṃ annapānehi naccagītehi cubhayaṃ  
  
       vitti hi maṃ vindati suta disvā 
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 imā nu nāriyo kimakaṃsu sādhuṃ  
 yo modare saggapattā vimāne  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ paññakammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       yā kāci nāriyo idha jivaloke 
 sīlavatiyo  upāsikā  
 dāne ratā niccapasannacittā 
 sacce ṭhitā uposathe appamattā  
 saṃyamā saṃvibhāgā ca tā vimānasmiṃ modare  
  
              
       pabhāsati idaṃ vyambhaṃ veḷuriyāsu nimmitaṃ  
 upetaṃ bhūmibhāgehi vibhattaṃ bhāgaso mitaṃ  
  
       āḷambarā mutiṅgā ca naccagitā suvāditā  
 dibbā saddā niccaranti savaṇeyyā manoramā  
  
       nāhaṃ evaṃ gataṃ jātu evaṃ suruciraṃ pure  
 saddaṃ samabhijānāmi diṭṭhaṃ vā yadi vā sutaṃ  
  
       vitti hi maṃ vindati suta disvā 
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 ime nu maccā kimakaṃsu pāpaṃ 
 ye modare saggapattā vimāne  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ puññakammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       ye keci maccā idha jivaloke sīlavanto upāsakā  
 ārāme udapāne ca papā saṅkamanāni ca  
 arahante sītibhūte  sakkaccaṃ paṭipādayuṃ  
  
    silavaniyo  machasaṃ    bhūtesu  machasaṃ 
  
               
       civaraṃ piṇḍapātañca paccayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ  
 adaṃsu ujubhutesu vippasantena cetasā  
  
       cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiṃ yāva pakkhassa aṭṭhamiṃ  
 pāṭihāriyapakkhañca aṭṭhaṅgasusamāgataṃ    
  
       uposathaṃ upavasuṃ sadā sīlesu saṃvutā  
 saññāmā saṃvihāgā ca te vimānasmiṃ modare  
  
              
       pabhāsati idaṃ vyambhaṃ eḷikāsu sunimmitaṃ  
 nārivaragaṇākiṇṇaṃ kuṭāgāravirocitaṃ  
  
       upetaṃ antapānehi naccagitehi cubhayaṃ  
 najjo ca anupariyāti nānāpupphadumāyutā  
  
       vitti hi maṃ vindati suta disvā 
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 ime nu maccā kimakāsi sādhuṃ 
 yo modati saggapatto vimāne  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ puññakammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       kimbilāyaṃ gahapati esa dānapatī ahu  
 ārāme udapāne ca papā saṅkamanāni ca  
  
       arahante sītibhūte sakkaccaṃ paṭipādayi  
 civaraṃ piṇḍapātañca pacacayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ  
 adāsi ujubhutesu vippasantena cetasā  
  
       cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiṃ yāva pakkhassa aṭṭhamiṃ  
 pāṭihāriyapakkhañca aṭṭhaṅgasusamāgataṃ  
  
       upesathaṃ upavasi sadā sīlesu saṃvuto  
 saññamo saṃvibhāgo ca so vimānasmaṃ modati  
       pabhāsati idaṃ vyambhaṃ eḷikāsu sunimmitaṃ  
 nārivaragaṇākiṇṇaṃ kūṭāgāravarocitaṃ  
  
              
       upetaṃ annapānehi naccagītehi cubhayaṃ  
 najjo ca anupariyāti nānāpupphadumāyutā  
  
    susamāhitaṃ  machasaṃ    akkhāsi  machaṣaṃ 
  
               
       rājāyanatā kapitthā ambā sālā ca jambuyo  
 tindukā  ca piyālā ca dumā niccaphalā bahu  
  
       vitti hi maṃ vindati suta disvā 
 pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 ayaṃ nu maccā kimakāsi sādhuṃ 
 yo modati saggapatto vimāne  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ puññakammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       mithilāyaṃ gahapati esa dānapatī ahu  
 ārāme udapāne ca papā saṅkamanāni ca  
 arahante sītibhūte  sakkaccaṃ paṭipādayi  
       civaraṃ piṇḍapātañca pacacayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ  
 adāsi ujubhutesu vippasantena cetasā  
  
       cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiṃ yāva pakkhassa aṭṭhamiṃ  
 pāṭihāriyapakkhañca aṭṭhaṅgasusamāgataṃ    
  
       upesathaṃ upavasi sadā sīlesu saṃvuto  
 saññamo saṃvibhāgo ca so vimānasmaṃ modati  
       pabhāsati idaṃ vyambhaṃ ḷuriyosu nimmitaṃ  
 upetaṃ bhūmibhāgehi vibhattaṃ bhagāso mitaṃ  
  
       āḷambarā mutiṅgā ca nāccagītā suvāditā  
 dibbā  saddā niccharanti savaṇeyyā manoramā  
  
       nāhaṃ evaṃ gataṃ jātu  evaṃ suruciraṃ  pure  
 saddaṃ samabhijānāmi diṭaṭhaṃ vā yadi vā sutaṃ  
  
              
       vitati hi maṃ vindati disvā pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 ayaṃ nu macco kimakāsi sādhuṃ 
 yo modati saggapatto vimāne  
  
    kiṇḍukā ca machasaṃ    sitibhutesu  machasaṃ    susamāhitaṃ  machasaṃ 
    dibya  machasaṃ    jātaṃ  machasaṃ    suruciyaṃ  machasaṃ 
  
               
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ puññakammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       bāraṇasiyaṃ gahapati esa dānapatī ahu  
 ārāme udapāne ca papā saṅkamanāni ca  
 arahante sītibhū   sakkaccaṃ paṭipādayi  
       civaraṃ piṇḍapātañca pacacayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ  
 adāsi ujubhutesu vippasantena cetasā  
  
       cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiṃ yāva pakkhassa aṭṭhamiṃ  
 pāṭihāriyapakkhañca aṭṭhaṅgasusamāgataṃ  
  
       upesathaṃ upavasi sadā sīlesu saṃvuto  
 saññamo saṃvibhāgo ca so vimānasmaṃ modati  
       yathā udayamādicce hoti lohitako mahā  
 tathupamaṃ idaṃ vyambhaṃ jātarūpassa nimmitaṃ  
  
       vitati hi maṃ vindati disvā pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 ayaṃ nu macco kimakāsi sādhuṃ 
 yo modati saggapatto vimāne  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ puññakammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       sāvatthiyaṃ gahapati esa dānapatī ahu  
 ārāme udapāne ca papā saṅkamanāni ca  
 arahante sītibhūte sakkaccaṃ paṭipādayi  
       civaraṃ piṇḍapātañca pacacayaṃ sayanāsanaṃ  
 adāsi ujubhutesu vippasantena cetasā  
  
       cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiṃ yāva pakkhassa aṭṭhamiṃ  
 pāṭihāriyapakkhañca aṭṭhaṅgasusamāgataṃ    
  
       upesathaṃ upavasi sadā sīlesu saṃvuto  
 saṃyamo saṃvibhāgo ca so vimānasmaṃ modati  
              
       vehāsayāme bahukā jātarūpassa nimmitā  
 daddallamānā ābhenti vijjuvabbhaghanantare  
  
    sitibhutesu  machasaṃ    susamāhitaṃ  machasaṃ 
  
               
       vitati hi maṃ vindati disvā pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 ime nu macco kimakaṃsu sādhuṃ 
 yo modare saggapatto vimāne  
  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ puññakammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       saddhāya suniviṭṭhāya saddhamme suppavedite  
 akaṃsu santhuvacanaṃ sammāsambuddhasāsanaṃ    
 tesaṃ etāni ṭhānāni yāni tvaṃ rāja passasi  
  
       viditāni te mahārāja āvāsaṃ pāpakamminaṃ  
 atho kalyāṇakammānaṃ ṭhānāni vidatāni te 
 uyyābhidāni rājisi devarājassa santike  
 vimānakaṇḍaṃ niṭṭhitaṃ  
  
              
       sahassayuttaṃ hayavāhiṃ dibbaṃ yānaṃ adhiṭṭhito  
 yāyamāno mahārājā addā sīdantare nage 
 disvānāmantiyī sutaṃ ime ke nāma pabbatā  
  
       sudassano karavīko īsadharo yugandharo  
 nemindharo vinatako assakaṇṇo giribrahā  
  
       ete sidantare nagā anupubbasamuggatā  
 mahārājānamāvāsā yāni tvaṃ rāja passasi  
  
       anekarūpaṃ ruviraṃ nānāvitraṃ pakāsati  
 ākiṇaṇaṃ indisehi vyaggheheva surakkhitaṃ  
  
              
       vitati hi maṃ vindati disvā pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 imaṃ nu dvāraṃ kimbhiññamāhu 
  mānoramaṃ dissati duratova     
  
    sāsane  machasaṃ    purakkhitā  machasaṃ     ayaṃ pāṭho syāmapotthake yeva dissati    
  
               
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ puññakammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
       cintakūṭoti yaṃ āhu devarājapavesanaṃ  
 sudassanassa girino dvāraṃ hetaṃ pakāsati  
  
       anekarūpaṃ ruciraṃ nānācitraṃ pakāsati  
 ākiṇṇaṃ indisadisehi vyaggheve surakkhitaṃ  
 pavisetena rājisi arajaṃ bhumimakkama  
  
       sahassayuttaṃ hayavāhiṃ dibbaṃ yānaṃ adhiṭṭhito  
 yāyamāno mahārājā addā devasabhaṃ idaṃ  
  
       yathā sarade ākāso nīlova patidissati  
 tathupamaṃ idaṃ vyambhaṃ veḷuriyāsu nimmitaṃ  
  
       vitati hi maṃ vindati disvā pucchāmi taṃ mātali devasārathi  
 imaṃ nu vyambhaṃ kimabhiññamāhu  
       tassa puṭṭho viyākāsi mātali devasārathi  
 vipākaṃ puññakammānaṃ jānaṃ akkhāsajānato 
  
              
       sudhammaṃ iti yamāhu passesā dissate sabhā  
 veḷuriyā rucirā citrā dhārayanti sunimmitā  
  
       aṭṭhaṃsā sukatā thambhā sabbe veḷuriyāmayā  
 yattha devā tāvatiṃsā sabbe indapurohitā  
  
       atthaṃ devamanussānaṃ cintayantā samacchare  
 pavisetena rājisi devānaṃ anumodanaṃ  
  
       taṃ devā paṭinandiṃsu disvā rājānamāgataṃ  
 svāgataṃ te mahārāja atho te adurāgataṃ  
  
       nisidadāni rājisi devarājassa santike  
 sakkopi paṭinandittha vedehaṃ mithilaggahaṃ  
  
               
       nimantayi ca  kāmehi āsanena ca vāsavo  sādhu khosi anuppatto āvāsaṃ vasavantinaṃ  
  
       vasa devesu rājisi sabbakāmasamiddhisu  
 tāvatiṃsesu devesu bhuñja kāme amānuse  
  
       yathā yācitakaṃ yānaṃ yathā yācitakaṃ dhanaṃ  
 evaṃ sammapadamevetaṃ yaṃ parato dānapaccayā  
  
              
       nacāhametaṃ icchāmi yaṃ parato dānapaccayā  
 sayaṃ katāni puññāni taṃ me āveṇiyaṃ dhanaṃ  
  
       sohaṃ gantvā samussesu kāhāmi kusalaṃ bahuṃ  
 dānena samacariyāya saṃyamena damena ca 
 yaṃ katvā sukhito hoti na ca pacchānutappati  
  
       bahupakāro no bhavaṃ mātalī devasārathi  
 yo me kalyāṇakammānaṃ pāpāni  paṭidassayi  
  
              
       idaṃ vatvā nimirājā vedeho mithilaggabho  
 puthuyaññaṃ yajitvāna saññamaṃ ajjhupāgamīti  
 nimijātakaṃ catutthaṃ  
  
    nimantayittha  machasaṃ    pāpānaṃ pacidassayi  machasaṃ 
  
               
    khaṇḍahālajātakaṃ  
              
       rājāsi luddakammo  ekarājāti pupphavatiyā    
 so pucchi brahmabandhuṃ khaṇḍahālaṃ purohitaṃ muḷhaṃ  
  
       saggānamaggamācikkha tvaṃsi brāhmaṇa dhammavinayakusalo  
 yathā ito vajanti sugatiṃ narā puññāni katvāna  
  
       atidānaṃ daditvāna  avajjhe deva ghātetvā  
 evaṃ vajanti sugatiṃ narā puññāni katvāna  
  
       kiṃ pana taṃ  atidānaṃ ke ca avajjhā imasmiṃ lokasmiṃ  
 etañca kho no akkhāhi yajissāma dadāma dānāni  
  
              
       puttehi deva yajitabbaṃ mahesīhi negamehi ca usabhehi  
 ājāniyehi catūhi sabbacatukkena deva yajitabbaṃ  
  
       taṃ sutvā antepure kumārā ca mahesiyo ca baññantu  
 eko ahosi nigghoso bhesmā  accuggato saddo  
  
              
       gacchatha vadetha kumāre vandaṃ suriyaṃ ca bhaddasenañca  
 surañca vāmagontaṃ pasurā  kira hotha yaññatthāya  
  
       kumāriyopi vadetha upaseniṃ  kokilañca muditañca  
 nandañcāpi kumāriṃ pasurā kira bhotha yaññatthāya  
  
       vijayampi mayhaṃ mahesiṃ erāvatiṃ kesinaṃ sunandañca  
 lakkhaṇavarūpapannā pasurā kira hotha yaññatthāya  
  
              
  
       gahapatayopi vadetha puṇaṇamukhaṃ bhaddiyaṃ sigālañca  
 vaḍḍhañcāpi gahapatiṃ pasurā kira hotha yaññatthāya  
  
    luddakapposi  machasaṃ    pupphavatiyāyaṃ  machasaṃ  syā vi 
    dadatvāna  machasaṃ    panetaṃ  machasaṃ  syā vi  
    bhismā  machasaṃ    pavurā  machasaṃ    upasenaṃ  machasaṃ 
  
               
       te tattha gahapatayo avociṃsu samāgatā puttadāra parikiṇaṇā  
 sabbasikhino deva karohi athavā no dāse sāvehi  
  
       abhayaṅkarampi me hatthiṃ nālāgiraṃ accutaṃ varuṇadantaṃ  
 anetha kho ne khippaṃ yaññatthāya bhavissanti  
  
       assaratanampi kesiṃ surāmukhaṃ puṇaṇakaṃ vinatakañca  
 ānetha kho ne khippa yaññatthāya bhavissanti  
  
              
       usabhampi yuthapatiṃ anojaṃ nisabhaṃ gavampatiṃ 
 samupākarontu sabbaṃ yajisasāma dadāma dānāni  
  
       sabbaṃ paṭiyādetha yaññaṃ pana uggatambhi suriyambhi  
 āṇāpetha ca kumāre  abhiramantu imaṃ rattiṃ  
       sabbaṃ upaṭṭhāpetha yaññaṃ pana uggatambhi suriyambhi  
 vadethadāni kumāre ajja vo pacchimā rattiṃ  
       taṃ taṃ mātā avacā rodanti āgatā  vimānato  
 yañño kira te putta bhavissati catūhi puttehi  
  
       sabbepi mayhaṃ puttā cattā candāsmiṃ haññamānasmiṃ  
 puttehi yaññaṃ yajitvāna sugatiṃ saggaṃ gamissāmi  
  
       mā  putta sadadahesi sugati kira hoti puttayaññena  
 nirayāneso maggo neso maggo hi saggānaṃ  
  
              
       dānāni dehi koṇḍañña ahiṃsā sabbabhūtabhavyānaṃ  
 esamaggo sugatiyā na ca maggo puttayaññena  
  
       ācariyānaṃ vacanā ghātessaṃ candañca suriyañca  
 puttehi yajitvāna ducacajehi sugatiṃ saggaṃ gamissāmi  
  
    aṇāpethacandakumāre  machasaṃ    āgantvā  machasaṃ    mā taṃ  machasaṃ syā  
  
               
       taṃ taṃ pitāpi avacā vasavatti orasaṃ sakaṃ puttaṃ  
 yañño kira te putta bhavissati catūhi puttehi  
  
       sabbepi mayhaṃ puttā cattā candāsmiṃ haññamānasmiṃ  
 puttehi yaññaṃ yajitvāna sugatiṃ saggaṃ gamissāmi  
  
       mā putta sadadahesi sugatiṃ kira hoti puttayaññena  
 nirayāneso maggo neso maggo hi saggānaṃ
