 puttaparivuto tuvaṃ raṭṭhaṃ janapadañca pālehi  
       mā no deva avadhi dāse no dehi khaṇḍahālassa  
 api nigaḷa  bandhakāpi hatthi asse ca pāpema  
  
       mā no deva avadhi dāse no dehi khaṇḍahālassa  
 api nigaḷabandhakāpi hatthicchakaṇāni ujjhema  
  
       mā no deva avadhi dāse no dehi khaṇḍahālassa  
 api nigaḷabandhakāpi assacchakaṇāni ujjhema  
  
       mā no deva avadhi dāse no dehi khaṇḍahālassa  
 yassa honti tava kāmā api raṭṭhā pabbajitā bhikkhācariyaṃ carissāma  
  
       dukkhaṃ kho me janayatha vilapantā jīvitassa kāmā hi  
 muñcathadāni kumāre alampi me hotu puttayaññena  
  
    niggaḷa  machasaṃ 
  
               
              
       pubbeva khosi me vutto dukkaraṃ durabhisambhavaṃ cetaṃ  
 atha no upakkhaṭassa yaññassa kasmā karosi vikkhepaṃ  
  
       sabbe vajanti sugatiṃ  ye yajanti yepi ceva yājenti  
 yecāpi anumodanti yajantānaṃ edisaṃ mahāyaññaṃ  
  
       atha kissa ca no pubbe sotthānaṃ brāhamaṇo avācesi    
 atha no akāraṇasmā yaññatthāya deva ghātesi  
  
       pubbeva no daharake samāne na hanesi na ghātayesi  
 daharambhā yobbanaṃ pantā adusakā tāta haññāma  
  
       hatthigate assagate sannaddhe passa no mahārāja  
 yuddheva yujjhamāne nahi mādisā surā honti yaññatthāya  
  
       paccante vāpi kupite aṭavisu vā mādise niyojenti  
 atha no akāraṇasmā abhumiṃ tāta haññāma  
  
       yāpi hi tā sakuṇiyo vasanti tiṇagharāni katvāna  
 tāsampi piyā puttā atha no tvaṃ dve ghātesi  
  
              
       mā tassa  saddahesi na maṃ khaṇḍahālo ghātaye  
 mamaṃ hi so ghātetvā anantaraṃ tampi deva ghāteyya  
  
       gāmavaraṃ nigamavaraṃ dadanti bhogaṃ pissa mahārāja  
 atha aggapiṇḍikāpi kule kulehete bhuñjanti  
  
       tesampi tādisānaṃ icchanti dubbhituṃ mahārāja  
 yebhuyyena ete akataññano brāhmaṇā deva  
  
       mā no dve avadhi dāse no dehi khaṇḍahālassa  
 api nigaḷabandhakāpi  hatthi asse ca pālema  
  
    suggati  machasaṃ    athavācesi  machasaṃ    khavassa  machasaṃ  syā 
    niggaḷa  machasaṃ  syā

 api nigaḷabandhakāpi hatthicchakaṇāni ujjhema

 api nigaḷabandhakāpi assacchakaṇāni ujjhema

 yassa honti tava kāmā api raṭṭhā pabbajitā carissāma

 atha no upakkhaṭassa yaññassa kasmā karosi vikkhepaṃ  
  
       sabbe vajanti sugatiṃ ye yajanti yepi ceva yājenti  
 ye cāpi anumodanti yajantānaṃ edisaṃ mahāyaññaṃ  
  
       yadi kira yajitvā puttehi devalokaṃ ito cutā yannī  
 brāhmaṇo tāva yajatu pacchāpi yajasi tuvaṃ rāja  
       yadi kira yajitvā puttehi devalokaṃ ito cutā yannī  
 eso ca khaṇḍahālo yajatu sakehi puttehi  
  
       evaṃ jānaṃ  vo khaṇḍahālo kiṃ puttake na ghātesi  
 sabbañca ñātijanaṃ attānañca na ghātesi  
  
       sabbe vajanti nirayaṃ ye yajanti yepi ceva yājenti  
 ye cāpi anumodanti yajantānaṃ edisaṃ mahāyaññaṃ  
  
              
       kathaññaca kira puttakāmāyo gahapatayo gharaṇiyo ca  
 nagarambhi na uparavanti rājānaṃ mā ghātayi orasaṃ puttaṃ  
  
    evaṃ jānanto  machasaṃ 
  
               
       kathaññaca kira puttakāmāyo gahapatayo gharaṇiyo ca  
 nagarambhi na uparavanti rājānaṃ mā ghātayi atrajaṃ puttaṃ  
  
       raññombhi atthakāmo hito ca sabbadā janapadassa  
 na koci assa paṭighaṃ mayā janapado na pavedeti  
  
       gacchatha vo gharaṇiyo tātañca vadetha khaṇḍahālañca  
 mā ghātetha kumāre adusake sihasaṅkase  
  
       gacchatha vo gharaṇiyo tātañca vadetha khaṇḍahālañca  
 mā ghātetha kumāre apekkhite sabbalokassa 
  
       yannunāhaṃ jāyeyyaṃ rathakārakule vā pukkusakule vā  
 veṇesu vā jāyeyyaṃ nahajja maṃ rājā yaññatthāya ghāteyya  
  
       sabbā sīmantiniyo gacchatha ayyassa khaṇḍabhālassa  
 pādesu nipatatha aparādhāhaṃ na passāmi  
              
       sabbā sīmantiniyo gacchatha ayyassa khaṇḍabhālassa  
 pādesu nipatatha kiṃ te bhante mayaṃ asusema  
  
       kapaṇaṃ vilapati selā disvā bhātaro upanītatte  
 yañño kira me ukkhipito tātena saggakāmena  
  
       āvatti ca parivatti ca vāsulo sammukhā rañño  
 mā no pitaraṃ avadhi daharambhā ayobbanaṃ pattā

 dukkhaṃ kho me janayasi vilapanto antarapurasmiṃ 
 muñcatha dāni kumāre alampi me hotu puttayaññena

 kese parikiritvāna rodantiyo maggamanuyanti

 nīyanti candasuriyā yaññatthāya ekarājassa

 tyajja candasuriyā ubhova pattikā yanti

 yajatettha ekarājā sammuḷho sabbacatukkena

 tedāni ayyaputtā cattāro vadhāya nintitā

       kathaṃ nāma sāmasamasundarehi candanamarakatagattehi

 tathā hessati pupphavatiyā yiṭṭhesu candasuriyesu  
  
              
       ummattikā bhavissāmi bhūnabhatā paṃsutā ca parikiṇaṇā  
 sace candavaraṃ hanti pāṇā me deva nirujjhanti  
  
       ummattikā bhavissāmi bhūnabhatā paṃsutā ca parikiṇaṇā  
 sace suriyavaraṃ hanti pāṇā me deva nirujjhanti

 ghaṭaṭiyā  oparakkhi ca pokkharakkhi ca nāyikā  
 candasuriyesu naccantiyo samo tāsaṃ na vijjati  
  
       imaṃ mayhaṃ hadayasokaṃ paṭimuccatu khaṇḍahāla tava mātā 
 yo mayhaṃ hadayasoko candasamiṃ vadhāya nintite  
  
              
       imaṃ mayhaṃ hadayasokaṃ paṭimuccatu khaṇḍahāla tava mātā 
 yo mayhaṃ hadayasoko suriyasmiṃ vadhāya nintite

       divyaṃ  upayācanti puttatthikā daḷiddāpi  nāriyo  
 paṭibhāṇānipa hitvā putte nahi labhanti ekaccā  
  
    dibba  machasaṃ    dasiddā  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
       assāsakāni  karonti puttā no jāyantu tato paputtā  
 atha no akāraṇasmā yaññatthāya deva ghātesi  
  
       upayācitakena puttaṃ labhanti mā tāta no aghātasi  
 mā kicchā laddhakehi puttehi yajittho imaṃ yaññaṃ  
  
       upayācitakena puttaṃ labhanti mā tāta no aghātasi  
 mā kapaṇaladdhakehi puttehi ammāya no vippavāsehi  
  
       bahudukkhaposiyā candaṃ amma tuvaṃ jiyyase puttaṃ  
 vandāmi kho te pāde labhataṃ tāto paralokaṃ  
  
       handa ca maṃ upaguha pāde te amma vandituṃ dehi  
 gacchāmidāni pavāsaṃ yaññatthāya ekarājassa  
  
       handa ca maṃ upaguha pāde te amma vandituṃ dehi  
 gacchāmidāni pavāsaṃ mātu katvā bhadayasokaṃ  
  
       handa ca maṃ upaguha pāde te amma vandituṃ dehi  
 gacchāmidāni pavāsaṃ janassa bhadayasokaṃ  
  
              
       handa ca padumapantānaṃ moḷiṃ bandhassu gotamiputta  
 campakadalavitimissāyo  esā te porāṇiyā pakati  
  
       handa ca vilepanante pacchamakaṃ candanaṃ vipimpassu  
 yehi ca suvilitto sobhasi rājaparisāya  
  
       handa mudukāni vatthāni paccimakaṃ kāsikaṃ vāsehi  
 yohi ca sunivattho sobhasi rājaparisāya  
  
    asisikāni  machasaṃ    ghātesi  machasaṃ    campakadalamissāyo  syā campakadalehi  machasaṃ    parisāya  machasaṃ 
  
               
       muttāmaṇikanakavibhūtāni gaṇhassu hatthābharaṇāni  
 yehi ca hatthābharaṇehi sohasi rājaparisāya  
  
       nahanunāyaṃ raṭṭhapālo bhumipati janapadassa dāyado  
 lokissaro mahantā puttesu sinehaṃ janayati  
  
       mayhaṃ piyā puttā attāpi  piyo tumbhe ca bhariyāyo  
 saggañca patthayāno tenāhaṃ ghātayissāmi  
  
              
       maṃ  paṭhamaṃ ghātehi mā me hadayaṃ dukkhaṃ aphālesi  
 alaṅkato sundarako putto tava deva sukhumālo  
  
       handayya maṃ hanassu salokā candiyena hessāmi  
 puññaṃ karassu vipulaṃ vicarāma ubhova paraloke  
  
       mā tvaṃ cande rucci bahukā tatava devarā visālakkhi  
 te taṃ ramayissanti yiṭṭhasmiṃ gotamiputte  
  
       evaṃ vutte candā annānaṃ hanti hatthatalakehī  
 alavatthu  jivitena pāyāmi  visaṃ marissāmi  
       nahanunimassa rañño mitatāmaccā ca vijjare suhadā  
 ye na vadanti rājānaṃ mā ghātayi orase putte  
  
       nahanunimassa rañño ñātimittā ca vijjare suhadā  
 ye na vadanti rājānaṃ mā ghātayi atraje putte  
  
              
       ime tepi mayhaṃ puttā guṇino kāyuradhārino rāja  
 tehipi yajassu yaññaṃ atha muñcatu gotamīputte  
  
       bilasatampi maṃ katvā yajassu sattadhā mahārāja  
 mā jeṭṭaputtamavadhi adūsakaṃ sihasaṅkāsaṃ  
  
    athopi  machasaṃ    ma  machasaṃ    alamettha  machasaṃ 
    piyāmi visaṃ  machasaṃ 
  
               
       bilasatampi maṃ katvā yajassu sattadhā mahārāja  
 mā jeṭṭaputtamavadhi apekkhitaṃ sabbalokassa 
  
       bahukā tava dinnā ābharaṇā uccāvacā subaṇitambhi  
 muttāmaṇiveḷuriyā idaṃ te pacchimakaṃ dānaṃ  
  
       yesaṃ pubbe khandhessu phullā mālāguṇā vivantiṃsu  
 tesajjapitanisito nentiṃso vivattisasti khandhesu  
  
       yesaṃ pubbe khandhessu citrā mālāguṇā vivantiṃsu  
 tesajja pita nisito  nentiṃso vivattisasti khandhesu  
  
       acirā  vata nettasā vivaittissati rājaputtānaṃ khandhesu  
 atha mama hadaṃ na phalati tāva daḷhabandhanañca me āsi  
  
              
       kāsikasuvivatthadharā kuṇḍalino agaḷucandanavilittā    
 niyyātha candasuriyā yaññatthāya ekarājassa

 niyyātha candasuriyā mātu katvā hadayasokaṃ

 niyyātha candasuriyā janassa katvā hadayasokaṃ    
  
       maṃsarasabhojino nabhāpakasunabhātā kuṇḍalino agaḷucandanacilittā  
 niyyātha candasuriyā yaññatthāya ekarājassa  
  
       maṃsarasabhojino nabhāpakasunabhātā kuṇḍalino agaḷunavilittā  
 niyyātha candasuriyā mātu katvāhadayasokaṃ 
  
    tesajjapisunisito  machasaṃ    aciraṃ  machasaṃ    aggalu  machasaṃ akalu  vi 
  
               
       maṃsarasabhojino nabhāpakasunabhātā kuṇḍalino agaḷuvandanavilittā  
 niyyātha candasuriyā janassa katvā dayasokaṃ  
  
       sabbasmiṃ upakkhaṭasmiṃ nisīdite candiyasmiṃ  yaññatthāya  
 pañcālarājadhitā pañajalikā sabbaparisamanupariyāyi  
  
       yena saccena khaṇaḍhālo pāpakammaṃ karoti dumemadho  
 etena saccavajjena samaṅgini sāmikena homi  
  
       yedhatthi amanussā yāni ca yakkhabhūtabhavyāni  
 karontu me veyyāvaṭikaṃ samaṅgini sāmikena homi  
  
              
       yā devatā idhāgatā yāni ca yakkhabhūtabhavyāni  
 saraṇesiniṃ anāthaṃ tāyatha maṃ yācāmahaṃ patimāhaṃ ajiyyaṃ  
  
       taṃ sutvā amanusesā ayokuṭaṃ paribbhametvāna  
 bhayamassa ranayanto rājānaṃ idamavoca  
  
       khujjhassa kho rājakali mātāhaṃ matthakaṃ nitāḷemi  
 mā jeṭṭhaputtamavadhī adūsakaṃ sīhasaṅkāsaṃ  
  
       ko te diṭṭhā rājakalī puttabhariyāyo haññamānā    
 soṭṭhi va gahapatayo adusakā saggakāmā hi  
  
       taṃ sutvā khaṇḍahālo rājā va abbhutamidaṃ disvāna  
 sabbesaṃ bandhanāni movecasuṃ yathā taṃ apāpānaṃ  
  
       sabbesu vippamuttesu ye ca tattha samāgatā tadā āsuṃ  
 sabbe ekekaleḍḍukamadaṃsu esa vadho khaṇaḍahālassa  
  
    candakambhi  machasaṃ    ajayaṃ  machasaṃ    haññamānāyo  machasaṃ  syā 
    anupaghātaṃ  machasaṃ  syā 
  
               
              
       sabbe patiṃsu  nirayaṃ yathā taṃ pāpakaṃ karitvāna  
 nahi pāpakammaṃ katvā labbā sugatiṃ ito gantuṃ  
  
       sabbesu vippamuttesu ye ca tattha samāgatā tadā āsuṃ  
 candaṃ abhisiñciṃsu samāgatā rājaparisā ca  
       sabbesu vippamuttesu ye ca tattha samāgatā tadā āsuṃ  
 candaṃ abhisiñciṃsu samāgatā rājakaññāyo  
  
       sabbesu vippamuttesu ye ca tattha samāgatā tadā āsuṃ  
 candaṃ abhisiñciṃsu samāgatā devaparisā ca  
       sabbesu vippamuttesu ye ca tattha samāgatā tadā āsuṃ  
 candaṃ abhisiñciṃsu samāgatā devakaññāyo 
       sabbesu vippamuttesu ye ca tattha samāgatā tadā āsuṃ  
 celukkhepamakāruṃ samāgatā rājaparisā ca  
       sabbesu vippamuttesu ye ca tattha samāgatā tadā āsuṃ  
 celukkhepamakāruṃ samāgatā rājakaññāyo  
  
       sabbesu vippamuttesu ye ca tattha samāgatā tadā āsuṃ  
 velukkhepamakāruṃ samāgatā devaparisā ca  
  
       sabbesu vippamuttesu ye ca tattha samāgatā tadā āsuṃ  
 velukkhepamakāruṃ samāgatā devakaññāyo 
       sabbesu vippamuttesu bahu ānandano ahu vaṃso  
 nandippavesi nagaraṃ bandhanā mokkho aghositthāti  
 khaṇḍahālajātakaṃ pañcamaṃ  
  
    sabbepaviṭṭhā patitvā  machasaṃ 
  
               
    bhuridattajātakaṃ 
              
       yaṃ kiñci ratanaṃ atthi dhataraṭṭhanivesane  
 sabbāni te upāyantu  dhitaraṃ dehi rājino  
  
       na no vivāho nāgehi katapubbo kudācanaṃ  
 taṃ vivāhaṃ asaṃyuttaṃ kathaṃ ambhe karomase  
  
              
       jīvitaṃ nūna te cantaṃ raṭṭhaṃ vā manujādhipa  
 na hi nāge kupitambhi ciraṃ jivanti tādisā  
  
       yo tvaṃ deva manussesu  iddhimantaṃ aniddhimā  
 varuṇassa niyaṃ puttaṃ yāmunaṃ atimaññasi  
  
       nātimaññāmi rājānaṃ dhataraṭṭhaṃ yasassina  
 dhataraṭṭho hi nāgānaṃ bahuntamapi issaro  
  
       ahi mahānubhāvopi na me dhitaramāraho  
 khattiyo ca videhānaṃ abhijātā samuddajā  
  
              
       kambalassatarā uṭṭhentu sabbe nāge nivedaya  
 bārāṇasaṃ pavajjantu mā ca kiñci viheṭhayuṃ  
  
       nivesanesu sobbesu rathiyā caccaresu ca  
 rukkhaggesu ca labbantu  vitatā toraṇesu ca  
  
       ahampi sabbasetena mahatā sumahaṃ puraṃ  
 parikkhipissaṃ bhogehi kāsīnaṃ janayaṃ  bhayaṃ  
  
              
       tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā uragā nekavaṇṇino  
 bārāṇasaṃ pavajjiṃsu na ca kiñciviheṭhayuṃ  
  
       nivesanesu sobbhesu rathiyā cacacaresu ca  
 rukkhaggesu ca lambiṃsu vatatā toraṇesu ca  
  
    upayantu  machasaṃ  syā    manussosi  machasaṃ  syā 
    lambanti  machasaṃ    janataṃ  machasaṃ    vihedhayuṃ  machasaṃ 
  
               
       te  disvāna lambante puthu kandiṃsu nāriyo  
 nage soṇḍikate disvā passasante muhuṃ muhuṃ  
  
       bārāṇasī pavyadhitā  āturā samapajjatha  
 bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ dhītaraṃ dehi rājino  
 nagarakhaṇḍo  
  
              
       pupphābhihārassa vanassa majjhe 
 ko lohitakkho vihatattaraṃso    
 kā kambukāyuradharā suvatthā 
 tiṭṭhanti nāriyo dasa vandamānā  
  
       ko tvaṃ brahābāhu vanassa mājjha 
 virocasi ghatasittova aggi  
 mahesakkho aññatarosi yakkho 
 udāhu nāgosi mahānubhāvo  
  
       nāgohamasmiṃ iddhimā tejasī duratikkamo  
 iseyyaṃ tejasā kuddho phītaṃ janapadaṃ api  
  
       samuddajā hi me mātā dhataraṭṭho ca me pitā  
 sudassanakaniṭṭhosmi bhuridattoti maṃ vidu  
  
              
       yaṃ gambhiraṃ sadāvaṭṭaṃ rahadaṃ bhesmaṃ  avekkhasi  
 esa divyo mamāvāso anekasataporiso  
  
       mayurakoñcābhirudaṃ nīlodaṃ vanamajjhato  
 yamunaṃ pavisa māhito khemaṃ vattavataṃ sivaṃ  
  
       tattha patto sānucaro sahaputtena brāhmaṇa  pujito mayhaṃ kamehi brāhmaṇa vacchasi  
  
              
       samā samantā parito bahuta  tagarā mahī  
 indagopakasañachantā sobhatī haritunnamā  
  
    citesu  machasaṃ    sabyādhitā  machasaṃ    vitatanataraṃso  machasaṃ 
    tā  machasaṃ    bhismaṃ  machasaṃ    vecchasi  machasaṃ    bahukātaggarā  machasaṃ  
  
               
       rammā vanacetyāni rammā  haṃsupakujitā  
 opupphadamā tiṭṭhanti pokkharañño sunimmitā  
  
       aṭṭhaṃsā sukatatthambhā sabbe veḷuriyāmayā  
 sahassathambhā pāsādā kaññāhi jotare  
  
              
       vimānaṃ upapannosi dibbaṃ puññehi attano  
 asambādhaṃ sivaṃ rammaṃ accantasukhasaṃhitaṃ  
  
       maññe sahassanettassa vimānaṃ nābhikaṅkhasi  
 iddhī hi tyāyaṃ vipulā sakkasseva jutīmato  
  
       manasāpi na patatabbo anubhāvo jutimato  
 parivārayamānānaṃ saindānaṃ vasavattinaṃ  
  
       taṃ vimānaṃ abhijjhāya amarānaṃ sukhesinaṃ  
 uposathaṃ upavasasanto semi vammikamuddhanī  
  
              
       ahañca migamesāno saputto pāvisiṃ vanaṃ  
 taṃ maṃ mataṃ vā jīvaṃ vā nābhivedenti ñātakā  
  
       āmantaye bhuridantaṃ kāsiputtaṃ yasassinaṃ  
 tayā vo samanuññātā api passemu ñātake  
  
       esohi vata me chando yaṃ vasesi mamattike  
 nahi etādisā kāmā sulabhā honti mānuse  
  
       sace tvaṃ na icchase vatthuṃ mama kāmehi pujito  
 mahā tvaṃ samanuññāto sotthiṃ passāhi  ñātake  
  
       dhārayīmaṃ maṇiṃ divyaṃ pasuṃ putte ca vindati  
 arogo sukhito hoti gacchevādāya brāhmaṇa  
  
    ramā  machasaṃ     passehi  machasaṃ 
  
               
       kusalaṃ paṭinandāmi vaco tava  
 pabbajissāmi jiṇeṇāsmi na kāme abhipatthaye  
  
       brahamacariyassa ce bhaṅgo hoti bhogehi kāriyaṃ  
 avikampamāno eyyāsi bahuṃ dassāmi te dhanaṃ  
  
              
       kusalaṃ paṭinandāmi bhuridatta vaco tava  
 punapi āgamissāmi sace attho bhavissati  
  
       idaṃ vatvā bhuridatto pesesi caturo jane  
 etha gacchatha uṭṭhetha khippaṃ pāpetha brāhmaṇaṃ  
  
       tassa taṃ vacanaṃ sutvā uṭṭhāya caturo janā  
 pesitaṃ bhuridattena khippaṃ pāpesuṃ brāhmaṇaṃ  
 vanappavesakaṇḍo  
  
              
       maṇiṃ paggayaha maṅgalyaṃ sādhu vittaṃ manoramaṃ  
 selaṃ vyañajanasampannaṃ ko imaṃ vaṇimajjhagā  
  
              
       lohitakkhasahassasāhi  samantā parivāritaṃ  
 ajja kālaṃ padaṃ  gacchaṃ ajjhagāhaṃ maṇiṃ imaṃ  
  
       supaciṇṇo ayaṃ solo accito mahito sadā  
 sudhārito sunikkhitto sabbatthabhisādhaye  
  
       upacāravipantassa nikkhepe dhāraṇāya vā  
 alaṃ  selo vināsāya pariciṇṇo ayoniso  
  
       na imaṃ akusalo divyaṃ  maṇiṃ dhāretumāraho  
 paṭipajja sataṃ nikkhaṃ dehimaṃ ratanaṃ mamaṃ  
  
       na vā  myāyaṃ maṇi keyyo gohi mā ratanena vā    
 solo vyañajanasampanto neva keyyo maṇi mamaṃ  
  
    sahassehi  machasaṃ    pathaṃ  machasaṃ    ayaṃ  machasaṃ  vi  
    na imaṃ kusalaṃ dibyaṃ  machasaṃ    neva  machasaṃ    nikkhehi ratanehi vā  machasaṃ  
  
               
              
       no ce tayā maṇi keyyo gohi vā ratanena vā  
 atha kena maṇi keyyo taṃ me akkhāhi pucchito  
  
       yo me saṃse mahānāgaṃ tejasiṃ duratikkamaṃ  
 tassa dajjaṃ imaṃ selaṃ jalantariva tejasā  
  
       konu brahmaṇavaṇṇena supaṇeṇā  patataṃ varo  
 nāgaṃ jigiṃsamanveti anvesaṃ bhakkhamantano  
  
       nāhaṃ dijādhipo homi na diṭṭho garuḷo mayā  
 āsivisena vittoti vejjo  maṃ brāhmaṇaṃ vidu  
  
       kinnu tuyhaṃ balaṃ atthi kiṃ sippaṃ vijjate tava  
 kismiṃ vā tvaṃ paratthaddho uragaṃ nāpacāyasi  
  
       āraññakassa isino cirarattatapassino  
 supaṇṇo kosiyassakkhā visavijjaṃ anuttaraṃ  
  
       taṃ bhāvitattaññataraṃ sammantaṃ  pabbatantare  
 sakkaccaṃ taṃ upaṭṭhāsiṃ ratanindivamatandito  
  
       so tadā pariciṇṇo me vatavā  brahmacariyavā  
 dibbaṃ pātukarī mantaṃ kāmasā bhagavā mamaṃ  
  
              
       tyāhaṃ mante paratthaddho nāhaṃ bhāyāmi bhoginaṃ  
 ācariyo visaghātānaṃ alambānoti maṃ vidu  
  
       gaṇhāmase maṇiṃ tāta somadatta vijānahi  
 mā daṇḍena siriṃ pattaṃ kāmasā pajahimbhase  
  
       sakaṃ nivesanaṃ patataṃ so taṃ brāhmaṇa pujayi  
 evaṃ kalyāṇakārissa kiṃ mohā dubhimicchasi  
  
       sace hi dhanakāmosi bhuridatto  padassati    
 tameva gantvā yācassu bahuṃ dassati te dhanaṃ  
  
    sukhaṇeṇa  machasaṃ    vijjo  machasaṃ    samantaṃ  machasaṃ 
    vattaṃ vā  machasaṃ vatvā  sīmu    bhuridattaṃ  machasaṃ 
    padissasi  machasaṃ 
  
               
       hatthagataṃ pantagataṃ nikkiṇṇaṃ khādituṃ varaṃ  
 mā no sandiṭhiko attho somadatta upaccagā  
  
              
       paccati niraye ghore mahissamavadīyati    
 mittadubhī  hitaccāgi jivarecāpi sussare  
  
       sace hi dhanakāmosi bhuridatto padassati  
 maññe antakataṃ veraṃ naciraṃ vedayissasi  
  
       mahāyaññaṃ yajitvāna evaṃ sujjhanti brāhmaṇā  
 mahāyaññaṃ yajissāma evaṃ mokkhāma pāpakā  
  
       handāni apāyāmi nāhaṃ ajja tayā saha  
 padampekaṃ nagaccheyyaṃ evaṃ kimbisakārinā  
  
       idaṃ vatvāna pitaraṃ somadatto bahussuto  
 ujjhāpetvāna bhūtāni tambhā ṭhānā apakkami  
  
              
       gaṇhāhetaṃ mahānāgaṃ āharetaṃ maṇiṃ mama  
 indagopakavaṇṇabho yassa lohitako siro  
  
       kappāsapicurāsīva eso kāyassa dissati    
 vammikaggagato seti taṃ tvaṃ gaṇhāhi brāhmaṇa  
  
              
       athosadhehi dibbehi japaṃ mantapadāni ca  
 evaṃ taṃ asakkhi saṭṭhuṃ  katvā parittamattano  
 kīḷanakhaṇḍo  
  
              
       mamaṃ disvāna āyantaṃ sabbakāmasamiddhinaṃ  
 indiyāni ahaṭṭhāni sāvaṃ jātaṃ  mukhaṃ tava  
  
       padumaṃ yathā hatthagataṃ pāṇinā parimadditaṃ  
 sāvaṃ jātaṃ mukhaṃ tuyhaṃ mamaṃ disvāna edisaṃ  
  
    mabhissamaci vivarati  machasaṃ mabhimassa cinadriyati  syā 
    mittadubbhi  machasaṃ  syā    kāyo disasti  machasaṃ  syā 
    satthuṃ  machasaṃ phuṭṭhuṃ  syā    jātiṃ  machasaṃ    padama  machasaṃ  
  
               
  
       kaccinnu te nābhisayi kacci te atthi vedanā    
 yena sāvaṃ mukhaṃ tuyhaṃ mamaṃ disvāna āgataṃ  
  
              
       supitaṃ tāta addakkhiṃ ito māsaṃ adhogataṃ  
 dakkhiṇaṃ viya me bāhaṃ  chetvā ruhiramakkhitaṃ 
 puriso ādāya pakkāmi mamaṃ rodantiyā sati  
  
       yato taṃ  supinamaddakkhiṃ sudasasna vijānahi  
 tato divā vā rattiṃ vā sukhaṃ me na upalabbati    
  
       yaṃ pubbe paricāriṃsu  kaññā ruciraviggahā  
 hemajālapaṭicchattā bhuridatto na dissati  
  
       yaṃ pubbe paricāriṃsu nettiṃsavaradhārino  
 kaṇikārā  viya samphullā bhuridatto na dissati  
  
       handadāni gamissāma bhuridattanivesanaṃ  
 dhammaṭṭhaṃ sīlasampannaṃ passāma tava bhātaraṃ  
  
       tañca disvāna āyantiṃ  bhuridattassa mātaraṃ  
 bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ bhuridattassa nāriyo  
  
       puttaṃ teyye na jānāma ito māsaṃ adhogataṃ  
 mataṃ vā yadi vā jīvaṃ bhuridattaṃ yasassinaṃ  
  
              
       sakuṇi hataputtāva suññaṃ disvā kulāvakaṃ  
 ciraṃ dukkhena jhāyissaṃ bhuridattaṃ apassati  
  
       sakuṇi hataputtāva suññaṃ disvā kulāvakaṃ  
 tena tena padhāvissaṃ piyaputtaṃ apassati  
  
       kuriraṃ hatachāpāva suññaṃ disvā kulāvakaṃ  
 ciraṃ dukkhena jhāyissaṃ bhuridattaṃ apassati  
  
       sā nūna cakkavākīva pallalasmiṃ anudake  ciraṃ dukkhena jhāyissaṃ bhuridattaṃ apassati  
  
    bahu  machasaṃ    haṃ  machasaṃ  syā    nopalabbha  machasaṃ  syā 
    paricāriṃsu  machasaṃ  syā    kaṇikārāva  machasaṃ  syā 
    āyantaṃ  machasaṃ  syā 
  
               
       kammārānaṃ yathā ukkā anto jhāyati no bahi  
 evaṃ jhāyāmi sokena bhuridattaṃ apassati  
  
       sālāva sampamathitā  mālutena pamadditā  
 senti puttā ca dārā ca bhuridattanivesano 
  
       idaṃ  sutvāna nigghosaṃ bhuridattanivesane  
 ariṭṭho ca subhago  ca upadhāviṃsu  ananatarā  
  
       amma assāsa mā sovi evaṃ dhammā hi pāṇino  
 cavanti upapajjanti phasassa pariṇāmitā  
  
              
       ahampi tāta jānāmi evaṃ dhammā hi pāṇino  
 sokena ca paretasmiṃ bhuridattaṃ apassati  
  
       ajja ce me imaṃ rattiṃ sudassana vijānahi  
 bhuridannaṃ apassanti maññe hessāmi  jīvitaṃ  
  
       amma assāsa mā soci ānayissāma bhātaraṃ  
 disodisaṃ gamissāma bhātupariyesanaṃ caraṃ  
  
       pabbate giriduggesu gāmesu nigamesu ca  
 orena dasarattassa  passa āgataṃ  
  
              
       hatthā pamutto urago pāde te nipatī bhusaṃ  
 kacci  taṃ nu ḍasī tāta mā bhāyi sukhito bhava    
  
       neva mayhaṃ ayaṃ nāgo alaṃ dukkhāya kāyaci  
 yāvatatthi abhiggāhā mayā bhiyyo na vijjati  
  
       konu brāhmaṇa vaṇeṇana datto parisamāgamā  
 avhayantu suyuddhena suṇātu parisā mamaṃ  
  
    saṃpamadditā  machasaṃ    tesaṃ  machasaṃ  syā    subhogova machasaṃ  syā    padhāciṃsu  machasaṃ  syā    pariṇāmatā  machasaṃ  syā 
    bhissāmi  machasaṃ  syā    ratatarattassa  machasaṃ  syā    kacacitaṃ ḍaṃsito  machasaṃ kaccisiṃnuḍato  syā    tava  machasaṃ 
  
               
       tvaṃ maṃ nāgena ālamba ahaṃ maṇḍukachāpiyā  
 hotu no abbhutaṃ tattha āsahassehi pacañahi  
  
       ahaṃ hi vasumā aḍḍho tvaṃ daḷiddosi māṇava  ko nu te paṭihogatthi upajutañca  kiṃ siyā  
  
       upajutañca me assa pāṭibhogo ca tādiso  
 hotu  no abbhutaṃ tattha āsahassehi pañcahi  
  
              
       suṇohi me mahārāja vacanaṃ bhaddamatthu te  
 pañcantaṃ me sahasasānaṃ pāṭibhogohi kintimā  
  
       pettikaṃ vā iṇaṃ hoti yaṃ vā hoti sayaṃ kataṃ  
 kiṃ tvaṃ evaṃ bahuṃ mayhaṃ dhanaṃ yācasi brāhmaṇa  
  
       ālambāno  hi nāgena mamaṃ abhijigiṃsati    
 ahaṃ maṇḍukachāpiyā ḍaṃsasissāmi brāhmaṇaṃ  
  
       taṃ tvaṃ daṭṭhuṃ mahārāja ajja raṭṭhābhivaddhana  
 khantasaṅghaparibbuḷho niyyāhi ahidassanaṃ  
  
       neva taṃ atimaññāmi sippavādena māṇava  
 atimantosi sippena uragaṃ nāpacāyasi  
  
              
       mayampi nātimaññama sippavādena brāhmaṇaṃ  
 avisena ca nāgena bhusaṃ vañcayase janaṃ  
  
       evaṃ cetaṃ jano jaññā yathā jānāmi taṃ ahaṃ  
 na tvaṃ lahasi  ālamba sattumuṭṭhiṃ  kuto dhanaṃ  
  
       kharājino jaṭi rummi  datto  parisamāgato  
 so tvaṃ evaṃ gataṃ nāgaṃ aviso atimaññasi  
  
    opajutañca  machasaṃ    assuto  machasaṃ assano  vi 
    ālambāyano ca syā alambano ca     abijigisati  machasaṃ 
    lahesi  machasaṃ    bhusamuṭṭhiṃ  machasaṃ  syā    dummi  machasaṃ 
    dittā  machasaṃ 
  
               
       āsajja kho taṃ  jaññāsi puṇaṇaṃ uggassa tejasā  
 maññe taṃ bhasmarāsivaṃ khippasā kairissati  
  
       siyā visaṃ siḷuttassa deḍḍhuhassa silābhuno  
 neva lohitasisassa visaṃ nāgassa vijjati  
  
       sutaṃ metaṃ arabhataṃ saññatānaṃ tapassinaṃ  
 idha dānāni datvāna saggaṃ gacchanti dāyakā 
 jivanto dehi dānāni yadi te atthi dātave  
  
       ayaṃ nāgo mahiddhiko tejasī duratikkamo  
 tena taṃ ḍaṃsayissāmi so taṃ bhasmaṃ karissati  
  
       mayāpetaṃ sutaṃ samma saññatānaṃ tapassinaṃ  
 idha dānini datvāna saggaṃ gacchanti dāyakā 
 tvameva dehi jivanto yadi te atthi dāteve  
              
       ayaṃ accimukhi nāma  puṇṇā uggassa tejasā  
 tena taṃ ḍaṃsayissāmi so taṃ bhasmaṃ karissati  
  
       yā dhītā dhataraṭṭhassa vemātā bhagini mama  
 sā dissatu accimukhi  puṇaṇā uggassa tejasā  
  
       chamāyaṃ ce nisiñcissaṃ brahmadanta vijānahi  
 tiṇalatāni osadhyo usasusseyyuṃ asaṃsayaṃ  
  
       addhaṃ  ce pātayissāmi brahmadanta vijānahi  
 sattavassānayaṃ devo na vasse na himaṃ pate  
  
              
       udakañce nisiñcissaṃ brahmadanta vijānahi  
 yāvatā  odakā pāṇā mareyyuṃ macchakacchapā  
 nagarappavesanakaṇḍaṃ niṭṭitaṃ  
  
    naṃ  machasaṃ    tejaso  machasaṃ    ajamukhi  machasaṃ 
    taṃḍaṃsatvājamukhi  machasaṃ ḍaṃsatu  syā    udake ce  machasaṃ 
    yāvanetā  machasaṃ 
  
               
              
       lokyaṃ sajantaṃ udakaṃ payāgasmiṃ patiṭṭhitaṃ  
 ko maṃ ajjhohari bhuto ogāḷhaṃ yamunaṃ nadiṃ  
  
       yadesalokādhipati yasassī 
 bārāṇasimpakirahari samantato  
 tassāhaṃ putto uragusabhassa 
 subhagoti maṃ brāhmaṇa vedayanti  
  
       sace hi putto uragusabhassa 
 kaṃsassa rañño amarādhipassa 
 mahesakkho aññataro pitā te 
 maccesu mātā pana te atulyā 
 na tādiso arahati brāhmaṇassa 
 dāsampi ohārituṃ mahānubhāvo  
  
              
       rukkhaṃ nissāya vijjhittho phaṇeyyaṃ pātumāgataṃ  
 so viddho duramasarā  saravegena sekhavā    
  
       taṃ tvaṃ patitamaddakkhi araññasmiṃ brahmane  
 sa maṃsakājamādāya sāyaṃ nigrodhupāgami  
  
       suvalāsiya  saṅghuṭṭhaṃ piṃgiyaṃ  santhatāyutaṃ  
 kokilābhirudaṃ rammaṃ dhuvaṃ haritasaddalaṃ  
  
       tattha te so pāturahu  iddhiyā yasasā jalaṃ  
 mahānubhāvo bhātā me kaññāhi parivārito  
  
       so tena pariciṇṇo tvaṃ sabbakāmehi tapapito  
 adubhassa  tuvaṃ dubhi taṃ te veraṃ idhāgataṃ  
  
       khippaṃ gīvaṃ pasārehi na te dassāmi jīvitaṃ  
 bhātuparisaraṃ veraṃ chedayissāmi te siraṃ  
  
       ajjhāyako yācayogo  āhutaggī ca brāhmaṇo  
 etehi tīhi ṭhānehi avajjho bhavati  brāhmaṇo  
  
    duramacari  machasaṃ  duramācari  syā    pekkhavā  machasaṃ  syā 
    sālika  machasaṃ    piṅgalaṃ  machasaṃ    pātvarahu  machasaṃ 
    parivārito  machasaṃ    aduṭṭhassa  machasaṃ  syā    yācayogi  machasaṃ  syā    hoti  machasaṃ  
  
               
              
       yaṃ puraṃ dhataraṭṭhassa ogāḷhaṃ  yamunaṃ nadiṃ  
 jotate  sabbasovaṇṇaṃ giriṃ āhacca yāmunaṃ    
  
       tattha te purisavyagghā sodariyā mama bhātaro  
 yathā te tattha vakkhanti tathā hessasi brāhmaṇa  
 subhagakhaṇḍo  
  
       anittarā ittarasampayuttā 
 yaññā ca vedā  ca subhoga loke  
 tadaggarayhaṃ hi vinindamāno 
 jahāti vittañca satañca dhammaṃ  
  
              
       ajjhenamariyā paṭaviṃ janinda 
 vessā kasiṃ paricariyañca suddā  
 upāgu paccekaṃ yathā padesaṃ 
 katāhu ete vasināti āhu  
  
       dhātā vidhātā varuṇo kuvero 
 somo yamo candimā vāyu sariyo  
 ete hi yaññaṃ puthuso yajitvā 
 ajjhāyakānaṃ atha  sabbakāme  
  
       vikāsitā cāpasatāni pañca 
 yo ajjuno balavā bhīmaseno    
 sahassabāhu asamo paṭhavyā 
 sopi tadā ādahi jātavedaṃ  
  
              
       yo brāhmaṇo bhojayī dīgharattaṃ 
 antena pāṇena yathānubhāvaṃ  
 pasannacitto anumodamāno 
 subhoga devaññataro ahosi  
  
       mahāsanaṃ devamanomavaṇṇaṃ 
 yo sappinā asakkhi jetumaggiṃ  
 so yaññatantaṃ varato yajitvā 
 dibbaṃ gatiṃ mucalindajjhagañachiṃ  
  
    oghāḷhaṃ  machasaṃ    jotantaṃ  machasaṃ    yamunaṃ  machasaṃ 
    khe  machasaṃ    atho  machasaṃ    bhimaseno  machasaṃ 
  
               
              
       mahānubhāvo vassasahassajivi 
 yo pabbaji  dassaneyyo uḷāro  
 hitvā apariyantarathaṃ  sasenaṃ 
 rājā dudipopi jagāmaṃ  saggaṃ  
  
       yo sāgaro sāgarantaṃ vijitvā 
 yupaṃ subhaṃ soṇṇamayaṃ uḷāraṃ  
 ussesi vessānaramādahāno  
 subhogi devaññataro ahosi  
  
       yassānubhāvena suboga saṅgā 
 pavattatha  dadhisannaṃ samuddaṃ  
 sa lomapādo paricariyamaggiṃ 
 aṅgo sahassakkhapurajjhagañachi  
  
              
       mahiddhiko deva varo yasassi 
 senāpati tidive vāsavassa  
 sa somayāgena malaṃ vihanatvā 
 subhoga devaññataro ahosi  
  
       akāri  yo lokamimaṃ parañca 
 bhāgīrathiṃ  himavantañca gijjhaṃ  
 yo iddhimā devavaro yasassī 
 sopi tadā ādahi jātavedaṃ  
  
       mālāgiri himavā yo ca gijjho 
 sudassano  nisaho kākaneru    
 ete ca aññe ca nagā mahantā 
 cityā katā yaññakarehi māhu  
  
              
       ajjhāyakaṃ mantaguṇupapannaṃ 
 tapassinaṃ yācayogoti cāha     
 tire samuddassudakaṃ sajantaṃ 
 taṃ sāgarajjhohari tenapeyyo  
  
    pabbajji  machasaṃ    raṭṭhaṃ  machasaṃ  syā    cagāmi  machasaṃ  
    vassānara  machasaṃ    pavattati  machasaṃ  syā    akāsi yaṃ  machasaṃ akārayi syā    hāgirathaṃ  syā bagirasi  machasaṃ    sudassino  machasaṃ 
    kuveru  machasaṃ kākaveru  syā     cāhu  machasaṃ dhāhu  syā 
  
               
       āyāgavatthuni puthu pathavyā 
 saṃvijjanti brāhmaṇā vāsavassa  
 purimaṃ disaṃ pacchimaṃ dakkhiṇuttaraṃ 
 saṃvijjamānā janayanti vedaṃ  
  
              
       kaliṃ  hi dhīrānaṃ kaṭaṃ magānaṃ 
 bhavanti vedajjhagatānariṭṭha  
 marividhammaṃ asamekkhitattā 
 māyāguṇā nāti vahanti paññaṃ  
  
       vedā na tāṇāya bhavantirassa  
 mittadduno bhunahuno narassa  
 na tāyate pariciṇṇo ca aggi 
 dosantaraṃ maccaṃ anariyakammaṃ  
  
       sabbañce maccā sadhanā  sabhogā  
 ādipitaṃ dārutiṇena missaṃ  
 dahaṃ na tappe asamattha  tejo 
 ko taṃ subhikkhaṃ dirasañña kuriyā  
  
       yathāpi khiraṃ viparināmadhammaṃ dadhi bhavitvā navanitampi hoti  evampi aggi viparināmadhammo 
 tejo samorohati yogayutto  
  
       na dissate aggimanuppaviṭṭho 
 sukkhesu kaṭṭhesu navesu cāpi  
 nāmanthamāno araṇinarena 
 nākammanā jāyati jātavedo  
  
       sace hi aggi antarato vaseyya 
 sukkhesu kaṭṭhesu navesu cāpi  
 sabbāni susseyyuṃ vanāni loke 
 sukkhāni kaṭṭhāni ca pajjaleyyuṃ  
  
    kalīhi  machasaṃ  syā    bhavantidassa  machasaṃ    sadhanaṃ  machasaṃ 
    sabhogaṃ  machasaṃ    aggi asamattha  machasaṃ    kayirā  machasaṃ  syā  
  
               
       karoti ce  dārutiṇena puññaṃ 
 bhojaṃ  naro dhumasikhiṃ 
 aṅgārikā loṇakarā ca sudā 
 sariradāhāpi kareyyuṃ puññaṃ  
  
              
       atha ve hi ete na karonti puññaṃ  
 ajjhenamaggiṃ idha tappayitvā  
 na koci lokasmiṃ karoti puññaṃ 
 bhojaṃ naro dhumasikhiṃ patāpavaṃ  
  
       kathaṃ hi lokāpacito samāno 
 amanuññagandhaṃ bahunnaṃ akantaṃ  
 yadeva maccā parivajjayanti 
 tadappasatthaṃ dirasañña bhuñeja  
  
       sikhiṃ hi devesu vadanti heke 
 āpaṃ milakkhā pana devamāhu  
 sabbeva ete vitathaṃ bhaṇanti  
 aggī na devaññataro na cāpo  
  
       nirindiyaṃ santaṃ asaññakāyaṃ  
 vessānaraṃ kammakaraṃ pajānaṃ  
 paricariya  maggiṃ sugatiṃ kathaṃ vaje  
 pāpāni kammāni pakubbamāno  
  
       sabbāhibhūtāhudha jivikatthā 
 aggissa brahmā paricārakoti  
 sabbānubhāvi ca vasī kimatthaṃ 
 animmito nimmitaṃ vanditassa  
  
       hassaṃ anijjhānakhaoṃ atacchaṃ 
 sakkārahetu pakiriṃsu  pubbe  
 te lābhasakkāre apātubhonte 
 santhambhitā  jantuhi santidhammaṃ  
  
       ajjhenamariyā paṭhaviṃ janindā 
 vessā kasiṃ paricariyañca suddā  
 upāgu paccekaṃ yathā  padesaṃ 
 katāhu ete vasināti āhu  
  
    ve  machasaṃ    bhojanaro  machasaṃ    gaṇhahanti  machasaṃ 
    anindriyabaddha masaññakāyaṃ  machasaṃ anindriyaṃ  syā 
    pariccaramaggiṃ sugatiṃ kathaṃ vajje  machasaṃ    vajje  machasaṃ  syā 
    pakakariṃsu  machasaṃ    santapitā  machasaṃ sandhāhitā  syā 
    tathā  machasaṃ 
  
               
              
       etañca saccaṃ vacanaṃ bhaveyya 
 yathā idaṃ bhāsitaṃ brāhmaṇehi  
 nākhantiyo jātu labhetha rajjaṃ 
 nābrāhmaṇo mantapadāni sikkhe 
 nāññatra vessehi kasiṃ kareyya 
 suddo na muñce parapessitāya   
  
       yasvā ca etaṃ vacanaṃ abhūtaṃ 
 musā cime odariyā bhaṇanti  
 tadappapaññā abhīsaddahanti 
 passanti taṃ paṇḍitā attanāva  
  
       khattyā na vessā na khaliṃ haranti 
 ādāya satthāni caranti brāhmaṇā  
 taṃ tādisaṃ saṃkhuhitaṃ vihinnaṃ  
 kasmā brahmā nujjukaroti lokaṃ  
  
       sace hi so issaro sabbaloke 
 brahmā bahu bhūtapati pajānaṃ  
 kiṃ sabbalokaṃ vidihi alakkhiṃ 
 kiṃ sabbalokaṃ na sukhī akāsi  
       sace hi so issaro sabbaloke 
 brahmā bahu bhūtapati pajānaṃ  
 mayā musāvajjamade cāpi 
 lokaṃ adhammena kimatthakāsi  
  
       sace hi so issaro sabbaloke 
 brahmā bahu bhūtapati pajānaṃ  
 adhammiyo  bhupati ariṭṭha 
 dhamme sati so vidahī adhammaṃ  
  
       kīṭā paṭaṃgā uragā ca bhekā  
 hanatvā kimiṃ sujjhati makkhikā ca  ete hi dhammā anariyarūpā 
 kambojakānaṃ vitathā bahunnaṃ  
  
              
       sace hi so sujjhati yo hanāti 
 hatopi sosa saggamupeti ṭhānaṃ  
 bhovādi bhovādinaṃ mārayeyyuṃ  
 ye cāpi tesaṃ abhisaddaheyyuṃ  
  
    parapesanāya  machasaṃ parapessatāya  syā    pahinnaṃ  machasaṃ 
    adhammiko  machasaṃ  syā    bhiṅga  machasaṃ  syā 
    māraśeyyuṃ  machasaṃ 
  
               
       neva migā nappasunopi gāvo 
 āyācanti antavadhāya  keci  
 vipphandamānaṃ idhajivikatthā 
  
       yupassa  te pasubandhe ca bālā 
 cittehi vaṇeṇahi mukhaṃ nayanti  
 ayaṃ te yupo kāmaduho parattha 
 bhavissati sassato samparāyaṃ  
  
       sace ca yupe maṇisaṅkhamuttaṃ 
 dhaññaṃ dhanaṃ rajataṃ jātarūpaṃ  
 sukkhesu kiṭṭhesu navesu cāpi 
 sace duhe tidive sabbakāme 
 tevijjasaṅghā ca puthu yajeyyuṃ 
 na brāhmaṇā kañci taṃ  yājayeyyuṃ  
  
       kuto ca yupe maṇisaṅkhamuttaṃ 
 dhaññaṃ dhanaṃ rajataṃ jātarūpaṃ 
 sukkhesu kaṭṭhesu navesu cāpi 
 kuto duhe tidive sabbakāme  
  
       yaṭhā ca luddā upaladdhabālā  
 cittehi vaṇeṇahi mukhaṃ nayanti  
 ādāya aggiṃ mama dehi vittaṃ 
 tato sukhī hohisi sabbakāme  
  
       tamaggihuttaṃ saraṇaṃ pavissa 
 cittehi vaṇeṇahi mukhaṃ nayanti  
 oropayitvā kesamassuṃ nakhañca 
 vedehi cittaṃ atigāḷayanti  
  
              
       kākā ulukaṃca rabho labhitvā 
 ekaṃ samānaṃ bahukā samecca  
 annāni bhutvā kuhāka kuhitvā 
 muṇḍaṃ karitvā yaññapathossajanti  
  
       evaṃ hi so vañcito brāhmaṇehi 
 eko samāno bahuhi  samecca  
 te yogayogena vilumpamānā 
 diṭṭhaṃ adiṭṭhena dhanaṃ haranti  
  
    rattavadhāya  machasaṃ    yupussa ne  machasaṃ  sāya    nici  machasaṃ  syā 
    paluddha  machasaṃ  syā    bahukā  machasaṃ  syā 
  
               
       akāsiyā rājuhi cānu  siṭṭhā 
 tadassa ādāya dhanaṃ haranti  
 teta tādisā corasamā asantā 
 vajjhā na haññanti ariṭṭha loke  
  
       indassa bāhārasi dakkhiṇāti 
 yaññesu chindanti palāsayaṭṭhiṃ  
 taṃ cepi saccaṃ maghavā chinnabāhu 
 kenassa indo asure jināti  
  
       tañceva tucchaṃ maghavā samaṅgī 
 hantā avajjho paramo sa devo  
 mantā  ime brāhmaṇā tuccharūpā 
 sandiṭṭhikā vañcanā esa loke  
  
       mālāgiri himavā yo ca gijjho 
 sudassano nisabho kākaneru    
 ete ca aññe ca nagā mahantā 
 cityā katā yaññakarehi māhu  
       yathāppakārāni hi iṭṭhakāni 
 cityā katā yaññakarehi māhu  
 na pabbātā honti tathappakārā 
 aññādisā acalā tiṭṭhaselā  
  
              
       na iṭṭhakā honti silā cirenapi 
 na tattha sañajāyati ayo na lohaṃ  
 yañce ca etaṃ parivaṇaṇayantā 
 cityā katā yaññakarehi māhu  
  
       ajjhāyakaṃ mantaguṇupapannaṃ 
 tapassinaṃ yācayogoti māhu  
 tire samuddassudakaṃ sajannaṃ 
 taṃ sāgarajjhohari tena  peyyo  
  
       paro sahassampi samantavede 
 manatuppanne nadiyo vahanti  
 na tena vyāpantarasudakānaṃ  
 kasmā samuddo atulo apeyyo  
  
    vānu  machasaṃ  syā    satatā  machasaṃ  syā    kāveru  machasaṃ 
    vāhu  machasaṃ    rasudaka ni  machasaṃ  syā  
               
       ye keci kūpā idha jivaloke 
 loṇudakā kūpakhaṇehi khātā  
 na brāhmaṇajjhoharaṇena tesu 
 āpo apeyyo dirasaññarāhu  
  
       pure puratthā kā kasasa bhariyā 
 mano manussaṃ ajanesi pubbe  
 tenāpi dhammena na koci hīno 
 evampi vossaggavibhāgamāhu  
  
       caṇḍāluttopi adhicca vede 
 bhāseyya mante kusalo mutimā  
 na tassa muddhā viphaleyya sattadhā 
 mantā ime attavadhāya katatā  
  
       vācākatā giddhikatā  gahitā 
 dummocayā kavyapathānupantā  
 bālānacittaṃ visame niviṭṭhaṃ 
 tadappapaññā abhisaddahanti  
  
       sīhassa vyagghassa ca dipano 
 na vijjati porisiyaṃ balena  
 manussabhāvo ca gavaṃva pekkho 
 jātī hi tesaṃ asamā samānā    
  
              
       sace ca rājā paṭhaviṃ vijitthā 
 sajivavā assavo pārisajjo  
 sayameva so sattusaṅghaṃ  vijeyya 
 tassa pajā niccasukhī bhaveyya  
  
       khattiyamantā ca tayo ca vedā 
 atthena ete samakā bhavanti  
 tesañca atthaṃ avinicchinitvā 
 na khujjhati oghapathaṃva channaṃ  
  
       khattiyamantā ca tayo ca vedā 
 atthena ete samakā bhavanti  
 lābho alābho ayaso yaso ca 
 sabbe te sabbesaṃ catunnadhammā  
  
    kātā  machasaṃ    giḍigatā  machasaṃ  syā    samānaṃ  machasaṃ  syā 
    saṃgha  machasaṃ 
  
               
       yathāpi ibbhā dhanadhañca hetu 
 kammāni kārenti  puthu pathavyā  
 tevijjasaṅghāpi  tatheva ajja 
 kammāni kārenti puthu pathavyā  
  
       ibbehi ete samakā bhavanti  
 niccussakā  kāmaguṇesu yuttā  
 kammāni kārenti puthu pathavyā 
 tadapappaññā dirasaññarā te  
 yaññabhedavādakaṇḍo  
  
              
       kassa heri mutiṃgā ca saṅkhāpaṇavadeṇḍimā    
 purato paṭipannāni hāsayantā rathesabhaṃ  
  
       kassa kañcanapaṭṭena puthunā vijjuvaṇaṇinā  
 yuvā kalāpasannaddho ko eti siriyā jalaṃ  
  
       ukkāmukhe  sahaṭṭhaṃva khadiraṅgārasannibhaṃ  
 mukhaṃ cārurivābhāti  ko eti siriyā jalaṃ  
  
              
       kassa jambonadaṃ chattaṃ sasalākaṃ manoramaṃ  
 ādiccaraṃsāvaraṇaṃ ko eti siriyā jalaṃ  
  
       kassa aṅkaṃ  pariggayha vāḷavijanittamaṃ  
 carate  varapaññassa muddhani uparūpari  
  
       kassa pekhuṇahatthāni vicitrāni muduni ca  
 tapaññamaṇidaṇḍāni  caranti ubhato mukhaṃ  
  
       khadiraṅgāravaṇaṇahā okkāmukhe pahaṃsitā  
 kassete kuṇḍalā vaggu sohanti ubhato mukhaṃ  
  
       kassa vānena chupitā niddhantā mudukālakaṃ     
 sobhayanti nalāvantaṃ nabhā vijjurivuggatā  
  
       kassa etāni akkhini āyatāni puthuni ca  
 ko sobhati visālakkho kassetaṃ uṇaṇajaṃ mukhaṃ  
  
    karonti  machasaṃ    cārudivā  machasaṃ 
    saṅghāva  machasaṃ    aṅgaṃ  machasaṃ  syā 
    niccussukkā  machasaṃ    ubhato  machasaṃ  syā 
    dindimā  machasaṃ  syā    kañavanamaṇidaṇḍāni  machasaṃ suvaṇṇa  syā 
    okkāmukha  aṭṭhakathā     kālakaṃ  machasaṃ 
  
               
       kassete lapanajā  suddhasaṅkhavarūpamā  
 bhāsamānassa sobhanti dantā kuppalasādisā  
  
       kassa lākhārasasamā hatthapādā sukhedhitā  
 ko so bimboṭṭha sampanno divā suriyova bhāsati  
  
       himaccaye bhemavato  brahāsālova  pupphito  
 ko so odātapācāro jayaṃ indova sebhati  
  
       suvaṇaṇapiḷakākiṇṇaṃ maṇidaṇḍavicittikaṃ    
 ko so parisamogayha īso  khaggaṃva muccati  
       suvaṇaṇa vikatā citrā  sukatā citrā sibbanā    
 ko soomuñcate padā namo katvā mahesino  
  
              
       dhataraṭṭhā hi  te nāgā iddhimanto yasassino  
 samuddajāya uppantā ete nāgā mahiddhikāti  
 bhuridattajātakaṃ chaṭṭhamaṃ  
  
 mahānāradakassapa jātakaṃ sattamaṃ  
              
       ahu rājā videhānaṃ aṅgāti    nāma khattiyo  
 pahutayoggo dhanimā anantabalaporiso  
  
       so ca paṇaṇarasiṃ   rattiṃ purime yā anāgate  
 cātumassa   komudiyā amacce sannipātayi  
  
       paṇḍite sutasamapanne mihitapubbe   vivakkhaṇe  
 vijayañca sunāmañca senāpatimalātakaṃ  
  
       tamanupucchi vedeho paccekaṃ brūtha saṃruciṃ  
 cātumassa   komudajja puṇhaṃ vyapagataṃ tamaṃ 
 kāyajja ratiyā rattiṃ viharemu imaṃ utuṃ  
  
    lapanājātā  machasaṃ    bhimavati  machasaṃ    mahāsālova  machasaṃ 
    rucittakaṃ  machasaṃ  syā    īsaṃ  machasaṃ  īse  syā 
    rittā  machasaṃ    cittako  machasaṃ syā 
    sibba sibbanī  machasaṃ  syā    dhatharaṭṭassa  syā 
     aṅgati  machasaṃ  syā     pannarase  machasaṃ  syā 
     cātumāsā  machasaṃ cātumāsa  vi     mita  machasaṃ syā 
     cātumāsā  machasaṃ 
  
               
       tato senāpati rañño alāto etadabravi  
 haṭṭhaṃ  yoggaṃ balaṃ sabbaṃ senaṃ santāhayāmase  
  
              
       niyyāma deva yuddhāya anantabalaporisā    
 ye te vasaṃ na āyanti vasaṃ upanayāmase    
 esā mayhaṃ sakādiṭṭhi ajitaṃ ojināmase    
  
       alātassa vaco sutvā sunāmo etadabravi  
 sabbe tuyhaṃ mahārāja avittā vasamāgatā  
  
       nikkhittasatthā paccatthā nivātamanuvatatare  
 uttamo ussavo ajja na yuddhaṃ mama ruccati  
  
       annaṃ pānañca khajjañca khippaṃ abhiharantu te  
 ramassu deva kāmehi naccagīte suvādite  
  
       sunāssa vāco sutvā vijayo etadabravi  
 sabbe kāmā mahārāja niccaṃ tava apaṭṭhitā  
  
       na hete dullahā deva tava kāmehi modituṃ  
 sadāpi kāmā labbhanti  netaṃ cittamataṃ mama  
  
       samaṇaṃ brāhoṃ vāpi upāsemu bahussutaṃ  
 yo najja vinaye kaṅkhaṃ atthadhammavidu ise  
       vijayassa vaco sutvā rājā aṅgātimabravi  
 yathā vijayo bhaṇati mayhampeteva ruccati  
       samaṇaṃ brāhoṃ vāpi upāsemu bahussutaṃ  
 yo najja vinaye kaṅkhaṃ atthadhammavidu ise  
  
       sabbeva santā karotha matiṃ kaṃ upāsemu paṇḍitaṃ  
 konajja vinaye kaṅkhaṃ atthadhammavidu ise  
  
       vedehassa vaco sutvā alāto etadabravi  
 atthāya migadāyasmiṃ avelo dhirasammato  
  
    hataṃ  machasaṃ    poriso  machasaṃ    upaniyyāmase  machasaṃ  syā 
    ojiyāmase  machasaṃ  syā    sulabhā  machasaṃ 
  
               
       guṇo kassapattoyaṃ suto citrakathi gaṇī  
 taṃ deva payirupāsaya  so no kaṅkhaṃ vinessati  
  
       alātassa vaco sutvā rājā codesi sārathiṃ  
 migadāyaṃ gamissāma yuttaṃ yānaṃ idānaya  
  
              
       tassa yānaṃ ayojesuṃ dantaṃ rūpiyapakkharaṃ  
 sukkamaṭṭhaparivāraṃ paṇḍaraṃ dosināmukhaṃ  
  
       tatrāsuṃ kumudā yuttā cattāro sindhavā hāyā  
 anilupamasamuppātā  sudantā soṇṇamālino  
  
       setaṃ chattaṃ setaratho setassā setavijanī  
 vedeho sahamaccehi nīyyaṃ candova sobhatha    
  
       tamannuyāyuṃ  bahāvo indakhaggadharā khalī  
 assapiṭṭhigatā dhīrā  narā naravarādhipaṃ  
       so muhuttaṃ va yāyitthā yānā oruyha khattiyo  
 vedeho sahamaccehi patti guṇamupāgami  
  
       yopi tattha tadā āsuṃ brāhmaṇibbhā samāgatā  
 na te apanayī rājā akaṭaṃ bhumimāgate  
  
              
       tato so mudukābhisiyā muducittakalandake  
 mudupaccatthate rājā ekamantaṃ upāvisi  
  
       nisajja rājā sammodi kathaṃ sārāṇiyaṃ tato  
 kacci yāpanīyaṃ bhante vātānamavisaggatā    
  
       kacci akasirā vutti labbhati piṇḍayāpanaṃ  
 appabādhovasi  kacci cakkhuṃ paribhāyati  
  
       taṃ guṇopaṭisammodi vedehaṃ vinaye rataṃ  
 yāpaniyaṃ mahārāja sabbametaṃ kadubhayaṃ  
  
    payirupāsema  machasaṃ  syā    akiluppasamuppādā  machasaṃ 
    sobhati  machasaṃ  syā    tamanuyāyiṃsu  machasaṃ 
    virā  machasaṃ    muduvitatakasanthate  machasaṃ 
    vātānamaciyatatatā  syā    appābādho  machasaṃ 
  
               
       kacci tuyhampi vedeha paccantā na baliyare  
 kacci arogaṃ yoggante kacci vahati  vāhanaṃ 
 kacaci te vyādhayo natthi sarirassupatāpikā    
  
       paṭisammodito rājā tato pucchi anantarā  
 atthaṃ dhammañca ñāyañca dhammakamo rathesabho  
  
       kathaṃ dhammaṃ care macco mātāpitusu kassapa  
 kathaṃ vacare ācariye puttadāre kathaṃ care  
  
       kathaṃ careyya vuddhesu kathaṃ samaṇabrāhmaṇe  
 kathañca balakāyasmiṃ kathaṃ jānapade care  
  
       kathaṃ dhammaṃ caritvāna pecca gacchati  suggatiṃ  
 kathañceke adhammaṭṭhā patanti nirayaṃ adho  
  
              
       vedehassa vaco sutvā kassapo ekadabravi  
 suṇohi me mahārāja saccaṃ avitatha padaṃ  
  
       natthi dhammassa ciṇaṇassa  phalaṃ kalyāṇapāpakaṃ  
 natthi deva paro loko ko tato hi idhāgato  
  
       natthi deva pitaro vā kuto mātā kuto pitā  
 natthi ācariyo nāma adantaṃ ko damesasti  
  
       samatulyāni bhūtāni natthī jeṭṭhāpavāyino  
 natthi balaṃ vā viriyaṃ vā kuto uṭṭhānaporisaṃ    
 niyatāni hi bhūtāni yathā goṭaviso tathā  
  
       laddhyeṃ labhate macco tattha dānaphalaṃ kuto  
 natthi dānaphalaṃ deva avaso deva viriyo  
  
       bālehi dānaṃ paññattaṃ paṇḍitehi paṭicchitaṃ  
 avāsā denti dhīrānaṃ bālā paṇḍitamānino  
  
    vāhati  machasaṃ    tāpiyā  machasaṃ  syā    maccāgacchanti  machasaṃ 
    caritassa  machasaṃ  vi    poriso  machasaṃ  syā 
  
               
              
       santime sassatā kāyā acchejjā avikopino    
 tejo paṭhavirāpo ca  vāyo sukhadukhañcime 
 jive ca sattime kāyā yesaṃ chettā  na vijjati  
  
       natthi hantā vā chettā vā haññare vāpi koci naṃ 
 antareneva  kāyānaṃ satthāni vitivatatare  
  
       yopāyaṃ  siramādāya paresaṃ nisitāsinā  
 na so chindati te kāye tattha pāpaphalaṃ kuto  
  
       cullāsiti māhakappe sabbe sujjhanti saṃsaraṃ  
 anāgate tambhi kāle saññatopi na sujjhati  
  
       caritvāpi bahuṃ bhadraṃ neva sujjhanti nāgete  
 pāpaṃ cepi bahuṃ katvā taṃ khaṇaṃ nātivattare  
  
       anupubbena no suddhi kappanaṃ cullasītiyā    
 niyatiṃ nātivattāma velantamiva sāgaro  
  
              
       kassapassa vaco sutvā alāto etadabravi  
 yathā bhadanto  bhaṇati mayhaṃpeteva ruccati  
  
       ahaṃpi purimaṃ jātiṃ dare saṃsaritattano  
 piṅgalo nāmahaṃ āsiṃ luddo goghātako pure  
  
       bārāṇasiyaṃ phitāya bahuṃ pāpaṃ kataṃ mayā  
 bahu mayhaṃ  hatā pāṇā mahisā  sukarā ajā  
  
       tato cuto idha jāto iddhe senāpatikule  
 natthi nūna phalaṃ pāpe  sohaṃ na nirayaṃ gato  
  
       athettha bījako nāma dāso āsi paḷaccarī     
 uposathaṃ upavasanto gaṇasantikupāgami  
  
    āpo machasaṃ  syā    chetā    antareyeva  machasaṃ  syā 
    yocāyaṃ  machasaṃ  syā    cullāsitiyā  machasaṃ  syā 
    yathā bhaṇanto bhaṇasi  machasaṃ yathābhaddanto  syā 
    mayā  machasaṃ syā    mabhiṃsā  machasaṃ  syā    pāpaṃ  machasaṃ 
     paṭiccharī  machasaṃ paṭajjari  syā 
  
               
       kassapassa vaco sutvā alāto bhāsitaṃ  
 passasanto muhuṃ uṇhaṃ rudaṃ assuti vattayi  
  
       tamanupucchi vedeho kimatthaṃ samma rodasi  kinte sutaṃ vā diṭṭhaṃ vā kiṃ maṃ vedesi vedanaṃ  
  
              
       vedehassa vaco sutvā khijako etadabravi  
 natthi me vedanā dukkhā vahārāja suṇohi me  
  
       ahampi purimaṃ jātiṃ sarāmi sukhamattano  
 sāketāhaṃ pure āsiṃ bhāvaseṭṭhi guṇe rato  
  
       sammato brāhmaṇibbānaṃ saṃvihāgarato suci  
 na cāpi pāpakaṃ kammaṃ sarāmi katamattano  
  
       tato cutāhaṃ vedeha idha jato duritthiyā  
 gabbambhi kumbadāsiyā yato jāto suduggato  
  
       evampi duggato santo samacariyaṃ adhiṭṭhito  
 upaḍḍhahāgaṃ bhattassa dadāmi yo me icchati  
  
       cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiṃ sadā upavasāmahaṃ    
 na cāpi bhute hiṃsāmi theyyañcāpi vivajjayiṃ  
  
       sabbameva hi nunetaṃ suciṇaṇaṃ bhavati nipphalaṃ  
 niratthaṃ maññadaṃ sīlaṃ alāto yatha bhāsati  
  
       kalimeva nūna gaṇhāmi asippo dhuttako  yathā  
 kaṭaṃ alāto gaṇhāti kitavo sikkhito yathā  
  
       dvāraṃ nappatipassāmi yena gacchāmi suggatiṃ  
 tasmā rāja parodāmi sutvā kassapabhāsitaṃ  
  
              
       khijakassa vāco sutvā rā aṅgātimabravi    
 natthi dvāraṃ sugatiyā niyatiṃ kaṅkha bījaka  
  
    ahaṃ  machasaṃ    dhuttiko  machasaṃ    aṅgati  machasaṃ 
  
               
       sukhaṃ vā yadivā dukkhaṃ niyatiyā  kira labbhathi  
 saṃsārasuddhi sabbesaṃ mā turittho anāgate  
  
       ahampi pubbe kalyāṇe brāhmaṇibbesu vyāvaṭo    
 vovahāramanusāsanto ratibhino tadantarā  
  
       punapi bhante dakkhemu saṅgati ce bavissati  
 idaṃ vatvāna vedeho paccagā sanivesanaṃ  
  
              
       tato ratyā vivasane upaṭṭhānambhi aṅgati  
 amacce sannipātetvā idaṃ vacanamabravi  
  
       candake me vimānasmiṃ sadā kāme vadhentu me  
 māmupagacchuṃ  atthesu guyhappākāsiyesu ca  
  
       vijayo ca sunāmo ca senāpati alātako  
 ete atthe nisidantu cohārakusalā tayo  
  
       idaṃ vatvāna vedeho kāme ca bahumaññatha  
 nacāpi brāhmaṇibbheṣu atthe kismiñci vyāvaṭo  
  
       tato dve sattarattassa vedehassatrajā piyā  
 rājakaññā rujā nāma dhātimātaramabravi  
  
       alaṅkarotha maṃ khippaṃ sakhiyo ca karontu me  
 suve paṇaṇaraso dibbo gacchaṃ issarasantike  
  
       tassā mālyaṃ abhihariṃsu candanañca mahārahaṃ  
 maṇisaṅkhamuttaratanaṃ nānāratte ca ambare  
  
       tañca sovaṇaṇatya pīṭhe nisinnaṃ bahukitthiyo  
 parikiriya asobhiṃsu  rujaṃ ruciravaṇaṇiniṃ  
  
              
       sā ca sakhimajjhagatā sabbābharaṇabhusitā  
 sateratā  abbhamiva candakaṃ pāvisi rujā  
  
    niyati  machasaṃ niyataṃ  syā    vāvaṭo  machasaṃ pāvaṭo  syā 
    māupagaccha  machasaṃ    amma  machasaṃ  syā 
    pasobhiṃsu  machasaṃ    saterita  machasaṃ sateritā  syā 
  
               
       upasaṅkamitvā vedehaṃ vanditvā vinaye ratā  
 suvaṇṇavikate  pīṭhe ekamantaṃ upāvisi  
  
              
       tañca disvāna vedeho accharānaṃva saṅgamaṃ  
 rujaṃ sakhijjhagataṃ idaṃ vacanamabravi  
  
       kacci bahuvidhaṃ mālyaṃ ovinitvā kumāriyo  
 kacci bahuvidhaṃ khajjaṃ sadā abhiharanti te  
  
       kacci bahuvidhaṃ mālyaṃ ovinitvā kumāriyo  
 gharake karotha paccekaṃ khiḍḍhāratiratā muhu  
       kena vā vikalaṃ tuyhaṃ kippaṃ  abhiharantu te  
 māno karassu kuḍḍamukhi api candasamambhipi    
  
       vedehassa vaco sutvā rujā pitaramabravi  
 sabbametaṃ mahārāja labbhatissarasantike  
  
       suve paṇaṇaraso dibbo sahasasaṃ āharantu me  
 yathādinnañca dassāmi dānaṃ sabbavaṇisuhaṃ  
  
       rujāya vacanaṃ sutvā rājā aṅgātimabravi  
 bahuṃ vināsitaṃ vittaṃ niratthaṃ aphalaṃ tayā  
  
       uposathaṃ vasaṃ niccaṃ antapānaṃ na bhuñjasi  
 niyatetaṃ abuttabbaṃ natthi puññaṃ abhuñajato  
  
              
       bijakopi hi sutvāna tadā kassapabhāsitaṃ  
 passasanto  muhuṃ uṇhaṃ rudaṃ assuni vatatyi  
  
       yāva ruje jivasi  no mā bhattamapanāmayi  
 natthi bhadde paro loko kiṃ niratthaṃ vihaññasi  
  
       vedehassa vaco sutvā rujā  ruciravaṇṇini  
 jānaṃ pubbāparaṃ dhammaṃ pitaraṃ etadabravi  
  
    khacite  machasaṃ  syā    ahu  machasaṃ  syā    kiṃ khippaṃ  machasaṃ syā 
    te  machasaṃ  syā    assasanto  machasaṃ    yāvarujejivamānā  machasaṃ syā    ruvā  machaṣaṃ syā 
  
               
       sutameva me pure āsi sakkhi diṭṭhamidaṃ  mayā  
 khālupasevi yo hoti bālova samapajjatha  
  
       muḷho hi muḷhamāgamma bhiyyo mohaṃ nigacchati  
 pakirūpaṃ alātena bījakena ca muyhituṃ  
  
              
       tvañca dve  sappañño dhīro atthassa kovido  
 kathaṃ bālehi sadisaṃ hīnaṃ diṭṭhiṃ  upāgami  
  
       sace hi saṃsārapathena sujjhati 
 niratthiyā pabbajjā guṇassa  
 kiṭova aggiṃ jalitaṃ apāpataṃ  
 uppajjati momuho naggabhāvaṃ  
  
       saṃsārasuddhiti pure niviṭṭhā 
 kammaṃ vidusenti  bahu ajānaṃ  
 pubbe kalī duggahitova atthā  
 dummocayā balisā ambujova  
  
       upamaṃ te karissāmi mahārāja navatthiyā  
 upamāyapidhekacce atthaṃ jānanti paṇḍitā  
  
       vāṇijānaṃ yathā nāvā appamāṇabharā garu  
 atibhāraṃ samādāya aṇaṇave avasidati  
  
       evameva naro pāpaṃ thoka thokampi ācinaṃ  
 atibhāraṃ samādāya niraye avasidati  
  
       na tāva bhāro paripuro  alātassa mahīpati  
 ācināti ca taṃ pāpaṃ yena gacchati duggatiṃ  
  
       pubbevassa kataṃ puññaṃ alātassa mahipati  
 tassesa  dve nissando yañceso labhate sukhaṃ  
  
       khiyatevassa  taṃ puññaṃ tathāhi aguṇe rato  
 ujumaggaṃ avāhāya   kummaggamanudhāvati  
  
    paccakkhaṃ diṭṭhaṃ  machasaṃ syā    devāsi  machasaṃ  syā 
    hinadiṭṭhaṃ  syā hinadiṭṭhi  machasaṃ    apāpitaṃ  machasaṃ 
    vidusanti bahu pajā  machasaṃ    attho  machasaṃ syā    patipuro  machasaṃ    tasesva  machasaṃ  syā 
    cassa  machasaṃ  syā     apihāya  machasaṃ  apāhāya  sīmu  
  
               
              
       tulā yathā paggahitā ohite tulamaṇḍale  
 unnameti tulāsisaṃ bhāre oropite sati  
  
       evameva naro puññaṃ thokathokampi ācinaṃ  
 saggātimāno dāsova khijako sātave  rato 
  
       yañcajja  bijako dāso dukkhaṃ passati antani  
 pubbe tassa  kataṃ pāpaṃ tameso paṭisevati  
  
       khiyatecassa taṃ pāpaṃ tathāhi vinaye rato  
 kassapañca samāpajja māhevuppatha  māgamā  
  
       yaṃ yaṃ hi rāja bhajati sataṃ vā yadi vā asaṃ  
 sīlavantaṃ visīlaṃ vā vasaṃ tasseva gacchati  
  
       yādisaṃ kurute mittaṃ yādisañcupasevati  
 sopi tādisako hoti sāhavāso hi tādiso  
  
              
       sevamāno sevamānaṃ samphuṭṭho samphusaṃ paraṃ  
 saro diddho  kalāpaṃva alittamupalimpati 
 upalepabhayā  dhīro neva pāpasakhā siyā  
  
       putimacchaṃ kusaggena yo naro upanayhati  
 kusāpi puti vāyanti evaṃ bālupasevanā  
  
       tagarañca  palāsena yo naro upanayhati  
 pattāpi surabhi vāyanti evaṃ dhirūpasevanā  
  
       tasmā palapuṭasseva  ñatvā sampāka  mantano  
 asante nopaseveyya sante seveyya paṇḍito 
 asanto nirayaṃ nenti santo pāpenti suggatiṃ  
  
       ahmipa jātiyo satta sare saṃsaritattano  
 anāgatāpi satteva yā gamissaṃ ito cutā  
  
    sādhave  machasaṃ    yamajja  machasaṃ syā vi 
    casasa  machasaṃ vassa  syā    mahevubbatha  machasaṃ 
    duṭṭho  machasaṃ  syā    upalimpa  machasaṃ 
    taggarañca  machasaṃ    pattapuṭasseva  machasaṃ 
    sapāka  machasaṃ 
  
               
       yā me sā santami jāti ahu pubbe janādhipa  
 kammāraputto magadhesu ahuṃ rājagahe pure  
  
       pāpaṃ sabhāyaṃ āgamma bahuṃ pāpaṃ kataṃ mayā  
 paradārassa heṭhento carimbha amarā viya  
  
       taṃ kammaṃ nihitaṃ aṭṭhā bhasmacchattova pāvako  
 atha aññehi kammehi ajāyiṃ vaṃsabhumiyaṃ  
  
              
       kosambiyaṃ soṭṭhikule iddhe phīte mahaddhane  
 ekaputto mahārāja niccaṃ sakkatapujito  
  
       tattha mittaṃ ṃasevissaṃ sahāyaṃ sātave  rataṃ  
 paṇḍitaṃ sutasampannaṃ so maṃ atthe nivesayi  
  
       cātuddasiṃ pañcadasiṃ bahuṃ rattimupāvasiṃ    
 taṃ kammaṃ nihitaṃ aṭṭhā nidhiva udakattike  
  
       atha pāpānaṃ kammānaṃ yametaṃ magadhe kataṃ 
 phalaṃ pariyāga taṃ  pacchā bhutvā duṭṭhavisaṃ yathā  
  
       tato cutāhaṃ vedeha roruve niraye ciraṃ  
 sakammanā  apaccisasaṃ taṃ saraṃ na sukhaṃ labhe  
  
       bahuvasasagaṇe tattha khepayitvā bahuṃ dukhaṃ  
 bheṇaṇakāṭa  ahuṃ rāja chakalo  uddhitapphalo  
  
              
       sātaputtā mayā vuḷhā piṭṭhiyā ca rathena ca  
 tassa kammassa nissando paradāragamanassa me  
  
       tato cutāhaṃ vedeha kapi āsiṃ brahāmane  
 nilicchita  phaloyeva yuthapena pagabbhinā  
 tassa kammassa nissando paradāragamanassa me  
  
       tato cutāhaṃ vedeha dasaṇeṇasu    pasu ahuṃ  
 nilicchito jave bhadro yoggahaṃ vuḷhaṃ ciraṃ mayā 
 tassa kammassa nissando paradāragamanassa me  
  
    sādhave  machasaṃ    mupāgami  machasaṃ    pariyāgamaṃ  machasaṃ 
    sakammunā  machasaṃ  syā    bhinnāgato  machasaṃ  syā 
    chagalo  machaṣaṃ  syā    niluñcita  machasaṃ  syā niliñcita  vi nilicchita  simu    assanesu machasaṃ 
  
               
       tato cutāhaṃ vedeha vajjisu kulamāgamā  
 nevitthi na pumā āsiṃ manussatte sudullahe  
 tassa kammassa nissando paradāragamanassa me  
  
       tato cutāhaṃ vedeha ajāyiṃ nandane vane  
 bhavane tāvatiṃsāhaṃ accharā kāmavaṇṇini  
  
       vicintavattābharaṇā āvuttamaṇikuṇḍalā  
 kusalā naccagitatassa sakkassa paricārikā  
  
       tattha ṭhitāhaṃ vedeha sarāmi jātiyo imā  
 anāgatepi satteva yā gamissaṃ ito cutā  
  
       parāyāgatantaṃ kusalaṃ yaṃ me kosambiyaṃ kataṃ  
 deve ceva manusse ca sandhāvissaṃ ito cutā  
  
       santa jacco  mahārāja niccaṃ sakkatapujitā  
 thibhāvāpi  na muccissaṃ chaṭṭhāni gatiyo imā  
  
              
       santamiva gati deva devaputto mahiddhiko  
 puma devo bhavissāmi devakāyasamimuttamo  
  
       ajjāpi santānamayaṃ mālaṃ ganthenti nandane  
 devaputto javo nāma yo me mālaṃ paṭicchati  
  
       muhutto viya so dibbo imāni vassāni soḷasa  
 rattindivo ca so dibbo mānusiṃ saradosataṃ  
  
       iti kammāni anventi asaṅkheyyāpi jātiyo  
 kalyāṇaṃ yadi vā pāpaṃ nahi kammaṃ panassati  
  
              
       yo icche puriso hotuṃ jātijātiṃ punappunaṃ  
 paradāraṃ vivajjayye dhotapādova kaddamaṃ  
  
       yā icche puriso hotuṃ jātijātiṃ punappunaṃ  
 sāmikaṃ apacāyeyya indaṃva paricārikā  
  
       yo icche dibbabhogañca dibbaṃ āyuṃ yasaṃ sukhaṃ  
 pāpāni parivajjetvā tividhaṃ dhammamācare  
  
    jaccā  machasaṃ  syā    itthibhāvā  machasaṃ  syā 
    pumādevo  machasaṃ  syā  vi  
  
               
       kayena vācā manasā appamatto vicakkhaṇo  
 antano hoti atthāya itthi vā yadi vā pumā  
  
       ye kecime manujā jivaloke 
 yasassino sabbasamantabhogā  
 asaṃsayaṃ tehi pure suciṇaṇaṃ  
 kammassakāse puthu pabbasattā 
  
       iṅghānucintesi sayampi deva 
 kuto nidānā te imā janinda  
 yā te imā accharāsantikāsā 
 alaṅkatā kañcanajālachantā  
  
              
       iccevaṃ pitaraṃ kaññā rujā tosesi aṅgatiṃ  
 muḷhassa maggamācikkhi dhammamakkhāsi subbatā  
  
              
       athāgamā brahmalokā nārado mānusiṃ  pajaṃ  
 jambudīpaṃ avekkhanto addā  rājānamaṅkatiṃ  
  
       tato patiṭṭhā pāsāde vedehassa puratthato    
 tañca disvā anuppantaṃ rujā isimavandatha  
  
              
       athāsanambhā oruyha rājā vyambhatimānaso  
 nāradaṃ paripucchanto idaṃ vacanamabravi  
  
       kuto nu āgacchasi devavaṇṇi 
 obhāsayaṃ saṃvaraṃ candimāva  
 akkhāhi me pucchito nāmagottaṃ  
 kathaṃ taṃ jānatti manussaloke  
  
       ahaṃ hi devato idāni emi 
 obhāsayaṃ saṃvaraṃ  candimāva  
 akkhāmi te pucchito nāmagottaṃ 
 jānanti maṃ nārado kassapo ca    
  
       acchariyarūpaṃ  vata  yādisañca 
 vohāsayaṃ gacchasi tiṭṭhasi ca  
 pucchāmi taṃ nārada etamatthaṃ 
 atha kena vaṇṇena tavāyamiddhi  
  
    mānusaṃ  machasaṃ    addasā  machasaṃ addasa  syā 
    purakkhato  machasaṃ  syā  vi    sabbadisā  machasaṃ  syā 
    vāti  machasaṃ  syā    accherarūpaṃ  machasaṃ 
    tava  machasaṃ  syā  
               
              
       saccañca dhammo ca damo ca cāgo 
 guṇā mamete pakatā purāṇā  
 teheva dhammehi susevitehi 
 manojavo yenakāmaṃ gamosmi    
  
       acachariya  mācikkhasi puññasiddhiṃ 
 sace hi ete tvaṃ yathā vadesi  
 pucchāmi taṃ nārada etamatthaṃ 
 puṭṭho ca me sādhu viyākarohi  
  
       pucchassu maṃ rāja tavesa attho 
 yaṃ paṃsayaṃ kuruse bhumipāla 
 ahaṃ taṃ nisasaṃsayataṃ gamemi  
 nayehi ñāyehi ca hetuhi ca  
  
              
       pucchāmi taṃ nārada etamatthaṃ 
 puṭṭho ca me nārada mā musā bhaṇa  
 atthi nu devā pitaro nu atthi 
 loko paro atthi jano yamāhu  
  
       attheva devā pitaro ca atthi 
 loko paro atthi jano yamāhu  
 kāmesu giddhā ca narā pamuḷhā 
 lokaṃ paraṃ na vidu mohayuttā  
  
       atthiti ce nārada saddahāsi 
 nivesanaṃ paraloke matānaṃ  
 idheva me pañcasatāni dehi 
 dassāmi te paraloke sahassaṃ  
  
       dajjemu kho pañcasatāni bhoto 
 jaññamu ce silavantaṃ vadaññaṃ  
 ludadaṃ taṃ bhontaṃ niraye vasantaṃ 
 ko codaye paraloke sahassaṃ  
  
       idheva yo hoti adhammasilo 
 pāpāvāro  alaso luddakammo  
 na paṇḍitā tasmiṃ iṇaṃ dadanti 
 nahi āgamo hoti pathāvidhambhā  
  
    gatosmi  machasaṃ  syā    acchera  machasaṃ    pāpanaro  machasaṃ 
  
               
              
       dakkhañca posaṃ manujā viditvā 
 uṭṭhāhakaṃ  silavantaṃ vadaññuṃ  
 sayameva bhogehi nimantayanti 
 kammaṃ karitvā putamāharesi  
  
       ito gato  dakkhasi tattha rāja 
 kākolasaṅghebhipi kaḍḍhamānaṃ    
 taṃ khajjamānaṃ niraye vasantaṃ 
 kākehi gijjhehi ca seṇakehi 
 sañachintagattaṃ ruhiraṃ savantaṃ 
 ko codaye paraloke sahasasaṃ  
  
              
       andhaṃtamaṃ tattha na candasuriyā 
 nirayo sadā tumulo ghorarūpo  
 sā neva ratti na divā paññāyati 
 tathāvidhe ko vicare dhanatthiko  
  
       sabalo ca sāmo ca duve supāṇā  
 pavaddhakāyā balino sahantā  
 khādanti dantehi ayomayehi ito panuṇaṇaṃ paralokapantaṃ  
  
       taṃ khajjamānaṃ niraye vasantaṃ 
 luddehi vāḷehi aghammigehi ca  
 saṃchintaganataṃ ruhiraṃ savantaṃ 
 ko codaye paraloke sahassaṃ  
  
              
       usuhi sattihi sunissitāhi 
 hananti vijjhanti ca pavavamittā 
 kāḷupakāḷā nirayamhi ghore 
 pubbe naraṃ dukkatakammakāriṃ  
  
       taṃ haññamānaṃ niraye vajantaṃ 
 kucchismiṃ passasmiṃ viphālitudaraṃ 
 saṃchinanagattaṃ ruhiraṃ savantaṃ 
 ko codeye paraloke sahassaṃ  
  
    uṭṭhānakaṃ  machasaṃ  syā    cuto  machasaṃ  syā 
    vikassamānaṃ  machasaṃ syā    suvāṇa  machasaṃ  syā 
    patantaṃ  machasaṃ  syā 
  
               
       santi usu tomarabheṇḍivālā  
 vividhāvudhaṃ vassati tattha devo  
 patanti aṅgāramivacavimanto 
 silāsani vasasti luddakamme  
  
       uṇho ca vāto nirayambhi duddaho 
 na tahiṃ sukha ṃlabbhati ittarampi  taṃ taṃ vidhāvantamalenamāturaṃ 
 ko codaye paraloke sahassaṃ  
  
              
       sandhāvamānaṃ taṃ rathesu yuttaṃ 
 sajotibhūtaṃ  paṭhaviṃ kamantaṃ  
 patodalaṭṭhihi  suvodiyantaṃ  
 ko codaye pariloke sahassaṃ  
  
       tamāruhantaṃ khurasañcitaṃ giriṃ 
 vibhiṃsanaṃ pajjalitaṃ bhayānakaṃ  
 sañachinnagattaṃ ruhiraṃ savantaṃ 
 ko codaye paraloke sahassaṃ  
  
       tamārubhantaṃ pabbatasantikāsaṃ 
 aṅgārarāsiṃ jalitaṃ bhayānakaṃ  
 saṃdaḍḍhagattaṃ  kapaṇaṃ rudantaṃ 
 ko codaye paraloke sahassaṃ  
  
       abbhakūṭasamā uccā kaṇṭakāpavitā  dumā  
 ayomayehi tikkhehi naralohitapāyihi  
  
       tamāruhanti nāriyo narā ca paradāragu  
 coditāsanti hatthehi yamaniddesakārihā  
  
       tamāruhantaṃ nirayaṃ simbaliṃ ruhiramakkhitaṃ  
 vidaḍḍhakāyaṃ vitavaṃ āturaṃ gāḷhavedanaṃ  
  
       passasantaṃ muhuṃ uṇhaṃ pubbakammāparādhikaṃ    
 dumaggaviṭapaggabhathaṃ  ko taṃ yāveyya taṃ dhanaṃ  
  
    bhiṇavivālā  machasaṃ    jotabhūtaṃ  machasaṃ    paṭodalaṭṭhīhi  machasaṃ 
    suvocayantaṃ  machasaṃ  syā    sudaḍḍhagattaṃ    kaṇṭakāni vitā  machasaṃ  syā vi     pubbakama parādhitaṃ  machasaṃ    dummagge vitavaṃgattaṃ  machasaṃ  syā 
  
               
              
       abbhukuṭasamā uccā asipattāvitā  dumā  
 ayomayehi tikkhehi naralohitapāyihi  
  
       tamānupattaṃ  asipattapādapaṃ 
 asihi tikkhehi ca chijjamānaṃ    
 saṃchinnagantaṃ ruhiraṃ savantaṃ 
 ko codaye paraloke sahassaṃ  
  
       tato nikkhantamantaṃ  taṃ asipattanirayā  dukhā    
 sampatitaṃ cetaraṇiṃ  ko taṃ yāceyya taṃ dhanaṃ  
  
       kharā khārodikā  tattā duggā vetaraṇi nadī  
 ayopokkharasañachantā tikkhapattetahi sandati  
  
       tattha sañachintagattaṃ taṃ vuyhantaṃ ruhiramakkhitaṃ  
 vetaraññe  anālambe ko taṃ yāceyya taṃ dhanaṃ  
  
       vedhāmi rukkho viya chijjamāno 
 disaṃ na jānāmi pamuḷhasaññi     
 bhayasānutappāmi mahā ca   me bhayaṃ 
 sutthāna gāthā   tava bhāsitā ise  
  
       āditte vārimajjhaṃva dipaṃvogherivaṇṇave  
 andhakāre pajjoto tvaṃ nosi saraṇaṃ ise  
  
              
       atthañca dhammañcanusāsa maṃ ise 
 atitamaddhā aparādhitaṃ mayā  
 ācikkha me nārada suddhimaggaṃ 
 yathā ahaṃ   no niraye   pateyyaṃ  
  
       yathā ahu dhataraṭṭho vessāmitto aṭṭhako yāmataggi   
 usinnaro   cāpi sivi ca rā paricārakā  samaṇabrāhmaṇānaṃ  
  
    asipatta  asipattāni citā  machasaṃ  syā vi     saññe  machaṣaṃ  syā 
    tamāruhantaṃ  machasaṃ  syā     mahāva mehayā  machasaṃ  syā 
    pabhijja  machasaṃ     kathā  machasaṃ 
    nikkhantaṃ patattaṃ  machasaṃ     ayaṃ  machasaṃ 
    asipatta citā  machasaṃ     nirayaṃ  machasaṃ 
    dumā  machasaṃ     yamadanti  syā 
    vettaraṇīṃ  machasaṃ     usindhatrā  machasaṃ 
    barodanā  machasaṃ  syā     parivārikā  machasaṃ  syā 
    vettaraññe  machasaṃ  syā  vi  
  
               
       ete caññe ca rājāno ye sakkavisayaṃ  gatā  
 adhammaṃ parivajjetvā dhammaṃ cara mahipati  
  
       antahatthā ca te vyambhe ghosayantu pure tava  
 ko chāto ko ca tasito ko mālaṃ ko vilepanaṃ  
 nānārattānaṃ vatthāṃ ko naggo paridahessati  
  
       ko patthe chattamādeti pādukā ca  mudu subhā  
 iti sāyañca pato ca ghosayantu pure tava  
  
       jiṇaṇaṃ posaṃ gavāsasaññaca māssu yuñaji  yathā pure  
 parihārañca dajjasi adhikārakato khali  
  
              
       kayo te rathasaññāto manosārathiko lahu  
 avihiṃsāsāritakkho saṃvibhāgapaṭicchado  
  
       pādasaññamanemiyo hatthasaññamapakkharo  
 kucchisaññamanabbhanto vācāsaññamakujano  
  
       saccavākyasamattaṅgo apesuññasusaññato  
 girāsakhilanelaṅgo mitabhāṇisilesito 
  
       saddhālohasusaṅkhāro nivātañajalikubbaro  
 atthaddhatānatisākho  silasaṃvaranandhano  
  
       akodhanamunagghāti dhammapaṇḍarachattako  
 bāhusaccamapālambo  ṭhitavittamupādhiyo  
  
    sagga  machasaṃ  syā    paradabhissati  machasaṃ  syā    kopāhanā ca  vi    yuñacha  machaṣaṃ  syā    makujjaro  machasaṃ    athaddhatāntisāko  machasaṃ    supālambo mupālambo  machasaṃ  syā 
  
               
       kālaññatāvittasāro vesārajjatidaṇḍako  
 nivātavutti yottako  anatimānayugo lahu  
  
       alinacittasanthāro  vaddhasevirajohato    
 satipatodo dhirassa dhiti yogo ca rasamiyo  
  
       mano dantapathatveti  samadantehi vāhibhī    
 icchā lobho ca kummaggo ujumagegā ca saññamo 
  
              
       rūpe sadde rase gandhe vāhanassa padhāvato  
 paññā ākoṭani rāja tathe attāva sārathi  
  
       sace etena yānena samacariyā daḷhā dhitī  
 sabbakāmaduho rāja na jātu nirayaṃ vaje  
  
              
       alāto devadatetāsi sunāmo āsi bhaddaji  
 vijayo sāriputtosi moggallānosi khijako  
  
       sunakakhanto licchaviputto guṇo āsi acelako  
 ānando ca rujā  āsi yā rājānaṃ pasādayi  
  
       uruvelakassapo rājā pāpadiṭṭhi tadā ahu  
 mahābrahmā bodhisatto evaṃ dhāretha jātakanti  
 mahānāradakassapajātakaṃ sattamaṃ  
  
    yotataṅgo  machasaṃ    sandhā  machasaṃ    buddhivi  machasaṃ 
    dantaṃ pathaṃ neti  machasaṃ    vājihi  machasaṃ    sā  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
    vidhurajātakaṃ 
              
       yo kopaneyye na karoti kopaṃ 
 na kujjhati sappuriso kadāvi  
 kuddhopi yo nāvikaroti kopaṃ 
 taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇaṃ āhu loke  
  
              
       ūnudaro yo sahate jighacchaṃ 
 danto tapassi mitapāṇabhojano  
 āhārahetu na karoti pāpaṃ 
 taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇaṃ āhu loke  
  
       khiḍḍaṃ ratiṃ vippajahetva bbaṃ 
 na cālikaṃ bhāsati kiñci loke  
 vibhusanaṭṭhānā virato methunasmā 
 taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇaṃ āhu loke  
  
              
       pariggahaṃ lohadhammañca sabbaṃ 
 ye ve pariññāya pariccajanati  
 dantaṃ ṭhitantaṃ amamaṃ nirāsaṃ 
 taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇaṃ āhu loke  
  
       pucchāma kantāraṃ anomapaññaṃ 
 gāthāsu no viggaho atthi jato  
 chindajja kaṅkhaṃ vivikicchitāni 
 tayajja kaṅkhaṃ vitaremu sabbe  
  
              
       ye paṇḍitā atthadassā bhavanti 
 bhāsanti te yoniso tattha kāle  
 kathannu gāthānaṃ ahāsitānaṃ 
 atthaṃ nayeyyuṃ kusalā janinda  
  
       kathaṃ bhave bhāsati nāgarājā 
 kathaṃ pana garuḷo cenateyyo  
 gandhabbarājā pana kiṃ vadeti 
 kathaṃ pana kurūnaṃ rājaseṭṭho  
  
       khantiṃ have bhāsati nāgarājā 
 appahāraṃ garuḷo venateyyo  
 gandhabbarājā rativippahānaṃ 
 akiñcanaṃ kurunaṃ rājaseṭṭho  
  
               
              
       sabbāni etāni subhāsitāni 
 na hettha dubbāsitamatthi kiñci  
 yasmiñca etāni patiṭṭitāni 
 arāva nābhyā susamohitāni  
 catubbhi dhammehi samaṅgibhūtaṃ 
 taṃ ve naraṃ samaṇaṃ āhu loke  
  
       tuvannu seṭṭho tvamanuttarosi 
 tvaṃ dhammagu dhammavidu sumedho 
 paññāya pañhaṃ samadhiggahetvā  
 acchecchi dhīro vicikicchitāni 
 acchecchi kaṅkhaṃ vicikicchitāni 
 cundo yathā nāgadantaṃ kharena  
  
       niluppalāhaṃ vimalaṃ anagghaṃ 
 vatthaṃ imaṃ dhumasamānavaṇaṇaṃ  
 pañhassa veyyākaraṇena tuṭṭho 
 dadāmi te dhammapujāya dhira  
  
       suvaṇṇamālaṃ satapattaphullaṃ 
 sakesaraṃ ratanasahassamaṇḍitaṃ  
 pañhassa veyyākareṇena tuṭṭho 
 dadāmi te dhammapujāya dhira  
  
       maṇiṃ anagghaṃ ruciraṃ pabhassaraṃ 
 kaṇṭhāvasannaṃ maṇibhusitaṃ me  
 pañhassa veyyākareṇena tuṭṭho 
 dadāmi te dhammapujāya dhira  
  
       gavaṃ sahassaṃ usabhañca nāgaṃ 
 ājaññayutte ca rathe dasa ime  
 pañhassa veyyākareṇena tuṭṭho 
 dadāmi te dhammapujāya dhira  
  
              
       paṇḍu kisiyāsi dubbalā 
 vaṇṇarūpaṃ na tavedisaṃ  pure  
 vimale akkhāhi pucchitā  
 kīdisi  tuyhaṃ sariravedanā  
  
              
       dhammo manujesu māninaṃ 
 dohaḷo nāma janinda vuccati  
 dhammāhaṭaṃ  nāgakuñajara 
 vidhurassa hadayābhipatthaye  
  
    tavedisi  machasaṃ  vi    pucchito  machasaṃ    kidisā  vi 
    dhammābhataṃ  machasaṃ  vi  
  
               
       candaṃ kho tvaṃ dohaḷāyasi  
 suriyaṃ vā athavāpi mālutaṃ  
 dullabhe  hi vidhurassa dassane  
 ko vidhura idhamānayissati  
  
              
       kinnu tāta tuvaṃ pajjhāyasi 
 padumaṃ hatthagataṃva te mukhaṃ  
 kiṃ dummanarūposi issara 
 mā tvaṃ soci amittatāpanā  
  
       mātā hi tava irandati  
 vidhurassa hadayaṃ dhaniyati  
 dullabhe hi vidhurassa dassane 
 ko vidhuraṃ idhamānayissati  
  
       bhattupariyesanaṃ  cara 
 yo vidhuraṃ idhamānayissati  
 pituno ca sā sutvāna vākyaṃ 
 rattiṃ nikkhamma avassutiṃ cari  
  
              
       ke gandhabbe ca rakkhase 
 nāge kimpurise ca mānuse  
 ke paṇḍite sabbakāmade 
 dīgharattaṃ bhattā me bhavissati  
  
       assāsa hessāmi te pati 
 bhattā hessāmi anindalocane  
 paññā hi mama  tathā vidhā 
 assāsa hessasi bhariyā mamaṃ  
  
              
       atha naṃ avacāsi  irandati 
 pubbapathānugatena cetasā  
 ehi gacchāma pitu mamantike 
 esova te etavatthaṃ pavakkhati  
  
       alaṃkatā suvasanā mālini candanussadā  
 yakkhaṃ hatthe gahetvāna pitu santikamupāgami  
  
       nāgavara vaco suṇohi me 
 patirūpaṃ paṭipajja suṅkiyaṃ  
 patthemi ahaṃ irandatiṃ  
 tāya samaṅgī   karohi me tuvaṃ   
  
    cimale dohaḷāyasi  machasaṃ    mamaṃ  machasaṃ 
    dullabhaṃ  machasaṃ    mama  machasaṃ 
    dassanaṃ  machasaṃ    avacāsi puṇaṇakaṃ  machasaṃ 
    irandhati  machasaṃ    irandhatiṃ  machasaṃ 
    taṃ bhattāraṃ  machasaṃ  syā  vi     samaṅgi  machasaṃ     maṃ machasaṃ 
  
               
       sataṃ hatthi sataṃ assā sataṃ assatarirathā  
 sataṃ vaḷabhiyo puṇaṇā nānāratanassa kevalā 
 te nāga paṭipajjassu dhitaraṃ dehi irandatiṃ  
  
       yāva āmantaye ñāti mitte ca suhadaṃ janaṃ    
 anāmantakataṃ kammaṃ taṃ pacchāmanutappati  
  
              
       tato so varuṇo nāgo pavisitvā nivesanaṃ  
 bhariyaṃ āmantayitvāna idaṃ vacanamabuvi  
  
       ayaṃ so puṇṇako yakkho yācatī maṃ irandatiṃ  
 bahunā vittalābhena tassa dema piyaṃ mamaṃ  
  
       na dhanena na vintena labbhā ambhaṃ irandati  
 sace hi vo  hadayaṃ paṇḍitassa 
 dhammena laddhā idhamāhareyya 
 etena vittena kumāri labbhā 
 nāññaṃ dhanaṃ uttariṃ patthayāma  
       tato so varuṇo nāgo nikkhamitvā nivesanaṃ  
 puṇaṇakāmantayitvāna idaṃ canamabravi  
  
       na dhanena na vintena labbhā ambhaṃ irandati  
 sace tuvaṃ hadayaṃ paṇḍitassa 
 dhammena laddhā idhamāhareyya 
 etena vittena kumāri labbhā 
 nāññaṃ dhanaṃ uttariṃ patthayāma  
       yaṃ paṇḍito teyyake vadanti loke 
 tameva bāloti punāhu aññe 
 akkhāhi me vippavadanti ettha  
 kaṃ paṇḍitaṃ nāga tuvaṃ vadesi  
  
              
       koravyarājassa dhanañajayassa 
 yadi te suto vidhuro nāma kattā  
 ānehi taṃ paṇḍitaṃ dhammaladdhā 
 irandati paddhacarā  te hotu  
  
       idañca sutvā varūṇassa vākyaṃ  
 uṭṭhāya yakkho paramappatito  
 tattheva santo purisaṃ asaṃsi 
 ānehi ājaññamidheva yuttaṃ  
  
    suhadajjane  machasaṃ    sace ca kho  machasaṃ  syā    paṭṭhācarā  machasaṃ  syā 
               
       jātarūpamayā kaṇaṇā kāvambhamayā  khurā  
 jambonadassa pākassa suvaṇaṇassa uracchado  
  
       devavāhavahaṃ yānaṃ assamāruyha puṇaṇako 
 alaṅkato kappitakesamassu 
 pakkāmi vehāsayamantalikkhe  
  
              
       sa puṇaṇako kāmavegena  giddho 
 irandatiṃ nāgakaññaṃ jigiṃsaṃ 
 gananvāna taṃ bhūtapatiṃ yasassiṃ 
 iccabravi vesasvaṇaṃ kuveraṃ  
  
       bhogavatināmamandire 
 vāsā bhiraññavatiti vuccati  
 nagare nimamite kañcanamaye 
 maṇḍalassa uragassa niṭṭhitaṃ  
  
       aṭṭālakā  oṭṭhagīviyo 
 lohitaṅkassa masāragallino  
 pāsādettha silāmayā 
 sovaṇaṇaratanne chāditā  
  
       ambā tilakā ca jambuyo 
 santapaṇaṇā mucalindaketakā    
 piyakā  uddālakā sahā 
 uparibhaddakā sinduvārakā  
  
       campeyyakā nāgamālikā 
 bhaginimālā athamettha koliyā  
 ete dumā parināmitā 
 sobhayanti uragassa mandiraṃ  
  
       khajjurettha silāmayā 
 sovaṇaṇadhuvapupphitā  
 bahu yattha vasatopapātiko 
 nāgarājā varuṇo mahiddhiko  
  
       tassa komārikā bhariyā 
 vimalā kañcanavelliviggahā  
 kāḷā taruṇāva uggatā 
 pucimandatthani cārudassanā  
  
    kācambhica  machasaṃ  syā    kāmarāgena  machasaṃ  syā 
    aṭṭaḷahatā  machasaṃ    keṭakā  machasaṃ 
    piyaṅgu uddālakā setā piyaṅgukā  machasaṃ  syā 
    pāribhaddakā sindhacāritā  machasaṃ    mandire  machasaṃ 
  
               
       lākhārasarattasucchavi 
 kāṇikārova nivātapupphito  
 tidivokacarāva accharā 
 vijjutabbhaghanāva nissaṭā  
  
              
       sā dohaḷini sucimbhitā 
 vidhurassa bhadayaṃ dhaniyati  
 taṃ tesaṃ dadāmi  issara 
 tena te denti irandatiṃ mamaṃ  
  
              
       sa puṇṇako bhūtapatiṃ yasassiṃ 
 āmantaya  vesasvaṇaṃ kuveraṃ  
 tattheva santo purisaṃ asaṃsi 
 ānehi ājaññamidheva yuttaṃ  
  
       jātarūpamayā kaṇaṇā kācambhamayā  khurā  
 jambonadassa pākassa suvaṇaṇassa uracchado  
  
       devavāhavahaṃ yānaṃ assamāruyha puṇaṇako  
 alaṅkato kappītakesamassu 
 pakkāmi vehāsayamantalikkhe  
  
       so āgamā  rājagahaṃ surammaṃ 
 aṅgassa rañño nagaraṃ durāyutaṃ    
 pahutabhakkhaṃ bahuantapānaṃ 
 masakkasāraṃ viya vāsavassa  
  
              
       mayurakoñcāgaṇasampaghuṭṭhaṃ 
 dijābhighuṭṭhaṃ dijasaṅghasevitaṃ  
 nānāsakuntā  bhirudaṃ subhaṅganaṃ 
 pupphābhikiṇṇaṃ himavaṃva  pabbataṃ  
  
       sa puṇṇako vepullamābhirucchi  
 siluccayaṃ kimpurisānuciṇṇaṃ  
 atvesamāno maṇiratanaṃ uḷāraṃ 
 tamaddasā pabbatakūṭamajjhe  
  
    demi  machasaṃ    āmantiya  machasaṃ    kāvambhica  machasaṃ 
    aggamā  machasaṃ    durāyuttaṃ  machasaṃ    sakuntā  machasaṃ 
    himavanta  machasaṃ    mābhiruyhi  machasaṃ 
  
               
       disvā maṇiṃ pabhassaraṃ jātivantaṃ 
 dhanāharaṃ  maṇīratanaṃ uḷāraṃ  
 daddallamānaṃ yasasā yasassinaṃ 
 obhāsati vijjurivantalikkhe  
  
       tamaggahī veḷuriyaṃ mahagghaṃ 
 manoharaṃ nāma mahānubhāvaṃ  
 ājaññamāruyha anomavaṇṇo 
 pakkāmi vehāsayamantalikkhe  
  
              
       so āgamā nagaraṃ indapattaṃ 
 oruyha cāgañchi  sabhaṃ kurūnaṃ  
 samāgame ekasataṃ samagge 
 avebhattha yakkho avikampamāno  
  
       ko nīdha raññaṃ varamābhijeti 
 kamābhijeyyāma varaṃdhanena    
 kamanuttaraṃ ratanavaraṃ jināma 
 ko vāpi no jeti varaṃdhanena  
  
       kuhiṃ nu raṭṭhe tava jātubhūmi 
 na koravyasseva vaco tavedaṃ  
 abhihosa no vaṇaṇanibhāya sabbe 
 akkhāhi me nāmañca bandhave ca  
  
              
       kaccāyano māṇavakosmi rajā 
 anunanāmo iti mavhayanti  aṅgesu me ñātayo bandhavā ca 
 akkhena devasmi idhānupatto  
  
       ki māṇavassa ratanāni atthi 
 ye taṃ jinanto hare akkhadhutto  
 bahuni rañño ratanāni atthi 
 te  tvaṃ daḷiddo kathamavhayesi    
  
       manoharo nāma maṇi mamāyaṃ 
 dhanāharo  maṇiratanaṃ uḷāraṃ 
 imañca ājaññaṃ amittatāpanaṃ 
 etaṃ me jetvā hare akkhadhutto  
  
    manoharaṃ  machasaṃ    orūyhupāgacchi  machasaṃ  syā    varaddhanena  machasaṃ 
    yo  machasaṃ    mavhayasi  machasaṃ    manoharā  machasaṃ 
  
               
       eko maṇi māṇava kiṃ karissati 
 ājāniyeko pana kiṃ karissati  
 bahuni rañño maṇiratanāni atthi 
 ājāniyā vātajavā anappakā  
 dohaḷakaṇḍo 
  
              
       idañca me maṇiratanaṃ passa tvaṃ dipaduttama  
 itthinaṃ viggahā vettha purisānañca viggahā  
  
       migānaṃ viggahā vettha sakuṇānañca viggahā  
 nāgarāje supaṇeṇa ca  maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
       hatthānikaṃ rathānikaṃ asse patti dhajāni ca    
 caturaṅginiṃ imaṃ senaṃ maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
       hatthāruhe anikaṭṭhe rathike patatikārike  
 balaggāni viyūḷhāni maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
              
       puraṃ uddāpasampannaṃ  bahupākāratoraṇaṃ  
 siṅghāṭakesu bhumiyo maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
       esikā parikhāyo ca palighaṃ aggalāni ca  
 aṭṭālake ca dvāre ca maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
       passa toraṇamaggesu nānādijagaṇā bahu  
 haṃsā koñcā mayurā ca cakkavākā ca kukkubhā  
  
       kuṇālakā bahū citrā sikhaṇḍī jivañjivakā    
 nānādijagaṇākiṇṇaṃ maṇimhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
       passa nagaraṃ supākāraṃ abbhutaṃ lomahaṃsanaṃ  
 samussitadhajaṃ rammaṃ suvaṇṇavālukasanthataṃ  
  
       passa  tvaṃ paṇaṇasālāyo vibhattā bhāgasomitā  
 nivesane nivese ca sandhibyubhe pathaddhiyo    
  
       pānāgāre ca soṇḍe ca suṇā  odaniyāgharā  
 vesī ca gaṇikāyo ca maṇimhi passa nimamitaṃ 
  
    supaṇṇāva  machasaṃ    vammine  machasaṃ  syā    uddhāpa  machasaṃ aṭṭāla  syā    jivajivakā  machasaṃ  syā    passettha  machasaṃ  syā 
    pathatthiyo  syā pathaṭṭhiyo  machasaṃ    saddā  syā puvā  machasaṃ 
  
               
       mālākāre ca rajake gandhike atha dussike  
 suvaṇṇakāre maṇikāre maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
       āḷāriye ca  sudace naṭanaṭṭakagāyake    
 pāṇissare kumbhathunike maṇimhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
              
       passa bheri mutiṅgā ca saṅkhā paṇavadeṇḍimā    
 sabbañca tālāvacaraṃ maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
       sammatālañca viṇañca naccagītaṃ suvāditaṃ  
 turiyatāḷitasaṃghuṭṭhaṃ maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
       laṅghikā muṭṭhikā cettha māyākārā ca sobhiyā  
 cetālike ca jalle ca maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
       samajjā cettha vattanti ākiṇaṇā naranārihi  
 mañcātimañce bhumiyo maṇimhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
       passa malle samajjasmiṃ poṭhente diguṇaṃ bhujaṃ  
 nihate nihatamāne ca maṇimhi passa nimmītaṃ  
  
       passa pabbatapādesu nānāmigagaṇā bahu  
 sihavyagghavarāhā ca acchakokataracchayo  
  
       palasatā ca gavajā ca mahisā rohitā rurū  
 phaṇeyyā ca varāhā ca gaṇino niṅkasukarā  
  
       kadalimigā bahu citrā khiḷārā sasakaṇṇakā  
 nānāmiggaṇākiṇaṇaṃ maṇimhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
              
       najjāyo supatitthāyo soṇṇavālukasanthatā  
 acchā savanti ambuni macchagumbanisevitā  
  
       kumbhilā makarā cettha suṃsumārā cakacchapā  
 pāṭhinā pāvusā macchā valajā mañcarohitā 
  
    āḷārike  machasaṃ  syā    gāyino  machasaṃ gāyine  syā 
    dindimā  machasaṃ    taracchake  machasaṃ 
  
               
  
       nānādumagaṇākiṇṇā nānādijagaṇāyutā  
 veḷuriyaphalakarodāyo  maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
       passettha pokkharaṇiyo suvibhattā catuddisā  
 nānādijagaṇākiṇṇā puthulomanisevitā    
  
       samanodakasampannaṃ mahiṃ sāgarakuṇḍalaṃ  
 upetaṃ vanarājehi  maṇimbhi passa nimmitaṃ  
  
       purato videhe passa goyāniye ca pacchato  
 kuruyo jambudipañca maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
       passa candāñca suriyañca obhāsente  catuddisā  
 sineruṃ anupariyanne maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
       sineruṃ himavantañca sāgarañca mahiddhikaṃ    
 cattāro ca mahārāja maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
       ārāme vanagumbe ca pāṭiye ca  siluccaye  
 ramme kimpurisākiṇṇe maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
       phārusakaṃ cittalataṃ missakaṃ nandanaṃ vanaṃ  
 vejayantañca pāsādaṃ maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
       sudhammaṃ tāvatiṃsañca pāricchattañca pupphitaṃ  
 pharāvaṇaṃ nāgarājaṃ maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
       passettha devakaññāyo nabhā vijjurivuggatā  
 nandane vicarantiyo maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
       passettha devakaññāyo devaputtapalohinī  devaputte caramāne maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
              
       parosahassapāsāde veḷuriyaphalakatthate  
 pajjalantaina vaṇṇena maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
    veḷuriyakarodāyo  machasaṃ    puthulomacchasevitā  machasaṃ 
    rājihi  machasaṃ    obhāsante  machasaṃ    mahitalaṃ  machasaṃ 
    piṭṭhiyeva  machasaṃ 
  
               
       tāvatiṃse ca yāme ca tusite cāpi nimamite  
 paranimamitābhiratino  maṇimhi passa nimitaṃ  
  
       passettha pokkharaṇīyo vippasannodikā  suci  
 mandālakehi saṃchantā padumuppalakehi ca  
  
       dasettha rājiyo setā dasa  nīlā manoramā  
 cha piṅgalā paṇṇarasā haḷiddā ca catuddasā  
  
       visatiṃ tattha sovaṇṇā visatiṃ rajatāmayā  
 indagopakavaṇṇābhā tāva dissanti tiṃsati  
  
       dasettha kāḷiyo cha ca mañjeṭṭhā  paṇṇavisati  
 missā bandhukapupphehi nīluppalavicittitā  
  
       evaṃ sabbaṅgasampannaṃ accimantaṃ pabhassaraṃ  
 odhisuṅkaṃ mahārāja passa tvaṃ dipaduttama  
 maṇikaṇḍo  
  
              
       upāgataṃ rāja upehi lakkhaṃ 
 netādisaṃ maṇiratanaṃ tavatthi  
 dhammena jiyyāma asāhasena 
 jito ca no khippamavākarohi  
  
       pañcāla paccuggata surasena 
 macchā ca maddā  sahakekakehi  
 passantu no te asaṭhena  yuddhaṃ 
 na no sabhāyaṃ na kāroti kiñci  
  
              
       te pāvisuṃ akkhamadena mattā 
 rājā kurūnaṃ puṇṇako cāpi yakkho  
 rājā kaliṃ vicinaṃ aggahesi 
 kaṭamaggahī puṇṇako nāma yakkho  
  
    paranimmitavattino  machasaṃ  syā    vippasannodakā  machasaṃ  syā 
    dassanīyā  machasaṃ  syā    mañajaṭṭha  machasaṃ 
    vicittataṃ  machasaṃ    majjhā  machasaṃ    assatthena  machasaṃ 
  
               
       te tattha jute ubhatyā samāgate
