       uggā ca rājaputtā ca vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇā  
 hatthāruhā anikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārakā 
 kevalo cāpi nigamo sivayo cāpi samāgatā  
  
       asmā ratyā vivasane suriyassugganampati  
 samaggā sivayo hutvā raṭṭhā pabbājayanti taṃ  
  
    sabbe  machasaṃ    tasmiṃ  machasaṃ  syā    suriyuggamate sati  machasaṃ 
  
               
       sa kantā taramānova sivirājena pesito  
 āmuttahatthābharaṇo suvattho candanabhusito  
  
       sīsaṃ nahāto udakeso āmuttamaṇikuṇḍalo  
 upāgami puraṃ rammaṃ vessantaranivesanaṃ  
  
       tatthadassa kumāraṃ so ramamānaṃ sake  pure  
 parikiṇṇaṃ amaccehi tidasānaṃva vāsavaṃ  
  
       so tattha gantvā ramamānaṃ  kattā vessantaraṃ bravi  
 dukkhaṃ te vedayissāmi mā me kujjhi rathesabha  
  
       vanditvā rodamāno so kattā rājānamabravi 
 bhattā mesi mahārāja sabbakārasāharo 
 dukkhaṃ te vedayissāmi tattha assāsayantu maṃ  
  
       sivayo deva te kuddhā negamā va samāgatā  
 uggā ca rājaputtā ca vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇā  
  
       hatthāruhā anikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārakā  
 kevalo cāpi nigamo sivayo cāpi samāgatā  
  
       asmā ratyā vivasane suriyassuggamanampati    
 samaggā sivayo hutvā raṭṭhā pabbājayanti taṃ  
  
       kismiṃ me sivayo kuddhā nāhaṃ passāmi dukkhataṃ    
 tamme katte viyācikkha kasmā pabbājayanti maṃ  
  
              
       uggā ca rājaputtā ca vesiyānā ca brāhmaṇā  
 hatthāruhā anikaṭṭhā rathikā pattikārakā 
 nāgadānena khiyanti tasmā pabbājayanti taṃ  
  
       hadayaṃ cakkhumpahaṃ dajjaṃ kiṃ me bāhirakaṃ dhanaṃ  
 hiraññaṃ vā suvaṇṇaṃ vā muttā veḷuriyā maṇi  
  
       dakkhiṇaṃ vāpahaṃ bāhuṃ disvā yācakamāgate  
 dadeyyaṃ navikampeyyaṃ dane me ramati mano  
  
    sakaṃ  machasaṃ    ramāno  machasaṃ    suriyuggane sati  machasaṃ 
    yo na passāmi dukkaṭaṃ  machasaṃ  syā 
  
               
       kāmaṃ maṃ sivayo sabbe pabbājentu hanantu vā  
 neva dānā viramissaṃ kāmaṃ chindantu sattadhā  
  
       evaṃ taṃ sivayo āhu negamā ca samāgatā  
 kontimārāya tirena giraṃ ārañajaraṃ pati 
 yena pabbajitā yanti tena gacchatu subbato  
  
              
       sohaṃ tena gamissāmi yena gacchanti dusakā  
 rattindivaṃ me khamatha yāva dānaṃ dadāmahaṃ  
  
       āmantayittha rājā naṃ maddiṃ sabbaṅgasobhanaṃ  
 yaṃ te kiñci mayā dinanaṃ dhanaṃ dhaññaca vijjati  
  
       hiraññaṃ vā suvaṇṇaṃ vā muttā veḷuriyā bahu  
 sabbaṃ taṃ nidaheyyāsi yañca te petatikaṃ dhanaṃ  
  
       tamabuvi rājaputti maddi sabbaṅgasohanā  
 kuhiṃ deva nidaheyyāmi  tamme akkhāhi pucchito  
       silavantesu dajjāsi  dānaṃ maddi yathārahaṃ  
 na hi dānā paraṃ atthi patiṭṭhā sabbapāṇinaṃ  
  
              
       puttesu maddi dayyāsi  sassuyā  sasuramhi ca  
 yo ca taṃ bhattā maññeyya sakkaccaṃ taṃ apaṭṭhahe  
  
       no ve taṃ hattā maññeyya mayā vippavasena te  
 aññaṃ bhattāraṃ pariyesa mā kisittha mayā vinā  
  
       ahaṃ hi vanaṃ gacchāmi ghoraṃ vāḷamigāyutaṃ  
 saṃsayo jīvitaṃ mayhaṃ ekakassa  brahāmane  
  
       tamabravi rājaputti maddi sabbaṅgasobhanā  
 abhumme kathaṃ nu bhaṇasi pāpakaṃ vata bhāsasi  
  
       nesa dhammo mahārāja yaṃ tvaṃ gaccheyya ekako  
 ahampi tena gacchāmi yena gacchasi khattiya  
  
       maraṇaṃ vā tayā saddhiṃ jīvitaṃ vā tayā vinā  
 tadeva maraṇaṃ seyyo yañce jive tayā vinā  
  
    nidahāmi  machasaṃ  syā    dajjesi  machasaṃ  syā    dayesi  machasaṃ  syā vi    sasasurā  machasaṃ vi    ekikassa  machasaṃ 
  
               
       aggiṃ nijjālayitvāna ekajālasamāhitaṃ  
 tattha me maraṇaṃ seyyo yañce jive tayā vinā  
  
              
       yathā āraññakaṃ nāgaṃ dantiṃ anveti hatthinī  
 jessantaṃ giriduggesu samesu visamesu ca  
  
       evaṃ taṃ anugacchāmi putte ādāya pacchato  
 subharā te bhavissāmi na te hessāmi dubbharā  
  
       ime kumāre pasusanto mañjuke piyabhāṇino    
 āsine  vanagumbasmiṃ na rajjassa sarissasi

       evaṃ ce me vilapantiyā rājaputtaṃ adūsakaṃ  
 pabbājasi vanaṃ raṭṭhā maññe bhessāmi jīvitaṃ  
  
              
       tassā lālappitaṃ sutvā sabbā antepure bahu    
 bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ sivikaññā samāgatā

 senti puttā ca dārā ca vessantaranivesane

 bāhā paggayha vessantaranivesane

 atha vessantaro rājā dānaṃ dātuṃ upāgami

 bhojanaṃ bhojanatthinaṃ sammā detha  pacecchatha

 tappetha annapānena gacchantu paṭipujitā

 nikkhamanne mahārāje sivinaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhate

       ye vuddhā ye ca daharā ye ca majjhimaporisā  
 bāhā paggayha pakkanduṃ 
 nikkhamante mahārāje sivinaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane

 bahā paggayha pakkanduṃ 
 nikkhamante mahārāje sivinaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane

 sivinaṃ vacanatthena sambhā raṭṭhā nirajjati

 suvaṇṇakacche mātaṅge hemakappanavāsase  
  
       arūḷhe gāmaṇiyehi tomaraṅkusapāṇihi  
 esa vessantaro rājā sambhā raṭṭhā nirajjati  
  
       satta assasate datvā sabbālaṅkārabhusite  
 ājāniye ca jātiyā sindhave sīghavāhane  
  
       arūḷhe gāmaṇiyehi illiyācāpadhārihi  
 esa vessantaro rājā sambhā raṭṭhā nirajjati

 dīpe athopi veyyaghge   sabbālaṅkārabhusite

 esa vessantaro rājā sambhā raṭṭhā nirajjati

 sannaddhā nikkharajjuhi suvaṇṇena alaṅkatā

 āḷārapakhumā  hasulā susaññā tanumajjhimā 
 esa vessantaro rājā sambhā raṭṭhā nirajjati  
  
    āḷārapambhā  machasaṃ 
        veyyaghge  should likely  veyyagghe 
               
       santa dhenusate datvā sabbā kaṃsupadhāraṇā    
 esa vessantaro rājā sambhā raṭṭhā nirajjati  
  
       sattadāsisate datvā sattadāsasatāni ca 
 esa vessantaro rājā sambhā raṭṭhā nirajjati

 esa vessantaro rājā sambhā raṭṭhā nirajjati  
  
       tadāsiṃ yaṃ bhiṃsanakaṃ tadāsi lomahaṃsanā  
 mahādāne padinnamhi medini samakampatha  
  
       tadāsiṃ yaṃ bhiṃsanakaṃ tadāsi lomahaṃsanā  
 yaṃ pañajalikato rājā sambhā raṭṭhā nirajjati

 dānena taṃ niharanti puna dānaṃ adā tuvaṃ  
  
       tesu mantā kilantā ca sampatanti vaṇibbakā  
 nikkhamante mahārāje sivinaṃ raṭṭhavaḍḍhane  
  
              
       āmantayittha rājānaṃ sañajayaṃ dhamminaṃ varaṃ  
 avaruddhasi maṃ deva vaṅkaṃ  gacchāmi pabbataṃ

 atintā yeva kāmehi gacchanti yamasādhanaṃ

 khaggadipinisevite ahaṃ puññāni karomi 
 tumbhe paṅkamhi sīdatha

 sohaṃ sake abhisasiṃ yajamāno sake pure  
  
 sivinaṃ vacanatthana sambhā raṭṭhā nirajjahaṃ

 khaggadipinisevite ahaṃ puññāni karomi

    kusumadhārino  machasaṃ    vaṅka gacchāmi pabbataṃ  machasaṃ  syā

 ayañca maddi kalyāṇi susaññā tanumajjhimā 
 acchataṃ saha puttehi kiṃ araññe karissati

 iṅgha maddī nisāmehi mane ye honti dussabhā

 tepi taṃ tattha hiṃseyyuṃ taṃ te dukkhataraṃ siyā

 sappā ajagarā nāma avisā te mahabbalā

 parikkhipitvā bhogehi vasamānenanti antano

 na tehi puriso diṭṭho rukkhamāruyha muccati

 mahisā vicarantettha nadiṃ sotumbaraṃ pati

 akhettaññāya te maddi bhavitante  mahabbhayaṃ  
  
    sañcavaratha  machasaṃ    bhavissate  machisaṃ bhavissante  syā 
  
               
       yā tvaṃ sivāya sutvāna muhuṃ uttasase pure  
 sā tvaṃ vaṅkaṃ anuppantā kathaṃ maddi karissasi

 sanateva brahāraññaṃ tattha kiṃ gantumicchasi

 yāni etāni akkhāsi vane paṭibhayāni me 
 sabbāni abhisambhossaṃ gacchaññeva rathesabha  
  
              
       kāsaṃ kusaṃ poṭakilaṃ usīraṃ muñajabbabajaṃ  
 urasā panudahessāmi nāssa hessāmi dunnayā

 udarassuparodhena gohanubbeṭhanena ca

 vedhammaṃ  kaṭukaṃ loke gacchaññeva rathesabha

 yo naṃ hatthe gahetvāna akāmaṃ parikaḍḍhati 
 vedhammaṃ kaṭukaṃ loke gacchaññeva rathesabha

    sannisicesu  machasaṃ    vedhabyaṃ  machasaṃ    vābhivākyaṃ na labhetha  machasaṃ 
    sakhinihi ca  machasaṃ 
  
               
       dhajo rathassa paññāṇaṃ dhumo paññāṇamaggino

 taṃ ve devā pasaṃsanti dukkaraṃ hi karoti sā

 pathavyāpi abhejjantyā  nicche vessantaraṃ vinā 
 vedhammaṃ kaṭukaṃ loke gacchaññeva rathesabha  
  
       api sāgarapariyantaṃ pahuvittadharaṃ mahiṃ  
 nānāratanaparipuraṃ nicche vessantaraṃ vinā
